### [1] [Linear Hamiltonians in generators of the real Jacobi group on the extended Siegel-Jacobi space and equations of motion attached](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19001)
*Elena Mirela Babalic,Stefan Berceanu*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文基于扩展的 Siegel-Jacobi 上半空间上的能量函数，推导了与实 Jacobi 群生成元相关的线性哈密顿量在特定变量下的运动方程，并单独讨论了 n=1 的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在扩展的 Siegel-Jacobi 上半空间（extended Siegel-Jacobi upper half space）$\tilde{\mathcal{X}}^J_n$ 上，通过能量函数研究线性哈密顿量（linear Hamiltonians）对应的运动方程，旨在建立该几何框架下的动力学描述。

Method: 借助定义在 $\tilde{\mathcal{X}}^J_n$ 上的能量函数（energy function），针对实 Jacobi 群（real Jacobi group）$G^J_n(\mathbb{R})$ 生成元构成的线性哈密顿量，推导其在变量 $(x,y,q,p,κ)$ 下的运动方程（equations of motion），其中 $x,y$ 为 $\mathcal{M}(n,\mathbb{R})$ 中的对称矩阵，$p,q$ 为实 $n$ 维向量。

Result: 给出了扩展 Siegel-Jacobi 上半空间 $\tilde{\mathcal{X}}^J_n$ 上线性哈密顿量对应的运动方程，并单独呈现了 $n=1$ 情形下的具体结果。

Conclusion: 论文完成了对一般 $n$ 阶以及 $n=1$ 特例下该动力学系统的数学表述，为后续在 Siegel-Jacobi 几何中的应用提供了基础。

Abstract: Using the energy function on the extended Siegel-Jacobi upper half space of order $n$, $\tilde{\mathcal{X}}^J_n$, with $n\in \mathbb{N}$, the equations of motion in the variables $(x,y,q,p,κ)$ attached to linear Hamiltonians in the generators of the real Jacobi group $G^J_n(\mathbb{R})$ are presented, where $x,y$ are symmetric matrices in $\mathcal{M}(n,\mathbb{R})$ and $p,q$ are real $n$-vectors. The case $n=1$ is presented separately.

</details>


<div id='math.DS'></div>

# math.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Time and Frequency domain analysis of Love waves generated by Gaussian, Ricker and double couple seismic sources in a memory dependent fractured poroviscoelastic layer on a heterogeneous viscoelastic half-space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18359)
*Anisha Kumari,Subhajyoti Sarkar,Santimoy Kundu*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文建立了分层裂缝性多孔粘弹性连续介质（stratified fractured poroviscoelastic continuum）中Love波（Love waves）时频域传播特性的理论数学框架，引入分数阶本构关系（fractional order constitutive relations）描述记忆依赖性力学行为，采用三种分布式震源模型（Gaussian、Ricker、双力偶），通过傅里叶变换（Fourier transform）与格林函数法（Green's function methodology）推导复杂色散关系，并利用混合Newton-Raphson迭代算法求解复根，最后通过合成地震图（synthetic seismograms）和单自由度振子（SDOF oscillator）模型验证结构响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常采用理想化点源模型，而分布式震源在裂缝性多孔粘弹性分层框架下的数学表述尚未建立，亟需发展更符合实际的震源模型与波传播理论。

Method: 上层为裂缝性多孔粘弹性材料，下半无限区域为非均匀介质，从交界面处的粘弹性（viscoelastic）行为逐渐过渡到深层纯弹性（elastic）响应；采用Riemann-Liouville分数阶导数刻画记忆依赖性力学行为；考虑Gaussian、Ricker和双力偶三种分布式震源模型；结合傅里叶变换与格林函数法推导色散关系；采用混合Newton-Raphson迭代算法求解色散方程的复根；借助单自由度（SDOF）振子模型评估结构表面响应。

Result: 生成合成地震图验证了解的物理一致性与有效性；数值模拟揭示了非均匀性（heterogeneity）、分数阶粘弹性（fractional viscoelasticity）和孔隙度（porosity）对波传播特性的影响，识别出对系统响应影响最显著的参数。

Conclusion: 所提出的分布式震源模型框架优于传统点源近似，能更真实地反映Love波在裂缝性多孔粘弹性介质中的传播行为；非均匀性、分数阶粘弹性和孔隙度是调控波传播特性的关键因素。

Abstract: The present study develops a detailed theoretical and mathematical formulation to analyze the time and frequency domain propagation characteristics of Love waves in a stratified fractured poroviscoelastic continuum.The top stratum is modeled as a fractured poroviscoelastic material,whereas the lower semi infinite region exhibits heterogeneity and a gradual transition from viscoelastic behavior near the interface to purely elastic response at greater depths.Fractional order constitutive relations are incorporated to capture the memory-dependent mechanical behavior of the medium using Riemann Liouville fractional derivatives. Three distributed source models, namely Gaussian, Ricker and double-couple sources, are considered. To the best of our knowledge, the mathematical formulation of these distributed sources within the present framework has not been established in earlier studies, where the excitation is typically modeled using an idealized point source. By applying Fourier transform techniques in conjunction with Greens function methodology, the complex dispersion relation is obtained. Since the resulting dispersion equation yields complex roots, a hybrid Newton Raphson iterative algorithm is employedto compute these roots efficiently. Synthetic seismograms are generated to verify that the obtained solutions remain physically consistent and meaningful. Numerical simulations are then performed to investigate the effects of heterogeneity, fractional viscoelasticity and porosity on wave propagation characteristics, thereby identifying the parameters that exert the most significant influence on the system response. Furthermore, to examine the structural implications of the propagated waves, a single degree of freedom SDOF oscillator model is employed to evaluate the surface response corresponding to different types of seismic sources.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Robust and Interpretable Adaptation of Equivariant Materials Foundation Models via Sparsity-promoting Fine-tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18691)
*Youngwoo Cho,Seunghoon Yi,Wooil Yang,Sungmo Kang,Young-woo Son,Jaegul Choo,Joonseok Lee,Soo Kyung Kim,Hongkee Yoon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于稀疏性促进（sparsity-promoting）的微调方法，利用E(3)-等变材料基础模型的结构特性，仅更新约3%甚至0.5%的参数即可在能量与力预测任务上达到或超过全参数微调与等变低秩适配方法，并在磁矩预测等任务上展示了可推广性，同时稀疏模式具有物理可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练的材料基础模型（pre-trained materials foundation model）或机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potential）虽能利用通用物理化学知识近似势能面，但由于物理化学多样性以及实际计算设置与预训练数据构建条件之间的不匹配，通常需要领域特定的校准（domain-specific calibration）。

Method: 提出一种稀疏性促进微调方法，通过利用E(3)-等变材料基础模型（E(3)-equivariant materials foundation model）的结构特性，选择性地更新模型参数，而非对所有参数进行全量微调。

Result: 在分子与晶体基准（benchmark）的能量和力预测任务上，该方法仅更新约3%（部分情况下低至约0.5%）的参数，即在性能上匹配或超越了全参数微调（full fine-tuning）与等变低秩适配（equivariant low-rank adaptation）。此外，该方法在磁矩预测与磁敏总能量建模任务上也展现了良好的任务泛化性。稀疏模式分析揭示了物理上可解释的特征，例如过渡金属体系中d轨道贡献的增强。

Conclusion: 稀疏性促进微调是一种灵活且可解释的方法，能够有效实现等变材料基础模型的领域特化（domain specialization）。

Abstract: Pre-trained materials foundation models, or machine learning interatomic potentials, leverage general physicochemical knowledge to effectively approximate potential energy surfaces. However, they often require domain-specific calibration due to physicochemical diversity as well as mismatches between practical computational settings and those used in constructing the pre-training data. To address this, we propose a sparsity-promoting fine-tuning method that selectively updates model parameters by exploiting the structural properties of E(3)-equivariant materials foundation models. On energy and force prediction tasks across molecular and crystalline benchmarks, our method matches or surpasses full fine-tuning and equivariant low-rank adaptation while updating only $\sim$3~\% of parameters, and in some cases as little as $\sim$0.5~\%. Beyond energy and force calibration, we further demonstrate task generalizability by applying our method to magnetic moment prediction and magnetism-aware total energy modeling. Finally, analysis of sparsity patterns reveals physically interpretable signatures, such as enhanced $d$-orbital contributions in transition metal systems. Overall, our results establish sparsity-promoting fine-tuning as a flexible and interpretable method for domain specialization of equivariant materials foundation models.

</details>


### [4] [Attention as Frustrated Synchronization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18694)
*Joshua Nunley*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出挫折同步网络（Frustrated Synchronization Network, FSN），将语言模型中的注意力机制建模为同步动力学（synchronization dynamics），通过引入核函数中的挫折项（frustration）实现结构化偏差，从而在百万参数和字符级语言建模任务上超越RoPE-SwiGLU Transformer。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完美同步的振荡器网络无法进行计算，因此基于同步机制的注意力架构必须在结构的非一致性中定位计算能力，这促使作者设计一种利用挫折同步（frustrated synchronization）的替代注意力机制。

Method: FSN将令牌状态表示为环面（torus）上的相位，整个值通路（value pathway）仅由一个可学习的复数耦合核（complex coupling kernel）及一步延迟（one-step delay）构成。核的每个分量对应同步文献中的挫折：复数相位为静态Kuramoto-Sakaguchi挫折角，有符号谐波为排斥性Daido分量，延迟项在代数上等价于挫折角为数据自身转移的Kuramoto-Sakaguchi耦合，从而将下一个令牌预测实现为由数据挫折化的同步过程。

Result: 在字符级文本和代码任务上，百万参数尺度的FSN在每一测量轮次中的验证损失均低于调优后的RoPE-SwiGLU Transformer。FSN每30轮训练的结果均低于Transformer收敛的50轮损失（1.611），FSN完成50轮后收敛至1.5953±0.0014。将前馈模块替换为平均场耦合（mean-field coupling）至学习集体模式（learned collective modes）的变体也与Transformer表现相当。在自然文本上，无挫折基础层在所有复制深度上落后于收敛的Transformer，而挫折核在深度4及以上反转了这一差距。优势在四百万参数尺度上持续保持。

Conclusion: 挫折同步网络证明了将同步动力学中的挫折概念引入注意力机制的有效性，在同等规模下优于标准Transformer，说明语言建模中的下一个令牌预测可以被理解为由数据自身转移驱动的挫折同步过程。

Abstract: A network of oscillators that synchronizes perfectly computes nothing further, so an attention architecture built from synchronization must locate its computation in structured departures from agreement. We introduce the Frustrated Synchronization Network (FSN), whose token states are phases on a torus and whose entire value pathway is one learned complex coupling kernel over harmonics and a one-step delay. Each component of the kernel is a frustration in the sense of the synchronization literature. The complex phases are static Kuramoto-Sakaguchi frustration angles, the signed harmonics are repulsive Daido components, and the delay term, which couples each token to the successors of the tokens it attends to, is algebraically identical to Kuramoto-Sakaguchi coupling whose frustration angle is the data's own transition, so next-token prediction is implemented as synchronization frustrated by the data. At matched one-million-parameter and training budgets on character-level text and code, the FSN's validation loss is below a tuned RoPE-SwiGLU transformer's at every epoch measured, and the comparison survives training the baseline to convergence: every thirty-epoch enwik8 seed finishes below the transformer's converged fifty-epoch loss of 1.611, and the FSN's completed fifty-epoch runs converge to 1.5953 +/- 0.0014. A variant with every feed-forward block replaced by mean-field coupling to learned collective modes, leaving no multilayer perceptron in the stack, tracks the transformer. On natural text the unfrustrated base layer falls behind the converged transformer at every copy depth, worst on long-range copy events; the kernel reverses the deficit at every depth of four and beyond. Headline comparisons are at the one-million-parameter scale; a scale ladder is complete through four million parameters with the advantage persisting, and remaining arms are marked as in progress.

</details>

# physics.comp-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Electromagnetic Characterization of Magnetic Ring: Case of Circular Cross-Section Shape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18270)
*Taha El Hajji,Lars Sjöberg*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在正弦激励下、具有圆形截面的环形磁环的二维解析模型，基于麦克斯韦方程（Maxwell's equations）和复磁导率（complex permeability）推导出内部磁场、磁通、复阻抗（complex impedance）及总损耗的解析表达式，严格分离了涡流损耗（eddy current losses）、磁滞损耗（hysteresis losses）和绕组损耗（winding losses），并通过贝塞尔函数（Bessel functions）显式纳入集肤效应（skin effect），为标准化磁性材料表征提供了高效准确的计算工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有磁性材料表征依赖二维或三维有限元分析（finite element analysis），计算成本较高，缺乏简洁高效的解析模型支持标准化测量，如布罗克豪斯（Brockhaus）和岩通（Iwatsu）环形测量法。

Method: 在局部极坐标下应用麦克斯韦方程组与复磁导率，推导出环内磁场、磁通、复阻抗和总损耗的解析表达式；利用贝塞尔函数显式建模导电芯体中的集肤效应，并严格区分涡流损耗、磁滞损耗与绕组损耗；进一步引入表观磁导率（apparent permeability），将非线性磁芯行为映射至简化线性材料模型。

Result: 得到了内部磁场、磁通、复阻抗和总损耗的解析表达式；导出了表观磁导率的表达式，实现非线性行为向线性模型的映射。

Conclusion: 该解析模型计算高效且准确，可作为标准化磁性材料表征（如Brockhaus和Iwatsu环形测量）的强有力工具，替代2D和3D有限元分析。

Abstract: This paper introduces a comprehensive two-dimensional analytical model of a toroidal magnetic ring with circular cross-section under sinusoidal excitation. Applying Maxwell's equations in local polar coordinates within a complex permeability, the model derives analytical expressions for the internal magnetic field, magnetic flux, complex impedance, and total losses. It rigorously separates the contributions of eddy current losses, hysteresis losses, and winding losses, while explicitly incorporating the skin effect in the conductive core via Bessel functions. An expression for the apparent permeability is also provided, enabling the nonlinear core behavior to be mapped onto simplified linear material models. The resulting analytical model offers a computationally efficient and accurate foundation for standardized magnetic material characterization, such as Brockhaus and Iwatsu ring measurements, as a powerful alternative to 2D and 3D finite element analysis.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Exact propagating Dirac wave packets in an attractive Coulomb-like potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18470)
*Siddhant Das*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在轴对称势 $V=-v_0/\rho$ 中构造了狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）的精确、正能量、可归一化波包解——据我们所知，这是首次在任何外势中构造出这类解。其中一个波包族仅由初等函数构成，其纵向轮廓在非相对论极限下复现自由薛定谔方程（free Schrödinger equation）的厄米-高斯（Hermite-Gauss）波包。所有波包具有两个显著特征：(i) 概率密度与自旋取向点态解耦——尽管狄拉克方程固有自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）；(ii) 在临界耦合 $v_0\to\hbar c/2$ 处时间演化完全冻结。文章还提出一个简单方案，将二维亥姆霍兹方程（2D Helmholtz equation）的解映射为更多精确狄拉克波包。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克方程在外势中的精确波包解长期缺失，而这类解对于理解相对论性量子力学中的波包动力学、自旋-轨道耦合效应以及临界耦合行为具有基础性意义。

Method: 作者在轴对称势 $V=-v_0/\rho$ 中构造了狄拉克方程的正能量、可归一化波包解。同时提出一个映射方案，将二维亥姆霍兹方程的解转化为狄拉克波包解。

Result: 得到了精确波包解，其中一个族仅由初等函数组成，在非相对论极限下纵向轮廓退化为自由薛定谔方程的厄米-高斯波包。所有波包的概率密度与自旋取向点态解耦，且在临界耦合 $v_0\to\hbar c/2$ 处时间演化完全冻结。

Conclusion: 本文首次构建了狄拉克方程在外势中的精确、正能量、可归一化波包解，揭示了波包动力学中自旋解耦与临界冻结等新颖现象，并提供了通过亥姆霍兹方程生成更多精确解的通用映射方法。

Abstract: We construct exact, positive-energy, normalizable wave-packet solutions of the Dirac equation in the axisymmetric potential $V=-\,v_0/ρ$ -- to our knowledge, the first such solutions in any external potential. Remarkably, one family comprises only elementary functions whose longitudinal profiles reproduce the free-Schrödinger Hermite--Gauss wave packets in the nonrelativistic limit. All packets share two striking features: (i) a probability density that is pointwise decoupled from spin orientation -- despite the inherent spin-orbit coupling of the Dirac equation -- and (ii) a complete freezing of their time evolution at the critical coupling $v_0\to\hbar c/2$. We also present a simple scheme that maps solutions of the 2D Helmholtz equation to further exact Dirac wave packets.

</details>


### [7] [Adiabatically-induced Kawaguchi geometry and jerk in quantum-classical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16037)
*Athanasios Chatzistavrakidis,Larisa Jonke,Ryan Requist*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过近恒等幺正变换（near-identity unitary transformations）对量子态进行序列化操作，推导了混合量子-经典系统中经典变量的有效作用量层级。研究表明三阶欧拉-拉格朗日方程是非牛顿的，力依赖于加加速度（jerk），并诱导出经典变量空间上的一种特殊 Kawaguchi 几何，其特征为几乎辛结构（almost symplectic structure）和依赖于速度与加速度的微分线元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在混合量子-经典系统中，绝热地消除量子自由度会在经典运动方程中产生有效力。为了更精确地捕捉高阶非绝热效应（nonadiabatic effects），需要系统性地推导更高阶的有效作用量，以改进分子动力学模拟的效率。

Method: 对量子态施加一系列近恒等幺正变换，按绝热参数（adiabatic parameter）的阶次系统地消除量子自由度，从而推导出经典变量的有效作用量层级。该方法可生成任意阶的有效力，并最终得到三阶欧拉-拉格朗日方程。

Result: 三阶有效力依赖于加加速度（jerk），即位置的三阶时间导数。该三阶项在经典变量空间上诱导出一种特殊的 Kawaguchi 几何，这是一种由几乎辛结构和依赖于速度与加速度的微分线元所表征的几何结构。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的方法可有效捕捉分子动力学模拟中的高阶非绝热效应，为混合量子-经典系统的精确数值计算提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Adiabatically eliminating the quantum degrees of freedom in a mixed quantum-classical system produces an effective force in the classical equation of motion. The elimination can be made to any order in the adiabatic parameter, generating a series of higher order forces. By applying a sequence of near-identity unitary transformations to the quantum state, we derive a hierarchy of increasingly accurate effective actions for the classical variables. The third order Euler-Lagrange equation is non-Newtonian as the force depends on the jerk, the third order time derivative of position. We find that the third order terms induce a special kind of Kawaguchi geometry on the space of classical variables. This geometry is characterized by an almost symplectic structure and a differential line element that depends on the acceleration in addition to the velocity. Our results can be used to efficiently capture higher order nonadiabatic effects in molecular dynamics simulations.

</details>


### [8] [Ground state preparation of random all-to-all Hamiltonians using ADAPT-VQE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18339)

Abstract: The ground state of random Hamiltonians with all-to-all interactions such as the quantum Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK) model and the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model follow volume-law entanglement and are expected to be hard to model using tensor networks. In recent years, some progress has been made to push the limit of classical methods using neural quantum states. However, it remains an open question whether there exist quantum algorithms that could offer a quantum advantage over the state-of-the-art classical methods in simulating random Hamiltonians. Method: 论文引入“局部无手征性”（local achirality）这一拓扑条件，证明当流形M满足该条件时，可从基态纠缠中提取其拓扑配分函数（topological partition function）Z(M)。进一步，通过分析四维流形的庞特里亚金数（Pontryagin number）与T-SPT序的关联，构建了一种可探测非平庸T-SPT的纠缠度量。

Result: 证明了局部无手征流形可用于提取2+1维拓扑相中超越S矩阵和T矩阵的普适性质；在四维中，这类流形具有零庞特里亚金数（Pontryagin number）；将此性质与四维中超越上同调的时间反演对称保护拓扑序（T-SPT）的存在性联系起来，并构造了能探测该T-SPT的纠缠度量。

Conclusion: 体纠缠度量可提取超越传统S、T矩阵的拓扑序信息，局部无手征性为系统地提取拓扑配分函数提供了新的判定条件，并有望推广到更高维度和更复杂拓扑相的探测。

Abstract: We consider the problem of identifying a topological order based on bulk entanglement of the ground-state wavefunction. It remains an open question to what extent such entanglement measures can be used to extract any universal information from the ground state. Here we show that the topological partition function $Z(M)$ of a manifold $M$ can be extracted provided that $M$ satisfies a topological condition which we term ``local achirality". We show that locally-achiral manifolds can be used to extract universal properties of 2+1d topological phases that go beyond the $S$ and $T$ matrices. As a first step towards classifying locally-achiral manifolds, we show that, in four dimensions, such manifolds have vanishing Pontryagin number. We relate this property to the existence of beyond-cohomology time-reversal symmetry protected topological order (T-SPT) in four dimensions. Abstract: The open quantum Rabi model describes a two-level system coupled to a harmonic oscillator. A Gaussian phase transition for the nonequilibrium steady states has been predicted when the bosonic mode is soft and subject to damping. We show that oscillator dephasing is a relevant perturbation, which leads to a non-Gaussian phase transition and an intriguing cascade of instabilities for $k$-th order bosonic operators, as well as a jump in the steady-state qubit polarization. For the soft-mode limit, the equations of motion form a closed hierarchy and spectral properties can be efficiently studied. In this work, we provide a comprehensive study of two central quantities that characterize the protocol, the post-selection probability and the fidelity, taking into account possible errors in time-reversed dynamics. Method: 采用量子光学中的典范模型——耗散Dicke模型（dissipative Dicke model），其中一个大自旋（large spin）与一个耗散谐振模（dissipative harmonic mode）相互作用。通过在大但有限的自旋尺寸下工作在半经典（semiclassical）区域，来调节经典/量子对应。

Abstract: The effect of a large environment on a finite-size quantum mechanical system is two-fold: It brings dissipation, but also fluctuations of thermal and quantum origin. While dissipation tends to stabilize the dynamics, we question if and how environmental quantum fluctuations can generate chaos in an otherwise classically non-chaotic system. We work out a paradigmatic model of quantum optics: the dissipative Dicke model, where a large spin interacts with a dissipative harmonic mode. We dial in the classical/quantum correspondence by working in the semiclassical regime at large but finite spin. We demonstrate that, starting from a classically regular phase space in the superradiant regime, quantum noise can generate a strange attractor with fractal dimension and a positive Lyapunov exponent. Method: 以耗散KPO为代表性模型，分析弱耗散区域稳态密度矩阵特征值的配对结构；通过系统经典极限分析，推导控制稳态光谱亲吻出现与消失的临界线的解析表达式。

Conclusion: 研究表明，闭系统中的光谱亲吻现象在耗散系统中具有明确的稳态对应物，其行为由耗散驱动的相变所调控，为理解开放量子系统中的激发态量子相变提供了新视角。

Abstract: Spectral kissing, recently realized in a Kerr parametric oscillator (KPO), refers to the merging of pairs of energy levels and arises as a manifestation of an excited-state quantum phase transition (ESQPT). Here, we show that this phenomenon has a dissipative counterpart encoded in the spectrum of the steady-state density matrix. Using a dissipative KPO as a representative example, we demonstrate that, in the weak-dissipation regime, the eigenvalues of the steady-state density matrix organize into quasi-degenerate pairs that mirror the spectral kissing of the corresponding closed system. As the dissipation strength increases, this pairing gradually disappears. By analyzing the classical limit of the system, we derive analytical expressions for the critical lines governing both the onset of steady-state spectral kissing and its disappearance at a dissipative phase transition.

### [14] [Equilibration of generalized subsystems: a quantum-channel approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18360)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子平衡化（quantum equilibration）结果通常分别处理系统-环境结构和受限测量两种情形，缺乏统一的态级描述框架。

Method: 引入广义子系统概念，将可访问的有效态定义为量子信道（quantum channel）作用于微观态的输出；推导平衡化界限，并分析典型初态及有限分辨率能量信道（finite-resolution energy channel）等示例。

Result: 广义子系统在维度远小于被丢弃微观信息的有效维度时平衡化；该条件在大子空间的典型初态下成立；平衡描述对微观初态细节不敏感；该框架恢复了普通子系统与有限族POVM（positive operator-valued measure）的平衡化界限；有限分辨率能量信道明确了残余有效相干性，并揭示了谱多重性（spectral multiplicities）对相干的约束作用。

Abstract: Quantum systems governed by unitary and reversible microscopic dynamics may nevertheless exhibit equilibration, in the sense that some effective description becomes time-independent. Standard equilibration results usually consider two separate situations: system-environment structures, in which the composite system evolves unitarily while the system of interest equilibrates, and restricted measurements, such as coarse-grained POVMs and observables, in which the measurement statistics equilibrate. Here, we bring these descriptions into a common state-level framework using the concept of generalized subsystems, where the accessible effective state appears as the output of a quantum channel acting on the microscopic state. We derive bounds showing that generalized subsystems equilibrate when their dimension is small compared with the effective dimension of the discarded microscopic information. We further show that this condition is met for typical initial states in large subspaces and that the resulting equilibrium description is largely insensitive to microscopic initial details. The framework recovers the usual equilibration bounds for ordinary subsystems and finite families of POVMs. As an example, we also introduce a finite-resolution energy channel that maps unresolved microscopic energy levels into effective energy levels, thereby making residual effective coherences explicit and showing how spectral multiplicities constrain those coherences while strengthening equilibration. Our results provide a unified state-level formulation of quantum equilibration under general forms of limited accessible information.

### [15] [Probing chaos and thermalization through out-of-time-ordered correlators in random field spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18982)
*C Jisha,Shivam Mishra,Ravi Prakash*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了随机场海森堡自旋-1/2链中乱时序关联器（OTOC）的动力学行为，发现OTOC趋近饱和的方式可区分可积与混沌体系，并揭示了长程谱统计在表征量子混沌中的作用，同时基于本征态热化假说（ETH）推导了OTOC长时间饱和的精确表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用数值模拟方法，在随机场海森堡自旋-1/2链（Heisenberg spin-1/2 chain）中通过参数化调控实现从可积到混沌动力学的交叉，系统分析了OTOC在不同区域中的弛豫行为、长程谱统计（如数方差，number variance）以及随机场实现的影响。

Result: 可积体系中OTOC趋近饱和时呈现幂律弛豫（1/t）；混沌体系中则先经历更高次幂律弛豫（1/t^α, α≥1）后再进入指数弛豫。长程谱统计在OTOC近饱和区对量子混沌的表征更为有效。OTOC的弛豫过程对随机场实现敏感，而初始置乱过程则具有鲁棒性。长时间饱和值因实现而异，其表达式通过本征态热化假说（Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis, ETH）导出。

Conclusion: OTOC的趋近饱和动力学可作为区分可积与混沌体系的有效诊断工具；长程谱统计在近饱和区优于短程统计；OTOC在不同时间尺度表现出不同普适特征，其饱和值可由ETH精确描述。

Abstract: Out-of-time-ordered correlators (OTOCs) have emerged as a diagnostic of information scrambling and quantum chaos in many-body systems. We investigate the imprints of chaos in the dynamics of OTOCs in the Heisenberg spin-$1/2$ chain with random fields. The system is parameterized to exhibit a crossover from integrable to chaotic dynamics. We demonstrate numerically that the approach to saturation of the OTOC can distinguish between integrable and chaotic regimes, with a power-law $(1/t)$ relaxation for integrable systems and a higher-degree power-law decay $(1/t^α; α\ge 1)$ followed by an exponential relaxation for the chaotic regime. We further show that long-range spectral statistics, such as the number variance, are more effective in characterizing quantum chaos in the regime near saturation of OTOC. We also demonstrate that the relaxation and initial scrambling regimes exhibit distinct and universal features, with the former being sensitive and the latter being robust against different realizations of random-fields. The long-time saturation of OTOC also fluctuates with different realizations, and its exact expression is derived through the Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis.

### [16] [Quantum solitons and their quantum walks in transmon arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19339)

Method: 理论上分析了一维电容耦合transmon线性阵列，将其有效描述为具有吸引相互作用的Bose-Hubbard哈密顿量（Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonian with attractive interaction）；通过重新审视最低能带的离散孤子（discrete soliton）性质，识别空间局域化的量子孤子态。

Result: 发现这些量子孤子态的时间演化呈现量子干涉图样（quantum interference pattern）或量子行走（quantum walk），揭示了其复合本性。同时提出了与当前最先进可调transmon电路（tunable-transmon circuits）兼容的量子孤子制备协议。

Conclusion: 超导电路为研究量子孤子物理提供了一个有前景且实验上可访问的平台。

Abstract: Superconducting qubits are artificial atoms whose spectra and interactions can be engineered through appropriate circuit design, a versatility that can be exploited for quantum simulation. We theoretically investigate a linear array of capacitively coupled transmons, effectively described by a Bose-Hubbard Hamiltonian with attractive interaction. We revisit the discrete-soliton nature of the lowest-energy band of the spectrum, and identify spatially localized quantum solitons. The solitonic character of these states is revealed through their time evolution, which displays a quantum interference pattern, or quantum walk, highlighting their composite nature. We discuss protocols for preparing spatially localized quantum solitons that are compatible with current state-of-the-art tunable-transmon circuits. Our results demonstrate that superconducting circuits provide a promising and experimentally accessible platform for the investigation of quantum soliton physics.

</details>

### [17] [Meromorphic amplitudes from 3-dimensional supersymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18331)
*Federico Ambrosino,Nathan Haouzi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文建立了超对称（supersymmetric）理论与散射振幅（scattering amplitudes）之间的新联系：证明Coon振幅等价于XYZ模型在非平凡边界条件下的三维$\mathcal{N}=2$半指标（half-index），并利用三维$\mathcal{N}=2$镜像对称性（mirror symmetry）实现了交叉对称性（crossing symmetry），进而通过椭圆完备化（elliptic completion）对Coon振幅进行了亚纯修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超对称理论与散射振幅之间的深层联系，特别是为Coon振幅提供规范理论（gauge theory）实现，并解决其历史上存在的分支割（branch cut）导致的单位性问题。

Method: 将Coon振幅等价于XYZ模型在非平凡边界条件下的3d $\mathcal{N}=2$半指标；利用3d $\mathcal{N}=2$镜像对称性（XYZ与SQED之间）实现交叉对称性；通过将产生分支割的$\mathfrak{q}^{ST}$因子提升为椭圆完备化（elliptic completion），构造Coon振幅的亚纯修正。

Result: Coon振幅与3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ XYZ模型半指标精确对应；XYZ模型的紫外（UV）定义流（flows）到红外（IR）的sigma模型，其配分函数为Veneziano振幅；通过椭圆完备化修正后的Coon振幅无需牺牲单值性（single-valuedness）即可在物理极点处实现正性（positivity）。

Conclusion: 超对称理论为散射振幅提供了新的实现框架；椭圆完备化方法有效解决了Coon振幅中分支割导致的单值性问题，同时保持了物理极点处的正性要求。

Abstract: We establish a new connection between supersymmetric theories and scattering amplitudes. We show that the Coon amplitude coincides with the 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ half-index of the XYZ model with nontrivial boundary conditions. Our 3d theory, intrinsically defined in the UV, flows to a sigma model in the IR whose partition function is the Veneziano amplitude. Crossing symmetry is realized as a consequence of 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ mirror symmetry between XYZ and SQED. We use this correspondence to construct a meromorphic modification of the Coon amplitude by promoting the long-standing dressing factor $\mathfrak{q}^{ST}$ responsible for a branch cut to an elliptic completion thereof. This illustrates that one does not have to give up single-valuedness to achieve positivity at the physical poles.

### [18] [The pole truth: an analytical graviton propagator from Asymptotic Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18343)
*Benjamin Knorr*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 基于渐近安全（Asymptotic Safety）框架，推导了引力子传播子（graviton propagator）的解析近似，发现在自旋-2（spin-two）扇区不存在额外极点或幺正性（unitarity）/因果性（causality）违反，支持渐近安全不引入新自由度、传播内容与广义相对论（General Relativity）相同的结论。机制在于有限阶导数展开中虚假极点（spurious poles）的留数（residues）随展开阶数增加而趋于零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验渐近安全框架下引力子传播子是否引入额外自由度（degrees of freedom），以及是否会导致幺正性或因果性违反，从而验证该理论能否保持与广义相对论相同的场内容（field content）。

Method: 基于渐近安全方法，推导引力子传播子的解析近似（analytical approximation），通过分析传播子在自旋-2扇区的极点结构（pole structure）及有限阶导数展开中虚假极点的行为来评估其物理一致性。

Result: 在自旋-2扇区未发现额外极点，也未检测到幺正性或因果性违反。有限阶导数展开中的虚假极点的留数随展开阶数增加而趋近于零。

Conclusion: 该结果强化了渐近安全不引入新自由度、传播内容与广义相对论相同的观点，并揭示了其底层机制：虚假极点的留数在高阶展开中被抑制。

Abstract: We derive an analytical approximation for the graviton propagator from Asymptotic Safety. We find neither extra poles nor indications of unitarity or causality violations in the spin-two sector. Our results strengthen the case that Asymptotic Safety does not introduce new degrees of freedom, and thus propagates the same field content as General Relativity. We also identify the underlying mechanism: the residues of spurious poles in finite-order derivative expansions approach zero as the order is increased.

Conclusion: 该方法有效降低了黑p-膜热力学计算的构造依赖性，为一类广义标量-引力耦合系统的热力学研究提供了统一且更简洁的推导途径。

Abstract: This paper generalizes the method used in the previous article 2512.09930 to black $p$-brane thermodynamics in arbitrary dimensions containing black holes and strings as special cases: thermodynamic quantities can be derived without constructing the corresponding black $p$-brane solutions. ### [20] [Exponentiation of higher-point and higher-genus Virasoro conformal blocks in the semiclassical limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18345)
*Marius Gerbershagen,Jakob Hollweck*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了一个长期存在的猜想：在中心荷 $c \to \infty$ 且 $h/c$ 有限的全经典极限下，Virasoro 共形块（conformal block）确实呈指数化行为。该证明从之前已知的四点球面块和一点环面块推广到任意道（channel）下的更高点函数和更高亏格（higher-genus）背景，并建立在一种将振子方法（oscillator method）扩展至三条内线交汇于顶点情形的新构造之上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种振子方法的新扩展，将其应用于三条内线在一个顶点处交汇的情形；该扩展同时为二维共形场论（2d CFT）中一般亏格下的全局共形块（global conformal block）提供了一种新的构造性计算方法。

Result: 成功将 Virasoro 共形块在全经典极限下指数化的证明从已知的四点球面块和一点环面块推广到任意道下的更高点函数和更高亏格背景。

Conclusion: 该指数化陈述在形式幂级数（formal power series）层面上成立，从而确认了该长期猜想在更一般情形下的正确性。

Abstract: A long-standing conjecture claims that Virasoro conformal blocks exponentiate in the semiclassical limit $c \to \infty$ with $h/c$ finite. However, this has been proven only for four-point blocks on the sphere and one-point blocks on the torus. Here we extend the proof to general conformal blocks for higher-point functions and higher-genus backgrounds in arbitrary channels. The statement is to be understood at the level of a formal power series. Our proof builds upon a novel extension of the oscillator method for the computation of conformal blocks to cases where three internal lines meet at a vertex. This extension also gives a new constructive method to compute global conformal blocks in 2d CFTs at general genus.

### [21] [Ghosts versus Unstable Particles in Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18349)
*Luca Buoninfante*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过对比量子场论中的不稳定粒子与多粒子阈值以上的“鬼（ghost）”，阐明了鬼的物理本质：鬼在渐近极限下不衰变，但由于负范数单粒子态被多粒子成分掩盖而无法获得粒子解释；两者在戴森传播子的复极点结构、黎曼面位置以及有限时间效应下的共振行为上均存在根本性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论中，多粒子阈值以上的鬼（ghost）其物理性质尚未被充分阐明，尤其是与不稳定粒子的本质区别。本文旨在通过分析渐近表述、戴森传播子（dressed propagator）的解析结构以及有限时间效应，揭示鬼的物理本质及其不可作为自由传播粒子的原因。

Method: 首先采用渐近表述（asymptotic formulation）分析正范数单粒子态的不稳定衰变与鬼的非衰变行为；其次通过戴森传播子的解析结构区分两类极点——鬼的复共轭极点位于第一黎曼面（first Riemann sheet），而普通不稳定粒子的极点位于第二黎曼面（second Riemann sheet）；最后将量子场论推广至有限时间区间，并在戴森传播子的合理近似下考察有限时间效应对共振行为的影响。

Result: 鬼共振在现象学上比普通共振更窄，正负能量峰之间的干涉更弱；有限时间效应放大了两者共振行为的差异，鬼共振出现更高的峰值。不同时间尺度的动力学行为也被识别：时间小于逆宽度时可用自由粒子近似，之后相互作用和干涉效应主导，导致衰变或多粒子掩盖。戴森传播子的复极点仅在晚期出现，渐近地形成复共轭对，支配渐近动力学。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持鬼在渐近极限下不存在自由传播的粒子态，即鬼无法作为可观测的渐近粒子存在。

Abstract: We elucidate the physical nature of ghosts above the multi-particle threshold by contrasting them with unstable particles in quantum field theory. We first consider the asymptotic formulation, where ordinary positive-norm one-particle states can be unstable and decay, whereas ghosts survive asymptotically without decaying, yet admit no particle interpretation due to interference with the multi-particle component which masks the negative-norm one-particle state. This distinction originates from two different analytic structures of the dressed propagator, whose complex conjugate poles lie in the first or second Riemann sheet in the ghost or ordinary case, respectively. Ghost resonances are, in principle, phenomenologically distinguishable from ordinary ones, being narrower and exhibiting weaker interference between positive- and negative-energy peaks. We then formulate the quantum field theory in a finite interval of time and, working within a suitable approximation for the dressed propagator, find that finite-time effects amplify differences in the resonant behavior and give rise to new features, such as higher peaks in ghost resonances. Distinct temporal regimes are also identified: for times shorter than the inverse width, an approximate free-particle description is valid, whereas at later times interactions and interference effects dominate, leading to decay or multi-particle masking. Complex poles in the dressed propagator emerge only at late times and become complex-conjugate pairs asymptotically, determining the asymptotic dynamics. This study supports the absence of freely propagating ghost particles in the asymptotic limit.

</details>


### [22] [Probing weak chaos in $\mathcal N=4$ super Yang-Mills and long-range spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18351)
*Pawel Caputa,Brian Creed,Rathindra Nath Das,Saskia Demulder,Tristan McLoughlin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过谱统计、本征向量诊断和扩展复杂性（spread complexity）等工具，系统研究了 $\mathcal N=4$ 超杨-米尔斯理论及其 $\beta$ 形变在 $\mathfrak{su}(2)$ 扇区中平面区域伸缩算子的有限圈截断所引发的量子混沌现象，发现二圈和四圈截断在足够大耦合常数下呈现类高斯正交系综（GOE）的能级统计，但具有弱可积破缺特征，而三圈截断在研究的参数范围内未观察到混沌 onset；同时，本征向量诊断表明对应本征态随机性低于 GOE 向量，体现弱遍历性（weak ergodicity）与多重分形性（multifractality），且 Krylov 链上的数据与能级统计存在关联。结果提示有限圈伸缩算子并非一般的长程自旋链哈密顿量，而是呈现与全圈平面理论中可积性恢复相一致的图案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面极限下的 $\mathcal N=4$ 超杨-米尔斯理论及其 $\beta$ 形变在全圈层次预期是可积的，而在有限圈截断下该模型构成近邻 XXX 自旋链的长程形变。本文旨在探究在可积的一圈极限与可积的全圈平面理论这两个可积边界之间，混沌行为如何通过有限圈截断逐步涌现，从而理解可积性破缺与恢复的动力学机制。

Method: 采用谱统计（spectral statistics）、本征向量诊断（eigenvector diagnostics）和扩展复杂性（spread complexity）三种互补方法，对 $\mathfrak{su}(2)$ 扇区中平面伸缩算子在二圈、三圈和四圈截断下的混沌特征进行定量分析，并考察耦合常数变化对能级统计与 Krylov 空间动力学的影响。

Result: 二圈和四圈截断在足够大耦合常数下呈现 GOE 类能级统计，但具有弱可积破缺（weak integrability breaking）特征；四圈截断的可积破缺弱于二圈截断，且出现混沌的临界耦合更大（至少对于长自旋链）。三圈截断在研究的参数范围内未出现混沌 onset。本征向量诊断显示对应本征态随机性低于 GOE 向量，体现弱遍历性与多重分形性。Krylov 链上的能级间距统计与扩展复杂性峰值及无序度存在关联，且初始态在哈密顿量本征基矢中的离域化程度显著影响复杂性的饱和行为。

Conclusion: 有限圈截断下的平面伸缩算子并非一般的（generic）长程自旋链哈密顿量，其混沌行为受特定圈数和耦合常数调控，并呈现与全圈平面理论中可积性恢复相一致的图案。该结果表明，有限圈截断为研究可积性破缺与恢复之间的过渡提供了自然框架。

Abstract: We study signatures of quantum chaos in finite-loop truncations of the planar dilatation operator in the $\mathfrak{su}(2)$ sector of $\mathcal N=4$ super Yang-Mills and its $β$-deformation. These truncations define holographically motivated long-range deformations of the nearest-neighbour XXX spin chain. At one-loop the model is integrable, while the all-loop planar theory is expected to again be integrable. Finite-loop truncations therefore provide a natural setting for investigating how chaotic behaviour emerges between these two integrable limits. We analyse this question using spectral statistics, eigenvector diagnostics and spread complexity. We find that the two- and four-loop truncations develop GOE-like level statistics at sufficiently large coupling but with features characteristic of weak integrability breaking. The integrability breaking at four-loops is weaker than at two-loops and the critical coupling at which chaos occurs is larger, at least for long spin chains. The three-loop truncation does not show the same onset of chaos in the range studied. Eigenvector diagnostics show that the corresponding eigenstates remain less random than GOE vectors, indicating weak ergodicity and multifractality. Finally, we can identify signatures of the eigenvalue and eigenvector chaos in the Krylov-space data. Namely, we demonstrate a correlation of the level spacing statistics with the peak of spread complexity and disorder on the Krylov chain. The delocalisation of the initial state in the Hamiltonian eigenbasis is shown to strongly affect the saturation of complexity. Our results suggest that finite-loop dilatation operators are not generic long-range spin chain Hamiltonians, but already display patterns consistent with the restoration of integrability in the all-loop planar theory.

</details>


### [23] [Tracing Transcendentality in Protected Correlators of N=4 SYM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18362)
*Marco S. Bianchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了N=4超杨-米尔斯理论（N=4 SYM）中受保护标量算子的两点函数，计算到双圈阶及经典维度10，发现均匀超越性（uniform transcendentality）在高维算子处出现可控的局部破缺，并通过应力张量多重态（stress-tensor multiplet）因子数量给出完整平面图（planar）外推公式，结果与局域化（localization）预言一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究N=4 SYM中受保护标量算子的两点函数在维度约化（dimensional reduction）下的超越性（transcendentality）性质，尤其是高维算子在量子修正中的超越性行为是否保持均匀。

Method: 通过显式计算至双圈阶（two loops）且算子经典维度至10，涵盖所有迹结构（trace structures），并利用平面图外推（planar extrapolation）方法推广到任意维度和迹结构。

Result: 单圈修正是普适的（universal）；双圈阶发现更高维度算子出现均匀超越性的可控局部破缺，该破缺可通过合适的关联函数组合完全抵消；给出了完整的平面图外推公式，其依赖完全由算子中应力张量多重态因子数量控制；所有可比较情形下与局域化预言一致。

Conclusion: 均匀超越性在受保护标量算子的两点函数中并非在所有阶都严格保持，但破缺具有可预测的结构，且与局域化结果吻合，表明该方法在更高维度算子的可积性（integrability）研究中具有推广价值。

Abstract: We study two-point functions of protected scalar operators in N=4 SYM, focusing on their transcendentality properties in dimensional reduction, where quantum corrections are subleading in the regulator. We compute the correlators explicitly through two loops and operators up to classical dimension 10, for all trace structures. The one-loop correction is universal. At two loops, we find a controlled partial breaking of uniform transcendentality for higher-dimensional operators, which can be cancelled by suitable combinations of correlators in a fully predictable way. A main result is a complete planar extrapolation for two-loop correlators at arbitrary dimension and trace structure, whose dependence is entirely controlled by the number of stress-tensor multiplet factors in the operator. The perturbative results agree with localization predictions in all cases where comparisons are possible.

</details>


### [24] [What makes spacetime spin in string theory?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18380)
*Matilda Delgado,Lorenz Eberhardt,Marija Tomašević*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在没有定向膜（orientifolds）的情况下，II型弦论要求目标时空X具有自旋结构（spin structure）这一条件，直接源于世界面GSO投影（worldsheet GSO projection）的一致性。该一致性条件由$(-1)^{\text{F}_L}$与目标空间背景数据之间的混合整体反常（mixed global anomaly）给出，可通过自旋配边群（spin bordism group）$Ω_3^{\mathrm{spin}}(B\mathbb{Z}_2\times X)$检测；该反常的消失对于光滑目标空间等价于X是自旋的，对于一般轨道簇（orbifold）$[\hat{X}/G]$则要求$\hat{X}$具有G-等变自旋结构（G-equivariant spin structure）。此外，论文对所有可能的θ角（theta angles）进行了分类，并证明它们对应于弦论微扰论（string perturbation theory）中所有可能的连续和离散背景场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: II型弦论中目标时空必须具有自旋结构是教科书中的熟知条件，但其根源——即该条件与世界面GSO投影一致性的内在联系——尚未被直接证明。本文旨在从世界面理论的一致性出发，系统地推导这一要求，并同时处理更一般的轨道簇情形以及θ角的分类问题。

Method: 利用自旋配边群$Ω_3^{\mathrm{spin}}(B\mathbb{Z}_2\times X)$检测$(-1)^{\text{F}_L}$与目标空间背景场之间的混合整体反常；通过计算该混合配边群（mixed bordism group），识别GSO投影后的世界面理论的配边类（bordism class），进而分析反常消失的条件。

Result: 混合整体反常的消失条件在光滑目标空间情形下精确还原了X需为自旋流形的经典结论；在一般轨道簇$[\hat{X}/G]$情形下，该条件要求$\hat{X}$承载一个G-等变自旋结构。同时，所有可能的θ角被分类，并证明它们对应弦论微扰论中所有可能的连续和离散背景场。

Conclusion: 从世界面GSO投影的一致性出发，可以严格导出目标时空自旋结构的必要性，且该分析自然地推广到轨道簇和背景场分类等更一般的情形，为II型弦论的背景一致性提供了更深刻的量子基础。

Abstract: Type II string theory in the absence of orientifolds requires the target spacetime $X$ to admit a spin structure. We show that this familiar requirement arises directly from the consistency of the worldsheet GSO projection. The obstruction is a mixed global anomaly between $(-1)^{\text{F}_L}$ and the target space background data, detected by the spin bordism group $Ω_3^{\mathrm{spin}}(B\mathbb{Z}_2\times X)$. We compute the relevant mixed bordism group and identify the bordism class of the GSO-projected worldsheet theory. For smooth target spaces, vanishing of the anomaly reduces to the condition that $X$ is spin, while for general orbifolds $[\hat{X}/G]$, $\hat{X}$ has to carry a $G$-equivariant spin structure. We also classify all possible theta angles in the worldsheet theory and show that they correspond to all possible continuous and discrete background fields of the target space theory visible in string perturbation theory.

</details>


### [25] [An effective field theory approach to the sign problem in BFSS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18396)
*Gauri Batra,Henry W. Lin,Haifeng Tang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种有效场论方法来分析费米子量子理论中的符号问题，并将其应用于D0-膜/BFSS矩阵量子力学。研究发现连续理论在't Hooft大N区域存在符号问题，但该问题在高温展开中延迟出现（需到10圈阶），且对热力学量的影响在温度T ≳ λ^{1/3}时较小，但在强耦合下可能加剧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 符号问题（sign problem）是经典模拟含费米子量子理论时面临的主要障碍。本文旨在提出一种有效场论方法，系统分析符号问题的产生机制和严重程度。

Method: 采用有效场论方法：在高温极限下，d+1维场论约化为d维玻色理论，高维理论中Pfaffian的相位编码在低维理论的一个算符中。将该框架应用于D0-膜/BFSS矩阵量子力学，此时相位变为玻色子多矩阵积分中的一个算符。

Result: 连续理论中的符号问题在't Hooft大N区域仍然存在，但需进行到10圈阶的高温展开才能检测到。该延迟源于Pfaffian相位具有O(9)赝标量（pseudoscalar）变换性质；相关图贡献的前因子数值上很小。因此忽略符号问题对热力学量的分数误差在T ≳ λ^{1/3}时较小，但在't Hooft区域强耦合下符号问题可能更严重。

Conclusion: 有效场论框架成功揭示了符号问题在高温展开中的延迟出现机制，并量化了其对热力学量的影响。该方法还可推广至更高维度的最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论（maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theories）的分析中。

Abstract: The sign problem is a notorious obstacle for classically simulating quantum theories with fermions. We propose an effective field theory method for analyzing the sign problem. At high temperatures, a $d$+1 dimensional field theory reduces to a bosonic $d$-dimensional theory; the phase of the Pfaffian in the higher dimensional theory is encoded in an operator in the lower dimensional theory. We apply this framework to the D0-brane/BFSS matrix quantum mechanics, where the phase becomes an operator in a bosonic multi-matrix integral. Our results show that the continuum theory has a sign problem that persists in the large-$N$ 't Hooft regime. However, detecting the sign problem involves going to 10-loop order in the high-temperature expansion. This delayed onset follows from the fact that the Pfaffian phase transforms as an $O(9)$ pseudoscalar. Furthermore, the relevant diagrams give a numerically small prefactor. Consequently, ignoring the sign problem leads to a relatively small fractional error in thermodynamic quantities for temperatures $T \gtrsim λ^{1/3}$. However, at stronger coupling in the 't Hooft regime, the sign problem may become more severe. Finally, we initiate the application of this framework to higher-dimensional maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theories.

*Tsvetan Vetsov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作主要关注翘曲黑洞的经典稳定性，对其热力学稳定性与涨落行为的研究尚不充分。本文旨在系统分析该黑洞解的热力学稳定性，并引入超越经典分析的有限时间非平衡涨落理论，以刻画宏观态间的弛豫过程。

Method: 基于修正的有限时间非平衡Ruppeiner Hessian涨落理论（modified finite-time nonequilibrium extension of Ruppeiner's Hessian-based fluctuation theory），结合热力学状态空间中的测地线方法，对等熵与等能过程进行精确解析。

Result: 确认翘曲黑洞热力学不稳定并识别出非平凡的Davies相变曲线（Davies phase-transition curves）；在等熵与等能过程中得到热力学状态空间上的精确角动量轨迹（on-shell angular momentum trajectories）及热力学长度（thermodynamic lengths），这些量可估算弛豫时间；热力学测地线方程不允许恒定角动量解，表明角动量连续变化。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic stability and the stochastic thermal fluctuations of the warped black hole solution in three-dimensional General Massive Gravity. We demonstrate that the black hole is thermodynamically unstable and identify the nontrivial Davies phase-transition curves from the behavior of its admissible heat capacities. Going beyond the classical stability analysis, we study thermal fluctuations within a modified finite-time nonequilibrium extension of Ruppeiner's Hessian-based fluctuation theory. For a class of isentropic and isoenergetic processes, we derive exact on-shell angular momentum trajectories in the thermodynamic state space and compute the corresponding thermodynamic lengths. These quantities characterize relaxation processes between macrostates and provide an estimate of the associated relaxation times. Furthermore, we show that the thermodynamic geodesic equations do not admit constant-angular-momentum solutions, suggesting a continuous change of the black hole's angular momentum. Our results consistently reproduce the warped AdS$_3$ black hole limit of Topological Massive Gravity.

### [27] [Two-point functions in $4-2\,\varepsilon$ dimensions from localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18442)
*Alessandro Georgoudis,Joseph A. Minahan,Anton Nedelin,Congkao Wen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在 S^d 球面上使用超对称局域化（supersymmetric localization）推导微扰矩阵模型（matrix model）表达式，得到关联函数的 ε-展开；在平面极限（planar limit）下获得全阶领头阶结果，并推广到有限-N 修正（finite-N corrections）和高电荷算符（higher-charge operators）。与平坦空间（flat space）中的直接微扰计算进行对比验证。

Result: 在 ε 阶（order ε），超对称局域化结果与微扰计算完全一致；在更高阶，由于共形对称性（conformal symmetry）在偏离四维时破缺，局域化构造无法复现微扰数据。针对维度二算符，通过分析偏差的具体形式，推测了一个 ε² 阶的全阶公式（all-loop formula）。

Conclusion: 超对称局域化在 ε 阶能正确描述关联函数，但更高阶的构造因共形对称性破缺而失效；对特定算符可通过偏差形式猜测更高阶的全阶结果，为理解非整数维度下超对称场论提供了参考。

Abstract: We study two-point functions of half-BPS operators in maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory continued to $d=4-2\,\varepsilon$ dimensions. Using supersymmetric localization on $S^d$, we derive perturbative matrix-model expressions for the $\varepsilon$-expansion of these correlators and obtain all-loop results at leading order in $\varepsilon$ in the planar limit, with extensions to finite-$N$ corrections and higher-charge operators. We compare the localization results with direct perturbative computations in flat space. At order $\varepsilon$ the two descriptions agree perfectly, while at higher orders our construction fails to reproduce the perturbative data due to the breaking of conformal symmetry away from four dimensions. Nevertheless, in the case of the dimension-two operator we conjecture an all-loop formula at order $\varepsilon^2$ by exploiting the precise form of the mismatch.

### [28] [Tropical WKB asymptotics of NRS coordinates for opers in $SU(2)$, $N_f=4$ theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18452)
*Vasilii Iugov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立半经典极限下 SL₂-opers 与 Seiberg-Witten 可积系统之间的精确联系，特别是在 Nekrasov-Rosly-Shatashvili (NRS) Darboux 坐标框架下，检验热带化后的渐近行为是否能恢复超对称规范理论的 Seiberg-Witten 周期结构。

Method: 采用精确 WKB 连接公式（exact WKB connection formulae）将 SL₂(C) 特征簇的迹坐标表达为 Voros 指数的有限洛朗和（finite Laurent sums）。对所得公式及 NRS 关系进行热带化（tropicalization），得到腔状（chamberwise）整数仿射线性系统。在所选腔中验证系统的幺模性（unimodular）与所选周期的原始辛对（primitive symplectic pair）条件。

Result: 在幺模且周期构成原始辛对的腔中，NRS 坐标的首项渐近行为（leading asymptotics）经味道周期平移（flavor-period shifts）后，与 N=2 SU(2) N_f=4 理论的 Seiberg-Witten 周期一致。在样本腔和弱耦合退化（weak-coupling degeneration）中验证了该机制。弱耦合退化下，可选择与 plumbing limit 兼容的 NRS 坐标图，使得所得腔在热带壁（tropical walls）之外是幺模且非退化的。

Conclusion: 不存在全局坐标无关的恢复定理（global coordinate-independent recovery theorem）；非幺模或退化腔被视为所选 NRS 坐标图的局限性。本文的方法仅能在特定腔中建立渐近等价关系，而非普遍的坐标无关对应。

Abstract: We study the semiclassical limit of SL_2-opers on the four-punctured sphere in Nekrasov-Rosly-Shatashvili Darboux coordinates. Using exact Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin (WKB) connection formulae, we express the trace coordinates of the corresponding SL_2(C) character variety as finite Laurent sums of Voros exponentials. Tropicalizing these formulae and the NRS relations gives a chamberwise integer affine linear system for the leading logarithms of the NRS coordinates. In chambers where this system is unimodular and the selected cycles form a primitive symplectic pair, the leading asymptotics agree, up to flavor-period shifts, with Seiberg-Witten periods of the N=2 SU(2) theory with N_f=4 fundamental hypermultiplets. We verify this mechanism in a sample chamber and in the weak-coupling degeneration. No global coordinate-independent recovery theorem is claimed; non-unimodular or degenerate chambers are treated as limitations of the chosen NRS chart. In the weak-coupling degeneration, we show that the NRS chart can be chosen compatibly with the plumbing limit so that the resulting chamber is unimodular and non-degenerate away from tropical walls.

Abstract: We present a holographic dual of a two dimensional conformal field theory with non-hermitian but Parity-Time (PT) symmetric boundary conditions, by applying the AdS/BCFT duality and by introducing an imaginary valued scalar field localized on an end-of-the-world brane. We find that as we increase the strength of the non-hermitian PT symmetric interactions, the system experiences a spontaneous PT symmetry breaking. ### [30] [A Note on Corrections to Entanglement Wedge Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18639)
*Edward Witten*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文定量证明了在量子引力全息对偶（holographic duality）中，若RT公式的面积项量级为1/G而体熵量级为1，则纠缠楔重构（entanglement wedge reconstruction）的修正相对于面积函数的修正是指数小（exponentially small，以G为底）。研究同时讨论了该框架中存在面积函数但不存在面积算符（area operator）的现象及其在全息学中的预期行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在精确纠缠楔重构假设下，RT公式中的面积项是c数，体量子态的选择不影响几何。Cao等人最近考虑了偏离精确重构的微扰，定义了最优重构和依赖于量子态的有效面积函数。本文旨在将该图像的一个方面——重构修正与面积函数修正的相对大小——进行定量化分析。

Method: 论文采用解析论证的方法，基于RT公式面积项量级为O(1/G)而体熵量级为O(1)的假定，通过数量级分析（order-of-magnitude analysis）比较纠缠楔重构修正与面积函数修正的相对大小，得出前者相对于后者为指数小的结论。

Result: 文章证明，在该假设框架下，纠缠楔重构的修正相对于面积函数的修正具有指数小的量级（exponentially small in G）。此外，研究指出现有框架中存在面积函数但不存在面积算符，并探讨了这一特征在全息学中是否属于预期行为。

Conclusion: 本文定量刻画了偏离精确纠缠楔重构时修正的相对大小，确认重构修正远小于面积函数修正，从而为该理论框架提供了更精确的定量支撑。同时，关于面积函数与面积算符的讨论为进一步理解全息对偶中的几何与量子态关系提供了线索。

Abstract: If entanglement wedge reconstruction is exact, then (under certain assumptions) the area term in the RT formula is a c-number, indicating that the choice of a bulk quantum state does not influence the geometry. Recently Cao, Cheng, Karthikeyan, Li, and Preskill considered a generic perturbation away from exact entanglement wedge reconstruction. The optimal reconstruction was defined; based on this, an effective area function that depends nontrivially on the quantum state was defined and its properties were analyzed. Here we make one aspect of this picture more quantitative, by showing that if as expected the area term in the RT formula is of order 1/G while the bulk entropy is of order 1, then the corrections to entanglement wedge reconstruction are exponentially small (in G) relative to corrections to the area function. In the framework under discussion, there is an area function but no area operator; we discuss to what extent this is the expected behavior in holography.

### [31] [SUSY meets pseudo-Hermiticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18641)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用超场形式（superfield formalism）构建伪厄米 Wess-Zumino 模型，其中超场为 Grassmann 奇数，通过伪厄米共轭（pseudo-Hermitian conjugation）定义场共轭以绕过传统的自旋统计定理（spin-statistics theorem）。为引入非零三次相互作用，将该模型与厄米 Wess-Zumino 模型耦合。

Conclusion: 伪厄米 Wess-Zumino 模型是超对称伪厄米量子场论的一个可行构造，通过伪厄米共轭规避了常规自旋统计定理，且与厄米 Wess-Zumino 模型耦合可以保持超对称性并引入有意义的相互作用项。

Abstract: In this work, we construct the simplest pseudo-Hermitian quantum field theory that is supersymmetric. This is the pseudo-Hermitian Wess-Zumino model in the sense that it contains a pair of symplectic fermions (anti-commuting scalar fields) that satisfy the Klein-Gordon equation and a spin-half boson that satisfies the Dirac equation. The conventional spin-statistics theorem is circumvented through the use of pseudo-Hermitian conjugation to define field adjoints. To make the supersymmetry manifest, we formulate the pseudo-Hermitian Wess-Zumino model using the superfield formalism. These superfields are Grassmann-odd so it is not possible to construct non-vanishing cubic interactions using only these superfields. We show that this problem can be resolved by coupling the pseudo-Hermitian Wess-Zumino model with the Hermitian Wess-Zumino model while preserving supersymmetry.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示双标度SYK模型与ASEP以及拓扑序（topological order）中奇异关联子之间的深层数学结构联系。

Method: 将双标度SYK模型的转移矩阵矩（moment of the transfer matrix）重新表达为ASEP稳态（stationary state）与一个乘积态（product state）的内积（overlap），并类比Levin-Wen弦网模型与Turaev-Viro态和之间的奇异关联子。

Result: 双标度SYK模型的转移矩阵矩等于ASEP稳态与乘积态的重叠；该重叠被论证是奇异关联子的类似物。

Conclusion: 该发现建立了双标度SYK模型与ASEP及拓扑场论（topological field theory）之间的新对应关系，丰富了可积系统与全息对偶（holographic duality）之间的交叉视角。

Abstract: We show that the moment of the transfer matrix of the double scaled SYK model is written as an overlap between the stationary state of ASEP (asymmetric simple exclusion process) and a product state. We argue that this overlap is an analogue of the strange correlator appearing in the correspondence between the Levin-Wen string-net model and the Turaev-Viro state sum.

### [33] [Hydrodynamics of perfect fluids with anomalies from the fermionic path integral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18779)
*Alexander G. Abanov,Andrea Cappelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermion）的路径积分（path integral）分析，在红外极限（infrared limit）下推导出与完美正压流体（perfect barotropic fluid）在零温异常情况下对应的流体力学有效作用量（hydrodynamic action），并识别出其中的跨界项（transgression forms）作为切恩-西蒙斯形式（Chern-Simons forms）的推广，为异常流体力学（anomalous hydrodynamics）作用量公式化提供了微观解释和红外约化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在从微观量子场论出发，解释和推导包含反常（anomaly）的流体力学作用量的构成要素，并阐明从有效场论（effective field theory）到局域流体力学描述（local hydrodynamic description）所需的红外约化（infrared reduction）机制。

Method: 通过分析带有矢量背景场和轴矢量背景场（axial gauge backgrounds）以及残余无关流-流相互作用（residual irrelevant current-current interaction）的狄拉克费米子路径积分，在积分掉费米子后，得到半经典的低能有效作用量（semiclassical low-energy effective action），并将其与已知流体力学作用量进行比较。

Result: 所得作用量对应于零温下带反常的完美正压流体的流体力学作用量；该方法还得到了分别对应于外尔费米子（Weyl fermion）以及具有独立矢量和轴矢流的狄拉克费米子的两种额外流体力学作用量。这些作用量包含四维和五维的体-边界项（bulk-boundary terms），源于反常流入（anomaly inflow），被识别为跨界项（transgression forms），即涉及两个规范场（动态场和背景场）的切恩-西蒙斯形式的推广。

Conclusion: 路径积分论证为包含反常所需的流体力学作用量公式化中的若干要素提供了微观解释；同时阐明了从有效场论到局域流体力学描述所需的红外约化，该约化通过考虑流体力学中常见的受限变分（restricted variations）来实现，使得五维跨界项产生四维运动方程。

Abstract: The path integral of the Dirac fermion with vector and axial gauge backgrounds is analyzed near the infrared limit in the presence of residual irrelevant current-current interaction. After integrating out fermions, a semiclassical low-energy effective action is obtained, written in terms of currents. Its expression is found to correspond to the hydrodynamic action previously proposed for perfect barotropic fluids with anomalies at zero temperature. This approach also leads to two further hydrodynamic actions to be associated, respectively, with the Weyl fermion, and the Dirac fermion having independent vector and axial currents. These actions feature four- and five-dimensional bulk-boundary terms, owing to anomaly inflow, which are identified as being the so-called transgression forms. These are generalizations of Chern--Simons forms that involve two gauge fields: the dynamical field and the background field. The path-integral argument provides a ``microscopic'' explanation for several ingredients of the action formulation of hydrodynamics that are necessary to incorporate anomalies. It also clarifies the infrared reduction required to pass from the effective field theory to a local hydrodynamic description. This reduction is implemented by considering restricted variations of the action, familiar from hydrodynamics, which at the same time lead to four-dimensional equations of motion from the five-dimensional transgression terms.

Abstract: Color graphs and their subgraphs, referred to as bubble graphs, correspond bijectively to the simplicial complexes of pseudomanifolds and their subsimplices, respectively. By using this correspondence, we define simplicial-complex matrices and subsimplex matrices that encode the simplicial complexes of pseudomanifolds and their subsimplices. Moreover, we formulate mutation and crossover operations on colored graphs. ### [37] [Universal Closed Form for Dynamical Love Numbers of Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19281)
*Mikhail P. Solon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究给出了史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）动态响应函数 $\bar{F}_{\ell,s}$ 的闭式解析解，涵盖所有自旋 $s$ 与多极数 $\ell$；该结果通过重整化群（renormalization group）方法重新求和了无穷阶的远区对数项，并在壳有效场论（shell effective field theory）框架下通过标量、电磁与引力扰动独立验证至 $\mathcal O(G^{15})$ 阶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞静态Love数（Love numbers）已知为零，但动态响应（dynamical response）非零，且其精确形式依赖于计算方案。本文旨在给出方案无关的闭式解析结果，以统一描述任意自旋与多极数的史瓦西黑洞动态响应。

Method: 采用重整化群方法，通过远区对数解的重新求和（resummation），将无穷阶对数项归并为普适的 $\tau$ 函数，其中包含一系列Riemann zeta值（Riemann zeta values），该序列源于远区的 $Γ(1-η)$ 散射控制因子。结果分解为三个核心要素：视界处的硬匹配系数（hard matching coefficient）、近区的反常维数（anomalous dimension）以及远区的修饰对数的（dressed log）。此外，使用壳有效场论独立验证标量、电磁与引力扰动情况。

Result: 得到了动态响应 $\bar{F}_{\ell,s}$ 的闭式表达式：$\bar{F}_{\ell,s}/4πR_S^{2\ell+1}=Φ_{\ell,s}(\bar{y})-\tfrac12η\,Φ_{\ell,s}'(\bar{y})$，其中 $\bar{y}=-\tfrac12η^2τ$，$η=iωR_S$。该形式在所有阶次上均成立，且展示出跨多极数与自旋的普适性。

Conclusion: 史瓦西黑洞的动态响应可解析地表示为重整化群主导对数解的简单组合，并通过重新求和将牛顿相位（Newtonian phase）的无穷项级数整合为闭式。该结果在壳有效场论框架下得到高精度数值验证，证明其方案无关性与普适性。

Abstract: Black hole static Love numbers vanish, but their dynamical counterparts do not. We present the scheme-independent dynamical response $\bar{F}_{\ell,s}$ of a Schwarzschild black hole in closed form, to all orders, and for every spin $s$ and multipole $\ell$. The result is $\bar{F}_{\ell,s}/4πR_S^{2\ell+1}=Φ_{\ell,s}(\bar{y})-\tfrac12η\,Φ_{\ell,s}'(\bar{y})$ with $\bar{y}=-\tfrac12η^2τ$ and $η=iωR_S$. Here $Φ_{\ell,s}$ is simply the leading-log solution to the renormalization group equation, but lifting the running logarithm to $τ=\log(R_S/R)-2\sum_{k\ge2}ζ_k\,η^{k-1}$ resums it to all orders. This tower of Riemann zeta values is the Newtonian phase in disguise: it originates from the same far-zone $Γ(1-η)$ that governs long-range scattering, and is universal across multipole and spin. Our result exhibits a factorization pinned to three ingredients: the hard matching coefficient at the horizon, the anomalous dimension in the near zone, and the dressed log in the far zone. Using shell effective field theory, we independently verify our formula for scalar, electromagnetic, and gravitational perturbations, reaching $\mathcal O(G^{15})$.

</details>


### [38] [Post-Carroll Algebra, Conformal Extensions, and Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19112)
*Mojtaba Najafizade*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出“后卡罗尔变换”（post-Carroll transformations），引入“后卡罗尔代数”（post-Carroll algebra）及其共形推广，发现该代数在高维允许中心荷，形成“卡罗尔-巴格曼代数”（Carroll-Bargmann algebra）；其共形版本精确匹配高维卡罗尔-薛定谔理论（Carroll-Schrödinger theory）的对称性；并推导出后卡罗尔共形场论（post-Carrollian CFT）的两点函数形式，其中$1+1$维存在电和磁两个扇区，高维仅存磁扇区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准卡罗尔代数（Carroll algebra）在高维中不允许存在中心荷，限制了其在场论和对称性分析中的应用。为突破这一限制并更精确地描述卡罗尔-薛定谔理论（Carroll-Schrödinger theory）等物理系统，有必要引入包含$c$依赖修正的扩展对称结构。

Method: 通过在卡罗尔变换中引入领先阶的$c$依赖修正，定义后卡罗尔变换（post-Carroll transformations）；在此基础上构造后卡罗尔代数（post-Carroll algebra），进而构建其共形推广，以及与中心荷兼容的卡罗尔-巴格曼代数（Carroll-Bargmann algebra）的共形版本，即卡罗尔-薛定谔代数（Carroll-Schrödinger algebra）。利用场论方法分析在这些对称性下不变的场论，并推导后卡罗尔共形场论（post-Carrollian CFT）中两点函数的一般形式。

Result: 后卡罗尔代数在高维中允许中心荷存在，形成卡罗尔-巴格曼代数（Carroll-Bargmann algebra）。其共形推广——卡罗尔-薛定谔代数（Carroll-Schrödinger algebra）——精确匹配高维卡罗尔-薛定谔理论（Carroll-Schrödinger theory）的对称代数。两点函数在$1+1$维后卡罗尔共形场论（post-Carrollian CFT）中同时展现出电扇区（electric sector）和磁扇区（magnetic sector），而在高维中仅存磁扇区（magnetic sector）。

Conclusion: 后卡罗尔变换及其代数为理解超越标准卡罗尔对称性的物理系统提供了更丰富的代数结构，特别是在高维中引入中心荷的能力，使得与卡罗尔-薛定谔理论（Carroll-Schrödinger theory）的对称性精确匹配成为可能。共形场论分析揭示了不同维度下扇区结构的差异，为后续相关场论和量子力学研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: By incorporating leading $c\,$-dependent corrections to the Carroll transformations, we introduce the ``post-Carroll transformations''. We demonstrate that these transformations are consistent with post-Carrollian mechanics \cite{Najafizadeh:2025ksm}; furthermore, they give rise to the so-called ``post-Carroll algebra''. We show that, unlike the Carroll algebra, this new structure allows for a central charge in higher dimensions; we refer to it as the ``Carroll-Bargmann algebra''. To construct conformal extensions, we first build the conformal extension of the post-Carroll algebra and study field theories invariant under this symmetry. We then construct the conformal extension of the Carroll-Bargmann algebra, referred to as the ``Carroll-Schrödinger algebra'', and demonstrate that it precisely matches the symmetry algebra of the higher-dimensional Carroll-Schrödinger theory \cite{Najafizadeh:2024imn}. Finally, we derive the general form of two-point functions in a post-Carrollian CFT, which in $1+1$ dimensions exhibits both electric and magnetic sectors, while in higher dimensions only the magnetic sector survives.

### [39] [Bubble wall velocity and nucleation rates in inverse holographic phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19166)

Result: 对于退禁闭相变，两相之间自由度数目的大跳跃导致气泡壁速度参数化地小，研究给出了临界温度附近的粗略估计。对于手征相变，则通过稳态近似计算得到了气泡壁速度和摩擦力。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of first-order inverse phase transitions (driven by superheating) at strong coupling, focusing on the top-down Witten-Sakai-Sugimoto model for holographic QCD. Two cases are considered: the deconfinement transition in the unflavored version of the model and a chiral symmetry-restoring transition occurring in the deconfined phase of the full theory. In both cases, we imagine driving the system into a metastable phase at high temperature, inducing the nucleation of bubbles of the stable phase. For both classes of transitions, we find the corresponding Euclidean bounce solutions and compute the bubble nucleation rates and the relevant transition parameters. For the deconfinement transition, the large jump in the number of degrees of freedom between the two phases suggests that the bubble wall velocity is parametrically small; we provide a rough estimate of it near the critical temperature. In the case of the chiral transition, instead, we compute the bubble wall velocity and the friction force exerted on the bubbles employing motivated ansatze and approximations for the steady-state configurations.

### [40] [Spectral Functions of Lorentzian Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19321)
*Gabriel Assant,Daniel F. Litim,Manuel Reichert*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过适用于洛伦兹符号泛函重整化群方法，计算了引力子模式的谱函数，实现了经典广义相对论与渐近安全紫外不动点之间的插值，并得到了可归一化的谱函数，同时计算了到曲率二次阶的全量子有效作用量及引力子诱导的形状因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力的可重整性与幺正性是核心问题。本文旨在通过计算洛伦兹量子引力中引力子模式的谱函数，检验渐近安全场景（asymptotically safe scenario）下紫外不动点（ultraviolet fixed point）与经典广义相对论之间的平滑插值，并探讨幺正性（unitarity）的一致性。

Method: 采用适用于洛伦兹符号（Lorentzian signature）的泛函重整化（functional renormalisation）方法，并引入新的对称性条件以考虑底层Ward恒等式（Ward identities）。直接推导并求解传播子的Källén-Lehmann表示（Källén-Lehmann representation）的流方程（flow equations）。

Result: 在多种重整化条件（renormalisation conditions）下得到了一致的结果：引力子（graviton）和标量引力子模式（scalar graviton mode）均具有可归一化的谱函数（normalisable spectral functions），且与红外有效理论（effective theory）相符。此外，计算了到曲率二次阶的全量子有效作用量（full quantum effective action），并提取了引力子诱导的形状因子（graviton-induced form factors）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，在渐近安全框架下，洛伦兹量子引力能够产生可归一化的谱函数，且与红外有效理论一致。基于形状因子的分析，本文进一步讨论了幺正性对量子引力的意义。

Abstract: We compute spectral functions of graviton modes in Lorentzian quantum gravity, interpolating between classical general relativity and an asymptotically safe ultraviolet fixed point. Using functional renormalisation adapted for theories in Lorentzian signature, and enhanced by new symmetry conditions to account for underlying Ward identities, we derive and solve flow equations directly for the Källén-Lehmann representation of propagators. Consistent results are found for several sets of renormalisation conditions yielding normalisable spectral functions for the graviton and the scalar graviton mode, in agreement with effective theory in the infrared. We further calculate the full quantum effective action to quadratic order in curvature, extract graviton-induced form factors, and discuss implications for unitarity of quantum gravity.

</details>


### [41] [Higher-spin self-dual gravity from holomorphic planes in twistor space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19173)
*Nicolas Boulanger,Yannick Herfray,Lionel Mason,Noémie Parrini*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 论文证明了一个用于高自旋自对偶引力的“非线性引力子定理”，通过扭曲空间（twistor space）的复结构形变，构造了无限维高自旋空间并得到了高自旋自对偶引力方程的解，揭示了该理论与Lax对（Lax pair）可积性之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典非线性引力子定理推广到高自旋自对偶引力，探索高自旋理论在扭量（twistor）框架下的几何构造与可积结构。

Method: 考虑非射影扭量空间（non-projective twistor space）在原点附近有界区域的复结构（complex structure）小形变，研究全纯嵌入复平面（holomorphically embedded complex planes）构成的空间 $M_{HS}$；通过将时空 $\mathcal{M}$ 嵌入 $M_{HS}$ 得到高自旋自对偶解，并以Lax对形式体现可积性。

Result: 证明了 $M_{HS}$ 是一个无限维复流形，具有到四维全纯自对偶时空 $\mathcal{M}$ 的规范投影；不同嵌入选择对应高自旋对称性（higher-spin symmetries）；给出了Lax对并推测手性高自旋引力（chiral higher-spin gravity）可通过原点无约束形变实现。

Conclusion: 成功建立了高自旋自对偶引力的非线性扭量构造，其几何结构自然导出了系统的可积性；对手性高自旋引力给出了类似的构造前景。

Abstract: We prove a `nonlinear graviton theorem' for higher-spin self-dual gravity. We consider small deformations of the complex structure of the non-projective twistor space that are bounded in a specified region near the origin and investigate the space $M_{HS}$ of holomorphically embedded complex planes $\mathbb{C}^2$ that intersect the origin. We show that this space is an infinite dimensional complex manifold with a canonical projection onto a four-dimensional holomorphic self-dual spacetime $\mathcal{M}$, and discuss the geometry induced on this new higher-spin space. Solutions of higher-spin self-dual gravity are then obtained by choosing an embedding of spacetime $\mathcal{M}$ into higher-spin space $M_{HS}$, with higher-spin symmetries arising from the different choices of embedding. Integrability of the theory is manifested in the form of a Lax pair for the system that we present. We conjecture that chiral higher-spin gravity can similarly be realized by considering deformations that are unconstrained at the origin.

</details>


### [42] [A Dispersive Bootstrap for the Virasoro-Shapiro Amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19283)
*Yongjun Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用色散S矩阵自举（dispersive S-matrix bootstrap）研究闭弦树级Virasoro-Shapiro振幅，通过解析性、交叉对称性、分波幺正性和Regge有界性等约束，结合Virasoro启发的非线性关系，将允许的参数区域压缩至包含Virasoro-Shapiro点的小岛，并给出解析自举解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验闭弦树级Virasoro-Shapiro振幅是否可以从更基本的物理原理（如解析性、幺正性、交叉对称性）出发，通过S矩阵自举方法（S-matrix bootstrap）唯一确定，而无需直接假设弦论（string theory）的具体微观结构。

Method: 对十维最大超对称四点振幅施加解析性（analyticity）、交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）、分波幺正性（partial-wave unitarity）和Regge有界性（Regge boundedness）；显式保留无质量引力子极点；利用色散关系（dispersion relations）和交叉零约束（crossing null constraints）导出低能Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）的数值界；引入Virasoro启发的非线性关系族进一步缩小允许区域；最后构造引力极点减除（gravity-pole-subtracted）设置，使振幅正则部分的前向极限良好定义。

Result: 色散关系和交叉零约束给出了低能系数（以引力耦合归一化）的数值界；Virasoro启发的非线性关系将允许区域显著压缩；在极点减除设置下，非线性约束将允许区域缩小至包含Virasoro-Shapiro点的小岛。

Conclusion: S矩阵自举方法可以有效约束闭弦振幅的低能参数，且Virasoro-Shapiro振幅在该自举框架下具有解析自举解释，表明弦振幅可能由基本物理原理唯一确定。

Abstract: We study the closed-string tree-level Virasoro-Shapiro amplitude using the dispersive S-matrix bootstrap. For the ten-dimensional maximally supersymmetric four-point amplitude, we impose analyticity, crossing symmetry, partial-wave unitarity, and Regge boundedness. With the massless graviton pole kept explicitly, the resulting dispersion relations and crossing null constraints give numerical bounds on the leading low-energy coefficients normalized by the gravitational coupling. We then introduce a Virasoro-inspired ansatz, which becomes a set of nonlinear relations among Wilson coefficients and shrinks the allowed region toward the Virasoro-Shapiro trajectory. Finally, we study a gravity-pole-subtracted setup, where the regular part of the amplitude has a well-defined forward limit. In this stripped problem, the nonlinear constraints reduce the allowed region to a small island containing the Virasoro-Shapiro point, for which we provide an analytic bootstrap explanation.

</details>


### [43] [Gauging in superconductors and other electronic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18733)
*Marcus Berg,Andrea Cappelli,Riccardo Villa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用拓扑场论（topological field theory）和广义对称性（generalized symmetry）框架，重新描述了普通s波超导体（s-wave superconductor）的拓扑性质。研究表明，在极低能下希格斯模型（Higgs model）约化为具有拓扑序（topological order）的BF理论；规范场必须是spin$_c$联络以描述库珀对（Cooper pair）中电子的自旋。通过规范（gauging）操作，超导体本质上是玻色子系统，但保留了源于费米子起源的引力-磁反常（gravito-magnetic anomaly），该反常与通过规范费米子宇称$(-1)^F$实现的Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren玻色化（bosonization）相关，在三维和四维时空维度中普遍表征规范电子物质，并禁止出现平庸的大质量相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 普通s波超导体已被认识到是拓扑物质相（topological phases of matter），但其中的动力学规范场（dynamical gauge field）所蕴含的全局特征（global features）尚未被充分理解。本文旨在利用拓扑场论和广义对称性等工具，为这些系统提供一种更新的、更完整的理论描述。

Method: 采用拓扑场论（topological field theory）和广义对称性（generalized symmetry）的分析工具。具体地，在极低能极限下将希格斯模型（Higgs model）约化为BF理论以揭示拓扑序；引入spin$_c$联络作为规范场以描述库珀对中费米子的自旋；通过规范（gauging）操作处理费米子宇称$(-1)^F$，建立与Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren玻色化方案的联系。

Result: 识别出超导体中普遍存在一种引力-磁反常（gravito-magnetic anomaly），该反常是费米子起源的残留，并与Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren玻色化相关联。这一反常特征在三维和四维时空维度中普遍适用于规范电子物质（gauged electronic matter），禁止平庸的大质量相在低能下存在。该结论不仅适用于希格斯模型的有效性范围，也适用于其他类型的超导体，并且在三维电动力学（three-dimensional electrodynamics）的非平庸无质量相中同样出现。

Conclusion: 普通s波超导体在低能下具有拓扑序，本质上是带有引力-磁反常的玻色子系统；该反常是理解其拓扑性质的关键，且具有超越特定模型的普适性，为统一描述各类超导体的低能物理提供了新视角。

Abstract: Ordinary, s-wave superconductors have been recognized as being topological phases of matter, in which the dynamical gauge field implies less understood global features. Using the tools of topological field theories and generalized symmetries, we provide an updated description of these systems. At very low energies, the Higgs model reduces to the BF theory, which exhibits topological order. Furthermore, the gauge field must be a spin$_c$ connection, to describe the spin of fermions forming Cooper pairs. Gauging implies that superconductors are inherently bosonic systems, yet they are endowed with a gravito-magnetic anomaly that is the remnant of their fermionic origin. We recognize that this anomaly is related to the Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren bosonization, achieved via gauging fermion parity $(-1)^F$, now included in the gauge dynamics. This anomaly characterizes gauged electronic matter in great generality in three and four spacetime dimensions, forbidding trivial massive phases at low energy. It holds beyond the validity of the Higgs model, nd in other kinds of superconductors as well. It also appears in the nontrivial massless phase of three-dimensional electrodynamics, recently understood.

</details>

### [44] [The Collins-Soper kernel from a vacuum soft function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19221)
*Anthony Francis,C. -J. David Lin,Wayne Morris,Yong Zhao*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过欧几里得格点（Euclidean lattice）上的类空威尔逊线（space-like Wilson lines）与复方向矢量，从真空软函数（vacuum soft function）首次高精度计算了Collins-Soper核（Collins-Soper kernel），并发现其在横向分离较大时呈现饱和行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Collins-Soper核是描述夸克横向动量依赖演化（Collins-Soper evolution）的关键量，但此前基于强子观测量（hadronic observables）的格点计算在统计精度和系统性控制上仍有改进空间。

Method: 采用纯规范（pure gauge）计算，在欧几里得格点上构造具有复方向矢量的类空威尔逊线，通过真空软函数提取Collins-Soper核，并分析其快度差异（rapidity dependence）随Collins-Soper演化的行为。

Result: 该方法在软函数计算中达到了高统计精度（high statistical precision）；提取的Collins-Soper核误差与基于强子观测量的最前沿格点计算相当，但在大横向威尔逊线分离（transverse Wilson-line separations）处表现出饱和行为（saturated behavior）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于真空软函数的格点方法能够以可比精度提取Collins-Soper核，且其在大横向分离处的饱和特征可能为理解红外物理机制提供新的观测窗口。

Abstract: The Collins-Soper kernel is calculated from a vacuum soft function using space-like Wilson lines with complex-directional vectors on the Euclidean lattice. Our pure gauge calculations with this method achieve high statistical precision in computing the soft function, whose rapidity dependence is well described by Collins-Soper evolution across a wide range of rapidity differences. The extracted kernel contains errors comparable to those achieved in state-of-the-art lattice calculations based on hadronic observables, but exhibits saturated behavior at large transverse Wilson-line separations.

</details>

### [45] [Josephson spectroscopy in a circular atomic tunnel junction with acceleration-induced symmetry breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18706)
*Yurii Borysenko,Yuriy Bidasyuk,Olena Prykhodko,Gerhard Birkl,Dominik Pfeiffer,Ludwig Lind,Mark Edwards,Alexander Yakimenko*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究长原子玻色-约瑟夫森结（Bose-Josephson junction）在多模布居数不平衡响应下的约瑟夫森动力学（Josephson dynamics），提出基于弱局域周期微扰的模分辨约瑟夫森谱学方案，并通过耗散含时玻戈留波夫理论（dissipative time-dependent Bogoliubov theory）获得与全Gross-Pitaevskii模拟定量一致的解析响应函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）如何将单一约瑟夫森等离子体振荡（Josephson plasma oscillation）转化为多模布居数不平衡响应，并揭示其背后的集体模激活机制。

Method: 采用Gross-Pitaevskii方程模拟和玻戈留波夫-德让纳（Bogoliubov-de Gennes）分析；提出基于弱局域周期微扰的模分辨约瑟夫森谱学协议；建立耗散含时玻戈留波夫理论以计算线性响应函数。

Result: 频率扫描在活跃玻戈留波夫模（Bogoliubov modes）的本征频率处显示共振幅度峰和相移；驱动位置的角度扫描可揭示对应模密度扰动的角结构；解析响应函数与全Gross-Pitaevskii模拟定量一致。

Conclusion: 加速双环凝聚体（dual-ring condensates）为对称性选择的约瑟夫森动力学和集体模谱学探测提供了可控平台。

Abstract: We study Josephson dynamics in a long atomic Bose-Josephson junction formed by two tunnel-coupled coplanar Bose-Einstein-condensate rings. An in-plane linear acceleration breaks the axial symmetry of the trap and transforms a single Josephson plasma oscillation into a multimode population-imbalance response. Gross-Pitaevskii simulations and Bogoliubov-de Gennes analysis show that the additional spectral components arise from collective modes that acquire finite overlap with the population-imbalance operator under symmetry breaking, with their activation governed by reflection symmetry about the acceleration direction. We also propose a mode-resolved Josephson-spectroscopy protocol based on a weak localized periodic perturbation. Frequency scans reveal resonant amplitude peaks and phase shifts at the eigenfrequencies of active Bogoliubov modes, while angular scans of the drive position provide access to the angular structure of the corresponding mode density perturbations. A dissipative time-dependent Bogoliubov theory yields analytical response functions in quantitative agreement with full Gross-Pitaevskii simulations in the linear regime. Our results demonstrate that accelerated dual-ring condensates provide a controllable platform for symmetry-selected Josephson dynamics and spectroscopic probing of collective modes.

### [46] [On operator product expansion in the spin-orbit coupled bosonic system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19290)
*Rajesh Kumar Gupta,Siddhant Tiwari*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文推导了超冷玻色子系统中两个算符 ψ†_σ(r⃗) 和 ψ_σ'(r⃗') 的算符乘积展开（OPE），并重点分析其中的接触密度项（contact density term），该术语控制着玻色子系统中的普遍物理行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷玻色子系统可被调控以展现丰富的量子相变现象，如Rabi耦合系统中的铁磁/顺磁相和自旋-轨道耦合系统中的超固态（supersolidity）等。为深入探索这些相与相变背后的普遍物理，需要发展有效的多体分析工具，算符乘积展开（operator product expansion, OPE）正是其中之一。

Method: 本文从量子场论（quantum field theory）角度推导了两个费米子型算符 ψ†_σ(r⃗) 和 ψ_σ'(r⃗') 之间的OPE形式，特别聚焦于局部算符（local operators）级数展开中的接触密度项（contact density term）。

Result: 给出了两个分离算符的OPE级数展开形式，并明确了其中的接触密度项——该项控制了玻色子系统中的许多普适（universal）物理性质。

Conclusion: 算符乘积展开为探测超冷玻色子系统中丰富的量子相和相变提供了有效的多体物理工具，尤其是接触密度项在支配系统中的普适行为方面发挥关键作用。

Abstract: Ultra-cold bosonic systems can be tuned to exhibit quantum phase transitions. For example, the Rabi-coupled bosonic system exhibits ferromagnetic and paramagnetic phases, whereas the spin-orbit-coupled system exhibits exciting phases such as supersolidity. The physics of these phases and phase transitions is very rich. It is an important topic of research to probe these phases and phase transitions using various tools in many-body physics. The operator product expansion (OPE) provides one such tool. It expresses the product of two separated operators as a series expansion of local operators. In this article, we will derive the OPE of two operators $ψ^\dagger_σ(\vec r)$ and $ψ_{σ'}(\vec r')$. More specifically, we look for the contact density term, which controls many of the universal physics of the underlying bosonic system.

</details>


### [47] [Observation of anyonic thermodynamics and generalized Pauli principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19009)
*Fansu Wei,Chi Zhang,Zimeng Ye,Dengbo Wang,Botao Wang,Xiaoji Zhou,Hepeng Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究在一维强相互作用量子气体中实现了服从广义排斥统计（generalized exclusion statistics）的任意子热力学系综，通过测量状态方程等热力学量，观察到偏离玻色-爱因斯坦和费米-狄拉克统计的明确信号，为广义泡利原理提供了直接实验证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然具有分数交换统计（fractional exchange statistics）的任意子已在多种平台中被观测到，但广义排斥统计（generalized exclusion statistics）的实验实现及其热力学特征的直接测量此前一直未能实现。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 利用一维系统中动力学相互作用与统计相互作用之间的双射映射（bijective mapping），通过大范围调谐相互作用强度和温度，在一维强相互作用量子气体中构建任意子热力学系综，并测量其状态方程及其他热力学量。

Result: 测量到状态方程（equation of state）明显偏离玻色-爱因斯坦统计和费米-狄拉克统计（Bose-Einstein and Fermi-Dirac statistics），这些偏差被广义排斥统计定量描述。对压力（pressure）和Tan接触（Tan contact）等其他热力学量的独立探测进一步验证了这一理论框架。

Conclusion: 该结果为广义泡利原理（generalized Pauli principle）提供了直接实验证据，建立了一个用于工程化任意子排斥统计的通用平台，并为任意子在量子技术中的热力学应用开辟了前景。

Abstract: Anyons are quasiparticles with quantum statistics interpolating between those of bosons and fermions. Two distinct manifestations of anyonic behaviour have been theoretically established: fractional exchange statistics where particle exchange can produce any phase, and generalized exclusion statistics which extends the Pauli exclusion principle. While anyons exhibiting fractional exchange statistics have been observed in diverse platforms, experimental realizations of generalized exclusion statistics and direct measurements of its thermodynamic signatures have remained elusive. Here, we realize an anyonic thermodynamic ensemble obeying generalized exclusion statistics and detect its anyonic thermodynamics in a one-dimensional strongly interacting quantum gas. To achieve this, we exploit the bijective mapping between dynamical and statistical interactions in one dimension. By tuning interaction strength and temperature over a wide range, we measure the equation of state and identify clear departures from Bose-Einstein and Fermi-Dirac statistics. These deviations are quantitatively captured by generalized exclusion statistics, providing direct evidence for the generalized Pauli principle. Independent probes of other thermodynamic quantities including pressure and the Tan contact further validate this framework. Our results establish a versatile platform for engineering anyonic exclusion statistics and open the door to thermodynamic applications of anyons in quantum technologies.

</details>
