### [48] [Elastic Surface Instability as a Topological Phase Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18542)
*Yu-Xin Xie*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，经历极端变形的软材料中的经典弹性表面不稳定性本质上是一种拓扑相变（topological phase transition），而非单纯的力学分岔。通过将李群度规演化（Lie group metric evolution）纳入广义Stroh形式体系，作者将高度非线性的几何受挫映射为代数表面阻抗矩阵，并解析地将半无限超弹性半空间在有限压缩下的系统映射为一维狄拉克哈密顿量（Dirac Hamiltonian），其中宏观机械拉伸充当狄拉克质量的可调旋钮。表面褶皱的萌生标志着从平庸相到非平庸相的拓扑转变，其缠绕数（winding number）出现量子化阶跃，自然产生一个稳健的宏观局域零能边缘态（zero-energy edge state）。这一基本联系将宏观对称性破缺与拓扑范式统一起来，为可编程智能软物质开辟了新理论路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上将软材料在极端变形下的宏观不稳定性视为纯结构或机械失效；本文旨在跨越宏观有限应变固体力学与量子类拓扑物理这两个看似无关的研究前沿，探寻不同物理系统中的普适原理。

Method: 将李群度规演化引入广义Stroh形式体系，将高度非线性的几何受挫映射为代数表面阻抗矩阵 $\mathbf{H}$；对于有限压缩下的半无限超弹性半空间，解析地将系统映射为一维狄拉克哈密顿量，使宏观机械拉伸成为狄拉克质量的可调旋钮。

Result: 表面褶皱的萌生标志着从平庸相到非平庸相的拓扑转变，缠绕数出现量子化阶跃，并自然产生稳健的宏观局域零能边缘态。

Conclusion: 经典的弹性表面不稳定性本质上是一种拓扑相变，而非单纯的机械分岔；这一基本联系将宏观对称性破缺与拓扑范式统一起来，为可编程智能软物质（programmable smart soft matter）开辟了新的理论路径。

Abstract: The macroscopic instability of soft materials undergoing extreme deformations is traditionally viewed as a pure structural or mechanical failure. Driven by the quest to uncover universal principles across disparate physical systems, we bridge two vibrant yet seemingly disconnected research frontiers: macroscopic finite-strain solid mechanics and quantum-like topological physics. Here, we demonstrate that the classical elastic surface instability of a deformed hyperelastic manifold is not merely a mechanical bifurcation, but fundamentally a topological phase transition. By incorporating Lie group metric evolution into a generalized Stroh formalism, we map the highly nonlinear geometric frustration onto an algebraic surface impedance matrix $\mathbf{H}$. For a semi-infinite hyperelastic half-space under finite compression, we analytically map the system to a one-dimensional Dirac Hamiltonian, where the macroscopic mechanical stretch acts as a tunable knob for the Dirac mass. We reveal that the onset of surface wrinkles marks a topological transition from a trivial to a non-trivial phase characterized by a quantized step in the winding number, naturally giving rise to a robust, macroscopically localized zero-energy edge state. This fundamental linkage unifies macroscopic symmetry breaking with the topological paradigm, opening a new theoretical pathway for programmable smart soft matter.

</details>


### [49] [Non-Perturbative Closure of the 3D $φ^4$ Field Theory via Operator-Valued Stroh Formalism and Barnett-Lothe Invariants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18635)
*Yu-Xin Xie*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对三维 φ⁴ 标量场理论在临界点附近的严格非微扰闭合框架，通过辛对称性（symplectic symmetry）导出 bootstrap 主积分方程，得到非微扰反常维度 η≈0.0363，并在二维与四维极限下分别退化为 Onsager 精确解和 Gaussian 平凡性结果；此外还揭示了统计状态方程与软物质后屈曲分岔之间的全息对偶关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，三维 φ⁴ 标量场理论在临界点附近依赖微扰费曼图展开（perturbative Feynman diagrammatic expansion），该方法存在固有限制，无法严格处理强耦合区域。本文旨在建立一种严格的非微扰框架，以绕过这些限制并提供理论上的精确闭合解。

Method: 通过沿空间轴对三维欧几里得空间进行切片（slicing），将精确 dressed 理论映射到由无限维辛李代数 $\mathfrak{sp}(\infty)$ 支配的矩阵算子演化。将经典 Stroh 形式论（Stroh formalism）和 Barnett-Lothe 积分不变量从各向异性弹性力学推广到量子场希尔伯特空间，证明 dressed 算子值 Barnett-Lothe 张量精确满足代数恒等式 $\hat{\mathbf{S}}^2 + \hat{\mathbf{H}}\hat{\mathbf{L}} = -\hat{\mathbf{I}}$。进而将该辛不变性与 Källén-Lehmann 谱表示和 Schwinger-Dyson 方程耦合，构建了“辛 Bootstrap”（Symplectic Bootstrap）主谱积分方程。

Result: 该框架在二维极限下自然退化为 Onsager 精确解（η=1/4），在四维极限下退化为 Gaussian 平凡性（Gaussian triviality）极限（η=0）。在强耦合共形不动点（conformal fixed point）下求解超越 bootstrap 方程，得到非微扰反常维度 η≈0.0363，与当前最先进的共形 bootstrap 数值极限一致。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个严格的非微扰闭合框架，成功克服了微扰方法的局限性，产出了与现有最先进数值结果高度吻合的反常维度值。此外，论文还讨论了统计状态方程与波动软物质（fluctuating soft matters）的后屈曲分岔（post-buckling bifurcation）之间的全息对偶（holographic duality），暗示该方法在软物质物理中具有潜在的应用价值。

Abstract: We establish a rigorous non-perturbative closure framework for the three-dimensional (3D) $φ^4$ scalar field theory near criticality, bypassing the long-standing limitations of perturbative Feynman diagrammatic expansions. By slicing the 3D Euclidean space along a spatial axis, the exact dressed theory is mapped onto a matrix operator evolution governed by the infinite-dimensional symplectic Lie algebra $\mathfrak{sp}(\infty)$. We generalize the classical Stroh formalism and Barnett-Lothe integral invariants from anisotropic elasticity to the quantum field Hilbert space. Crucially, we prove that the dressed operator-valued Barnett-Lothe tensors satisfy the algebraic identity $\hat{\mathbf{S}}^2 + \hat{\mathbf{H}}\hat{\mathbf{L}} = -\hat{\mathbf{I}}$ exactly and non-perturbatively, regardless of the coupling strength. By coupling this symplectic invariance with the Källén-Lehmann spectral representation and the Schwinger-Dyson equations, a novel "Symplectic Bootstrap" master spectral integral equation is formulated. The framework exhibits exact dimensional reduction, naturally degenerating to the Onsager exact solution ($η= 1/4$) in 2D and the Gaussian triviality limit ($η= 0$) in 4D. Solving the transcendental bootstrap equation under the strong-coupling conformal fixed point yields the non-perturbative anomalous dimension $η\approx 0.0363$, matching the state-of-the-art conformal bootstrap numerical limits. Finally, a profound holographic duality between the statistical state equations and the post-buckling bifurcation of fluctuating soft matters is discussed.

</details>


### [50] [Self-averaging of replica overlaps in the random field Edwards-Anderson model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18752)
*C. Itoi,Y. Sakamoto*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在任意维度的Edwards-Anderson（EA）模型中，副本重叠（replica overlap）在耦合常数空间几乎处处具有自平均性（self-averaging），并展示了该模型与平均场自旋玻璃模型的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋玻璃（spin glass）模型中副本重叠的自平均性是一个基础性问题，关系到EA序参量（order parameter）的合理性以及平均场理论与有限维模型之间的差异。

Method: 将EA序参量表示为自由能密度（free energy density）对随机场强度（random field strength）的导数，并利用Tasaki关联不等式（Tasaki's correlation inequality）将副本重叠平方的期望限制于EA序参量的平方。

Result: 证明了在无限体积极限（infinite-volume limit）下副本重叠的方差（variance）为零；在具有高斯交换相互作用（Gaussian exchange interaction）且无随机场的EA模型中，副本键重叠（replica bond overlap）的自平均性也得到了证明。

Conclusion: 短程（short-range）自旋玻璃模型的行为与具有副本对称性破缺（RSB, replica symmetry breaking）相的平均场自旋玻璃模型不同。

Abstract: The self-averaging of the replica overlap is proven in the Edwards-Anderson (EA) model under random field almost everywhere in the coupling constant space in any dimension. The EA order parameter is represented in terms of the derivative of the free energy density with respect to the random field strength, regardless of boundary conditions. Tasaki's correlation inequality for finite-dimensional spin glass models shows that the expectation of the squared replica overlap is bounded by the squared EA order parameter. These simple evaluations enable us to prove that the variance of the replica overlap vanishes in the infinite-volume limit. The self-averaging of the replica bond overlap is proven also in the EA model with Gaussian exchange interaction without random field. Short-range spin glass models have been shown to behave differently from mean-field spin glass models with RSB phase.

</details>


### [51] [A finite element-based eigenvalue analysis for predicting thermal runaway in Li-ion battery packs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18983)
*Shailendra Rahi,Vinay Dhakal,Ankur Jain,Manish Agrawal*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个基于有限元（finite element）的广义特征值（generalized eigenvalue）框架，通过求解最小特征值的符号来判断系统是否会发生热失控（thermal runaway），无需进行耗时的瞬态分析，并在圆柱形锂离子电池及电池组上验证了其准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热失控是电池系统和其他热活性设备中的关键安全问题，现有方法需要大量瞬态计算，缺乏一种高效、适用于复杂几何构型的热稳定性（thermal stability）判据。

Method: 建立含温度依赖内热源的瞬态热传导（transient heat conduction）有限元模型，将问题转化为广义特征值问题，以最小特征值的正负作为热失控发生的直接判据，从而避免瞬态分析。

Result: 通过与圆柱形锂离子电池及其电池组的解析解对比验证，结果高度吻合；基于该模型分析了材料属性、边界条件、几何参数和空间变化热源对稳定极限的影响。

Conclusion: 该框架在解析方法不可行的复杂几何中依然有效，为电池系统的热设计与安全评估提供了一种系统化且计算高效的工具。

Abstract: Thermal runaway remains a critical safety concern in battery systems and other thermally active devices, necessitating reliable methods for predicting the conditions under which thermal runaway may occur. In this work, we develop a finite element framework for assessing thermal stability in systems undergoing transient heat conduction with temperature-dependent internal heat generation. The formulation leads naturally to a generalized eigenvalue problem, wherein the sign of the smallest eigenvalue provides a direct criterion for determining the onset of thermal runaway. This approach enables direct prediction of thermal runaway thresholds in geometrically complicated problems without requiring computationally expensive transient analysis. The proposed methodology is validated through comparison with analytical solutions for a cylindrical Li-ion cell, as well as with a pack of cylindrical cells, demonstrating excellent agreement in both cases. Based on this model, the influence of material properties, boundary conditions, geometric parameters, and spatially varying heat generation on stability limits is examined. A key advantage of this formulation is its effectiveness even for complex geometries where analytical methods become impractical. By providing a systematic and computationally efficient means to identify stability thresholds, the present work offers a practical tool for the thermal design and safety assessment of battery systems.

</details>

*Fabio Bagarello,Gloria Liarda*

Method: 采用非自伴哈密顿量构造系统的类海森堡动力学方程，将政党联盟（C）及其支持者（Sc）作为系统组成部分。在一般性引入后，提出三个具体模型并分析Sc∪C全系统的动力学行为，同时详细讨论作者先前提出的平衡哈密顿量（balanced Hamiltonian）在运动积分（integrals of motion）关联下的作用。

Conclusion: 非自伴哈密顿量与类海森堡动力学框架能够有效建模政治系统中支持者观点受执政联盟表现影响的动态过程，平衡哈密顿量在该框架中具有重要的结构意义。

Abstract: We discuss here how non self-adjoint Hamiltonians, and their related Heisenberg-like dynamics, can be used to model a political system consisting in a coalition $\C$ of different parties (forming a government) and by their (original) supporters $\Sc$. Our aim is to model how the opinion of these supporters changes depending on the efficiency, competence and coherence of the coalition $\C$, as these are perceived by $\Sc$ during their action while governing. After a rather general introduction we propose three specific models, and we describe and comment the dynamical behaviour of the { full} system, $\Sc\cup\C$. The role of the so-called {\em balanced Hamiltonians}, recently introduced by the authors in connection with integrals of motion, is discussed in details.

### [53] [Bulk-boundary correspondence of (1+1)D symmetric gapped phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19137)
*Yizhou Ma,Gen Yue,Tian Lan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个算子代数（operator-algebraic）框架，用于描述具有范畴对称性（categorical symmetry）的一维能隙相（gapped phases）中的边界条件与体-边界对应关系（bulk-boundary correspondence），利用幺半范畴（fusion category）、模范畴（module category）及Q-系统（Q-system）等代数结构，严格证明了边界条件的分类定理，并给出了边界对称拓扑场论（symmetry topological field theory）的微观表述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在一维能隙系统中，边界条件及其与体相（bulk phase）的对应关系缺乏统一的算子代数描述。本文旨在从代数角度严格建立该框架，并实现边界条件的完整分类。

Method: 利用幺半范畴𝒞、右𝒞-模范畴ℳ、指定体相的Q-系统Q∈𝒞以及指定边界的右Q-模K∈ℳ_Q（视为ℳ_Q^{op}的对象），在热力学极限下构造半无限融合自旋链（half-infinite fusion spin chain）和对易投影子边界哈密顿量（commuting-projector boundary Hamiltonian）。通过DHR双模（DHR bimodules）给出边界对称拓扑场论的微观表述。

Result: 证明这些哈密顿量具有唯一基态，且由此导出的实现函子（realization functor）ℳ_Q^{op}→BCond是等价（equivalence），从而边界条件由ℳ_Q的简单对象分类，一般边界条件由其有限直和给出。边界DHR范畴（boundary DHR category）与(𝒞_ℳ^∨)^{rev}是幺半等价的（monoidally equivalent），体DHR范畴在边界DHR范畴上的典范作用与Z_1(𝒞^{rev})的范畴作用一致。

Conclusion: 本文给出了一个一维体-边界对应关系：描述体的丰富幺半范畴（enriched monoidal category）是描述边界的丰富范畴（enriched category）的丰富中心（enriched center）。该工作为具有范畴对称性的一维系统提供了严格的代数分类框架。

Abstract: We develop an operator-algebraic framework for boundary conditions and bulk-boundary correspondence in one-dimensional gapped phases with categorical symmetry. Working directly in the thermodynamic limit, we construct half-infinite fusion spin chains and commuting-projector boundary Hamiltonians from a unitary fusion category $\mathcal{C}$, an indecomposable semisimple right $\mathcal{C}$-module category $\mathcal{M}$, a Q-system $Q\in\mathcal{C}$ specifying the bulk phase, and a right $Q$-module $K\in\mathcal{M}_{Q}$, regarded as an object of $\mathcal{M}_{Q}^{\mathrm{op}}$, specifying the boundary. We prove that these Hamiltonians have unique ground states and that the resulting realization functor $\mathcal{M}_{Q}^{\mathrm{op}}\to\mathrm{BCond}$ is an equivalence, so simple boundary conditions are classified by simple objects of $\mathcal{M}_{Q}$ and general boundary conditions by their finite direct sums. We also give a microscopic formulation of the boundary symmetry topological field theory using DHR bimodules of the boundary quasi-local algebra. For a half-infinite fusion spin chain, the boundary DHR category is monoidally equivalent to $(\mathcal{C}_{\mathcal{M}}^{\vee})^{\mathrm{rev}}$, and the canonical action of the bulk DHR category on it agrees with the categorical action of $Z_1(\mathcal{C}^{\mathrm{rev}})$. Finally, we identify the action of the boundary DHR category on boundary conditions with the categorical action of $(\mathcal{C}_{\mathcal{M}}^{\vee})^{\mathrm{rev}}$ on $\mathcal{M}_{Q}^{\mathrm{op}}$. This yields a one-dimensional bulk-boundary correspondence: the enriched monoidal category describing the bulk is the enriched center of the enriched category describing the boundary.

</details>


### [54] [Topology of Bloch Bands from Cauchy Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19141)
*Didier Felbacq,Emmanuel Rousseau*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文为反演对称一维周期介质中的拓扑 formalism 提供了几何解释，通过将阻抗类函数的极点-零点模式与投影 Cauchy 数据空间上的反演对称作用、Bloch 本征向量的实线丛（Real eigenline bundle）以及单值符号（monodromy sign）联系起来，建立了极点-零 formalism、Berry–Zak 相位、实丛（Real bundles）和局部系数系统（local coefficient systems）之间的几何关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期工作通过 Bloch 波关联的阻抗类函数的极点-零点模式（pole-zero pattern）表征反演对称一维周期介质的拓扑，重构了 Berry–Zak 不变量（Berry–Zak invariant）并为拓扑界面态提供了判据。本研究旨在为这一 formalism 提供几何解释。

Method: 通过分析反演对称性在 Cauchy 数据的投影空间（projectivized space of Cauchy data）上的作用，自然导出极点与零点，并将 Dirichlet 态和 Neumann 态识别为 Riemann 球面上诱导 $\mathbb Z_2$ 作用的两个不动点。Bloch 本征向量被构造在 Brillouin 圆的通用覆盖（universal covering）上，关联的实本征线丛（Real eigenline bundle）的拓扑由覆盖变换群（deck transformation group）对提升本征向量的作用编码，该作用由单值符号 $\rho\in\{\pm1\}$ 描述。

Result: 该单值符号定义了一个 Brillouin 圆上的自然秩一局部系数系统（rank-one local system）。对应的实线丛（Real line bundle）由第一 Stiefel–Whitney 类（first Stiefel–Whitney class）分类，该示性类与关联的 $\mathbb Z_2$ 极点-零不变量（pole-zero invariant）一致。

Conclusion: 建立了极点-零 formalism、Berry–Zak 相位、实丛（Real bundles）和局部系数系统（local coefficient systems）之间的几何联系。

Abstract: In a previous work, the topology of inversion-symmetric one-dimensional periodic media was characterized through the pole-zero pattern of an impedance-like function associated with Bloch waves. This construction reproduces the Berry--Zak invariant and provides a criterion for topological interface states.
  In the present work, we give a geometric interpretation of this formalism. We show that poles and zeros arise naturally from the action of inversion symmetry on the projectivized space of Cauchy data. The corresponding Dirichlet and Neumann states are identified with the two fixed points of the induced $\mathbb Z_2$ action on the Riemann sphere.
  The key observation is that Bloch eigenvectors are naturally constructed on the universal covering of the Brillouin circle. The topology of the associated Real eigenline bundle is encoded in the action of the deck transformation group on lifted eigenvectors. This action is described by a monodromy sign $ρ\in\{\pm1\}$, determined by the inversion representations carried by the band at the fixed points of the Brillouin zone.
  We show that this monodromy defines a natural rank-one local system over the Brillouin circle. The corresponding Real line bundle is classified by its first Stiefel--Whitney class, which coincides with the associated $\mathbb Z_2$ pole-zero invariant. This establishes a geometric connection between the pole-zero formalism, Berry--Zak phases, Real bundles and local coefficient systems.

</details>

### [55] [A Note on the Matched Asymptotic Structure of Weak Shock Reflection at Nearly Glancing Incidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18618)
*Justin Kin Jun Hew*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究了弱激波近乎掠入射刚性壁面的反射问题，在弱激波强度与掠射角联合极限下，通过非定常跨声速小扰动（UTSD）方程控制了内部反射区域，推导了关键参数与脱体阈值，并给出了数值基准验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解析弱激波近乎掠入射刚性壁面时，在联合极限（weak shock strength and nearly glancing incidence）下的反射结构，并确定Guderley-Mach反射的物理阈值。

Method: 采用区分标度（distinguished scaling）M=1+λα²，引入单一规范参数a；导出自相似UTSD约化、声速抛物线（sonic parabola）、UTSD激波极线（shock polar）及其正则反射三次方程；通过局部线性化与形式伴随可解性条件定义一阶修正H(a;γ)；使用时间推进求解器对完整首阶规范UTSD系统进行数值求解。

Result: 脱体值a_d=√2映射到物理标度阈值λ_d=1/8，当λ>1/8时出现Guderley-Mach反射；规范UTSD轨迹函数g(a)通过马赫数强度标度给出物理轨迹角χ_phys；数值求解器在保留横向压缩（u>1）后，计算的u=0.5等值线通过(ξ,η)=(1.007,0.514)，与发表值(1.008,0.514)高度吻合。

Conclusion: 极限内参数a_0=1/(2√λ)与比热比γ无关，表明该反射问题由单一规范参数a完全控制；数值基准验证了UTSD系统的有效性，并为后续完整修正曲线的计算提供了框架。

Abstract: We study the reflection of a weak planar shock from a rigid wall in the joint limit of weak shock strength and nearly glancing incidence. In the distinguished scaling (M=1+λα^2), where (M) is the incident-shock Mach number and (α) is the glancing angle, the inner reflection region is governed by the unsteady transonic small-disturbance (UTSD) equation. The corresponding canonical shock-reflection problem is controlled by the single parameter[a=\fracα{\sqrt{2(M^2-1)}}=\frac{1}{2\sqrtλ}+O(α^2),]so the limiting inner parameter (a_0=1/(2\sqrtλ)) is independent of (γ). Consequently, the detachment value (a_d=\sqrt2) maps to the physical scaling threshold (λ_d=1/8), with Guderley--Mach reflection for (λ>1/8). The physical trajectory angle is obtained from the canonical UTSD trajectory function (g(a)) by the Mach-number strength scale[χ_{\rm phys}\sqrt{2(M^2-1)},g(a)+O(M^2-1) 2\sqrtλ,α,g(a_0)+O(α^3).]We derive the self-similar UTSD reduction, the sonic parabola, the UTSD shock polar and its regular-reflection cubic, recovering (a_d=\sqrt2) directly. We also give the local linearisation and formal adjoint solvability condition defining the first correction (H(a;γ)), without claiming a computed correction curve. Finally, a time-marching solver for the full leading-order canonical UTSD system is benchmarked against the Hunter--Tesdall (a_0=0.5) triple point: once transverse compression (u>1) behind the Mach stem is retained, the computed (u=0.5) contour passes through ((ξ,η)=(1.007,0.514)), compared with the published ((1.008,0.514)).

</details>

### [56] [ParticleTransformer is all you need for reconstructing hadronic tau leptons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18460)
*Nalong-Norman Seeba,Laurits Tani,Torben Lange,Joosep Pata*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个针对FCC-ee实验的全机器学习（fully machine learned）强子性tau轻子重建方法，将重建任务分解为tau鉴别、衰变模式分类、电荷重建和四动量回归等多个互补子任务。基于CLD探测器设置的完整模拟数据，任务专用模型与统一多任务模型均实现了极低的tau误鉴别率（千分之一量级）、高达0.95的衰变模式分类F1分数以及亚千分之一的电荷误判率，在运动学重建上达到千分之一的角分辨率和百分级的可见横动量分辨率，性能显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FCC-ee的TeraZ计划将产生海量Z → ττ事例，需要高精度的强子性tau轻子重建。由于未探测中微子的存在和强子性tau衰变拓扑的多样性，传统启发式重建算法面临严峻挑战，亟需更鲁棒、更精确的重建方法。

Method: 将强子性tau重建形式化为一组互补学习任务，包括tau鉴别（tau identification）、衰变模式分类（decay mode classification）、电荷重建（charge reconstruction）和全四动量回归（full four-momentum regression）。采用CLD探测器设置下的全模拟电子-正电子对撞样本，对比任务专用模型（task-specific models）与统一多任务模型（unified multi-task model）的性能。

Result: 两种模型均实现了千分之一量级（per-mille-level）的tau误鉴别率和高信号效率；主导衰变通道的F1分数达0.95；电荷误判率低于千分之一（sub-per-mille），相较传统喷注电荷估计器（jet-charge estimator）提升多达两个数量级；运动学重建达到千分之一的角分辨率和百分级（percent-level）的可见横动量分辨率，优于重建级喷注观测量（reconstruction-level jet observables）。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于机器学习的方法为FCC-ee的强子性tau重建提供了一种高性能实用方案，能够在鉴别、电荷区分、衰变模式分析和全运动学重建等多个维度实现卓越表现。

Abstract: The large number of $Z \rightarrow ττ$ events expected during the TeraZ program at FCC-ee will allow for precision measurements and searches for physics beyond the Standard Model, requiring accurate reconstruction of hadronically decaying tau leptons. This reconstruction is particularly challenging due to the presence of undetected neutrinos and the diverse topology of hadronic tau decays, making the design of robust heuristic reconstruction algorithms challenging. In this work, we present the first fully machine learned hadronic tau reconstruction approach tuned for FCC-ee studies. The reconstruction is formulated as a set of complementary tasks, including tau identification, decay mode classification, charge reconstruction, and full four-momentum regression. The algorithms are evaluated on fully simulated electron--positron collision samples with realistic detector effects using the CLD detector setup. We compare dedicated task-specific models with a unified multi-task model and quantify their performance in a granular manner across all reconstruction tasks. Both approaches achieve per-mille-level tau mis-identification rates at high signal efficiency, decay mode classification F1 scores of up to 0.95 for the dominant channels, and sub-per-mille charge mis-identification rates, outperforming a conventional jet-charge estimator by up to two orders of magnitude. For the full kinematic reconstruction, the models achieve per-mille-level angular resolution and percent-level visible transverse momentum resolution, exceeding the performance of reconstruction-level jet observables. The resulting models provide a realistic high-performance solution for hadronic tau reconstruction at FCC-ee, offering identification, charge discrimination, decay mode analysis and full kinematic reconstruction.

### [57] [Electromagnetic Shower Reconstruction and Identification in FASER's Emulsion Detector for LHC Forward Neutrino Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18517)
*FASER Collaboration,Roshan Mammen Abraham,Xiaocong Ai,Saul Alonso Monsalve,John Anders,Emma Kate Anderson,Akitaka Ariga,Tomoko Ariga,Jeremy Atkinson,Florian U. Bernlochner,Jianming Bian,Tobias Boeckh,Eliot Bornand,Jamie Boyd,Lydia Brenner,Angela Burger,Franck Cadoux,Roberto Cardella,David W. Casper,Charlotte Cavanagh,Shiyang Chen,Xin Chen,Xing Cheng,Dhruv Chouhan,Andrea Coccaro,Fabio Cufino,Stephane Débieux,Ansh Desai,Sergey Dmitrievsky,Radu Dobre,Monica D'Onofrio,Sinead Eley,Yannick Favre,Jonathan L. Feng,Carlo Alberto Fenoglio,Didier Ferrere,Max Fieg,Wissal Filali,Elena Firu,Haruhi Fujimori,Edward Galantay,Stephen Gibson,Sergio Gonzalez-Sevilla,Yuri Gornushkin,Yotam Granov,Jinjing Gu,Carl Gwilliam,Elie Hammou,Daiki Hayakawa,Michael Holzbock,Shih-Chieh Hsu,Zhen Hu,Giuseppe Iacobucci,Tomohiro Inada,Luca Iodice,Sune Jakobsen,Cesar Jesus-Valls,Arash Jofrehei,Hans Joos,Enrique Kajomovitz,Alex Keyken,Felix Kling,Daniela Köck,Pantelis Kontaxakis,Jelle Koorn,Umut Kose,Peter Krack,Susanne Kuehn,Thanushan Kugathasan,Sebastian Laudage,Lorne Levinson,Botao Li,Jiaxi Liu,Jinfeng Liu,Yi Liu,Margaret S. Lutz,Joern Mahlstedt,Toni Mäkelä,Yasuhiro Maruya,Anna Mascellani,Lawson McCoy,Josh McFayden,Andrea Pizarro Medina,Hiroaki Menjo,Théo Moretti,Toshiyuki Nakano,Laurie Nevay,Yuma Ohara,Ken Ohashi,Hidetoshi Otono,Lorenzo Paolozzi,Annabelle Parry,Pawan Pawan,Brian Petersen,Titi Preda,Markus Prim,Junkai Qin,Michaela Queitsch-Maitland,Juan Rojo,Hiroki Rokujo,André Rubbia,Osamu Sato,Paola Scampoli,Kristof Schmieden,Matthias Schott,Cristiano Sebastiani,Anna Sfyrla,Davide Sgalaberna,Mansoora Shamim,Yosuke Takubo,Kakeru Tanaka,Noshin Tarannum,Simon Thor,Eric Torrence,Serhan Tufanli,Oscar Ivan Valdes Martinez,Svetlana Vasina,Emanuele Villa,Benedikt Vormwald,Chi Wang,Yuxiao Wang,Eli Welch,Aaron White,Monika Wielers,Benjamin James Wilson,Zhongyi Wu,Yue Xu,Heng Yang,Lekai Yao,Daichi Yoshikawa,Stefano Zambito,Shunliang Zhang,Yuxuan Zhang,Xingyu Zhao,Zijian Zhao*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于CERN SPS H4束流线100 GeV和200 GeV电子测试束数据，提出了FASERnu乳胶探测器中电磁簇射重建与识别方法。采用基于聚类的算法、多级识别链（含BDT分类器），在模拟样本中达到58.9%–70.8%的总重建与识别效率，能量重建相对偏差在±0.8%以内，分辨率约22%–25%。该方法为LHC上FASERnu探测器的电子中微子识别提供了验证框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为FASERnu乳胶探测器开发并验证一套针对电磁簇射（electromagnetic shower）的重建与识别方法，以支撑LHC上电子中微子（electron neutrino）的识别任务。

Method: 采用基于聚类的算法（clustering-based algorithm）确定簇射轴（shower axes），无需依赖能量调优。识别链包含三层：径迹预选（track pre-selection）、基于截断的选择（cut-based selection）以及BDT分类器（boosted decision tree classifier）。能量重建使用总重建段数（total number of reconstructed segments）作为量能估算量（calorimetric estimator）。

Result: 多级识别链在100 GeV和200 GeV下分别实现99.99%和99.94%的联合背景抑制率（combined background rejection rate）。模拟样本评估的总重建与识别效率为58.9%（100 GeV）和70.8%（200 GeV）。能量重建相对偏差为+0.6%（100 GeV）和-0.8%（200 GeV），分辨率为25.4%和22.6%。系统不确定度主要由乳胶膜探测效率（emulsion film detection efficiency）变化主导，贡献分别为(+10.9%/-8.2%)和(+10.3%/-6.9%)。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法为FASERnu探测器在LHC上的电子中微子识别提供了经过测试束数据验证的框架。

Abstract: We present methods for electromagnetic shower reconstruction and identification in the FASERnu emulsion detector using 100 GeV and 200 GeV electron test-beam data from the CERN SPS H4 beamline. The reconstruction employs a clustering-based algorithm without energy-dependent tuning to determine shower axes. A multi-level identification chain comprising track pre-selection, a cut-based selection, and a BDT classifier achieves combined background rejection rates of 99.99% (100 GeV) and 99.94% (200 GeV). The method reaches total reconstruction and identification efficiencies of 58.9% (100 GeV) and 70.8% (200 GeV) evaluated from simulated samples. Energy reconstruction using the total number of reconstructed segments as the calorimetric estimator yields relative biases of +0.6% (100 GeV) and -0.8% (200 GeV), with resolutions of 25.4% and 22.6%, respectively. Systematic uncertainties on the energy reconstruction are dominated by variations in emulsion film detection efficiency, contributing (+10.9%/-8.2%) at 100 GeV and (+10.3%/-6.9%) at 200 GeV. The methodology provides a validated framework for electron neutrino identification with the FASERnu detector at the LHC.

</details>


### [58] [Gluon dominance model and multiparticle production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18638)
*E. S. Kokoulina,A. Ya. Kutov,V. A. Nikitin,V. N. Riadovikov,R. G. Shulyakovsky*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出胶子主导模型（gluon dominance model），将多粒子产生过程分为两个阶段：QCD微扰区中的夸克-胶子级联（Markov分支过程）和强子化现象学方案。模型与广泛能量范围内的实验数据吻合良好，支持价夸克保留在领头粒子中、胶子是次级强子来源的观点。首次给出了50 GeV质子相互作用高多重数区域中性π介子实验分布的描述，表明该区域主要贡献来自胶子裂变（gluon fission）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高能轻子与强子相互作用（包括湮灭过程和重夸克偶素衰变）中，需要对次级粒子的多粒子产生过程建立统一的描述框架。现有模型在解释强子化机制方面仍存在不足，特别是在区分轻子相互作用中的碎裂机制（fragmentation mechanism）与强子相互作用中的复合机制（recombination mechanism）方面。

Method: 模型将多粒子过程分为两个阶段：第一阶段将夸克-胶子级联描述为微扰QCD（perturbation QCD）区域中的Markov分支过程（Markov branching process）；第二阶段采用基于实验现象的唯象学方案来描述强子化（hadronization），即夸克与胶子转变为可观测强子的过程。

Result: 模型在整个宽能量区域内与实验数据吻合良好。定量估计证实轻子相互作用中强子化遵循碎裂机制，而强子相互作用中则遵循复合机制。首次给出了50 GeV质子束相互作用中高多重数区域的中性π介子实验分布描述，证明该区域的主要贡献来自胶子裂变。

Conclusion: 在强子相互作用中，价夸克（valence quarks）保留在领头粒子中，胶子（gluons）则是次级强子的来源。这些结果对未来实验的规划具有参考价值。

Abstract: The gluon dominance model describes multiparticle production of secondary particles at high energies in lepton and hadron interactions, including annihilation processes and heavy quarkonium decays. According to this model, the multiparticle process is divided into two stages. The first stage describes the development of a quark-gluon cascade as a Markov branching process in the region of perturbation QCD. For the second stage, the transformation of quarks and gluons into observable hadrons (hadronization), a phenomenological scheme is proposed. It is universal and based on an experiment. The gluon dominance model demonstrates good agreement with data over a wide energy region. It testifies that in hadron interactions valence quarks remain in the leading particles, and gluons are the sources of secondary hadrons. Quantitative estimates of the model parameters confirm the fragmentation mechanism of hadronization in leptonic interactions and the recombination mechanism in hadronic ones. The model description of the experimental distributions on the number of neutral pions in proton interactions at 50 GeV beams in the high multiplicity region are presented for the first time. It is shown that the main contribution to this region is made by gluon fission. These results can be useful in planning of future experiments.

</details>


### [59] [QCD studies and precision physics at the LHeC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19064)
*Francesco Giuli*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文总结了LHeC（大型强子电子对撞机）桥接项目研究中与QCD和部分子分布函数（PDF）相关的内容。LHeC通过将高电流能量回收直线加速器接入HL-LHC，实现TeV能级的电子-质子碰撞，其高亮度、大运动学覆盖范围可在一个实验中统一确定所有质子PDF，大幅降低胶子、价夸克、奇异夸克和重味夸克分布的不确定性，并对强耦合常数和弱混合角提供竞争性测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前质子部分子分布函数（PDF）的测定通常依赖多个实验数据的组合，导致不同部分子间的系统性误差难以统一控制。LHeC能够通过单一实验对全部分子进行自洽测量，避免多源数据合并带来的不确定性。

Method: LHeC设计利用高电流能量回收直线加速器（Energy Recovery Linac）与HL-LHC对接，产生TeV能级的电子-质子碰撞。通过高亮度、大Bjorken x和Q^2运动学杠杆臂以及干净的带电流和中性流深度非弹性散射（deep-inelastic scattering）测量，实现对质子PDF的统一确定。

Result: LHeC能显著降低胶子（gluon）、价夸克（valence）、奇异夸克（strange）和重味夸克（heavy-flavour）分布的不确定性；提供对微扰QCD和小x QCD的严格检验；提高HL-LHC及未来强子对撞机中进入精确测量与发现测量的部分子亮度（parton luminosities）；同时给出强耦合常数（strong coupling）和弱混合角（weak mixing angle）的竞争性及互补性测定，包括对其跑动（running）效应的测量。

Conclusion: LHeC是一个在QCD和PDF测量方面极具潜力的未来对撞机方案，其单一实验自洽测定全部分子分布的能力将显著提升标准模型参数的精度，并为更高能标的精确测量与发现提供基础。

Abstract: The Large Hadron electron Collider (LHeC) would add a high-current Energy Recovery Linac to the HL-LHC, delivering electron-proton collisions at centre-of-mass energies around the TeV scale. This contribution summarises the QCD and parton-distribution-function (PDF) aspects of the recent LHeC bridge-project study. The combination of high luminosity, a very large lever arm in Bjorken $x$ and $Q^2$, and clean neutral- and charged-current deep-inelastic scattering measurements would enable a coherent determination of all proton PDFs in a single experiment. The resulting constraints would substantially reduce uncertainties in the gluon, valence, strange and heavy-flavour distributions, provide stringent tests of perturbative and small-$x$ QCD, and improve the parton luminosities that enter precision and discovery measurements at the HL-LHC and at future hadron colliders. The same programme gives competitive and complementary determinations of the strong coupling and weak mixing angle, including measurements of its running over a wide range of scales.

</details>


### [60] [High-$p_{\rm T}$ physics and jet production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19068)
*Francesco Giuli*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该文综述了DIS2026会议上关于喷注产生（jet production）的最新测量结果，涵盖单喷注（inclusive-jet）、双喷注（dijet）及喷注多重数（jet-multiplicity）观测量，重点讨论了实验精度、次次领头阶（NNLO）预言、非微扰与电弱修正以及关联系统误差处理，并展示了喷注物理在强耦合常数提取和部分子分布函数（PDF）约束方面的进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 喷注产生是强子对撞机中占主导的高横动量（high-$p_{\rm T}$）过程，为微扰量子色动力学（pQCD）、部分子分布函数（PDF）和强耦合常数测定提供了核心检验平台，因此需要系统综述最新实验进展及其对理论预言的约束能力。

Method: 综述基于CMS和ATLAS合作组对单喷注、双喷注及喷注多重数可观测量进行的实验测量，结合次次领头阶（NNLO）理论预言、非微扰修正和电弱修正，并系统处理关联系统误差（correlated systematic uncertainties）。

Result: CMS和ATLAS的单喷注测量约束了高Bjorken $x$区域的胶子分布（gluon distribution），并提取出与世界平均值兼容的强耦合常数$α_s(m_Z)$；双喷注测量通过不变质量、快度间隔和纵向boost提供互补灵敏度；喷注多重数比值有效降低了实验和PDF不确定性，直接探测额外QCD辐射。

Conclusion: 喷注能量校准的最新进展，结合RHIC、ALICE和CMS在喷注子结构（jet substructure）和重夸克辐射方面的结果，展现了当前高$p_{\rm T}$喷注物理的广泛覆盖面及其对Run 3和未来全局PDF分析的重要性。

Abstract: Jet production is the dominant high-$p_{\rm T}$ process at hadron colliders and provides a central testing ground for perturbative QCD, parton distribution functions and determinations of the strong coupling. This contribution summarises recent measurements of inclusive-jet, dijet and jet-multiplicity observables presented at DIS2026, with emphasis on the interplay between experimental precision, next-to-next-to-leading-order predictions, non-perturbative and electroweak corrections, and the treatment of correlated systematic uncertainties. Inclusive jet measurements from CMS and ATLAS constrain the gluon distribution at large Bjorken $x$ and enable extractions of $α_s(m_Z)$ compatible with the world average. Dijet measurements provide complementary sensitivity through the dijet invariant mass, rapidity separation and longitudinal boost, while ratios of inclusive jet multiplicities reduce several experimental and PDF uncertainties and directly probe additional QCD radiation. Recent progress in jet-energy calibration, together with new results from RHIC, ALICE and CMS on jet substructure and heavy-quark radiation, illustrates the breadth of current high-$p_{\rm T}$ jet physics and its relevance for Run~3 and future global PDF analyses.

</details>


### [61] [Probing Long-Lived Particle Production in Muon Decays at the SNS with a Highly Capable Hydrocarbon Detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19299)
*M. Andriamirado,A. B. Balantekin,C. D. Bass,O. Benevides Rodrigues,E. P. Bernard,N. S. Bowden,C. D. Bryan,R. Carr,T. Classen,A. J. Conant,N. Craft,G. Deichert,A. Erickson,M. D. Fuller,A. Galindo-Uribarri,S. Ghosh,S. Gokhale,C. Grant,S. Hans,A. B. Hansell,T. E. Haugen,K. M. Heeger,A. Irani,J. Koblanski,C. E. Lane,B. R. Littlejohn,A. Lozano Sanchez,F. Machado,J. Maricic,M. P. Mendenhall,A. M. Meyer,R. Milincic,P. E. Mueller,H. P. Mumm,R. Neilson,J. R. Newby,D. Norcini,N. Patel,C. Roca,R. Rosero,D. Venegas-Vargas,J. Wilhelmi,M. Yeh,X. Zhang,M. Hostert,S. Urrea*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文研究了在橡树岭国家实验室散裂中子源（SNS）部署吨级烃类闪烁体探测器（HC²）探测亚GeV暗物质粒子的可行性，重点关注10-100 MeV轴子类似粒子（axion-like particles）和重中性轻子（heavy neutral leptons）衰变产生的e⁺e⁻末态，结果表明灵敏度可比当前全球极限提升一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SNS是丰沛的缪子（muon）产生源，适合研究缪子静止衰变中产生的暗区（dark sector）粒子。现有对亚GeV暗物质粒子的探测能力有限，需要利用强中子源和高效探测器技术来提升灵敏度。

Method: 研究使用吨级烃类闪烁体探测器HC²（典型代表为PROSPECT和Mobile Antineutrino Demonstrator），利用其对宇宙射线本底（cosmic ray background）的强排斥能力，基于PROSPECT在ORNL的地表宇宙射线数据对标，为SNS多年代部署生成稳健预测。

Result: 结果表明，在10-100 MeV质量范围内，对轴子类似粒子和重中性轻子的灵敏度可比当前全球极限提升一个数量级（order-of-magnitude improvement）。

Conclusion: HC²探测器在SNS部署具有显著的暗物质探测潜力，同时还可实现中微子（neutrino）探测。该方案为未来亚GeV暗区粒子搜索提供了可行的实验路径。

Abstract: The Spallation Neutron Source (SNS) at Oak Ridge National Laboratory (ORNL) is a prolific muon producer, making it an ideal location for studying dark sector particles produced in muon decays at rest. In this paper, we explore sub-GeV dark particle detection possibilities in a tons-scale, highly capable hydrocarbon scintillator ($HC^2$) detector at the SNS. We consider a search for $e^+e^-$ final states produced by decays of long-lived, $O(10-100)$ MeV axion-like particles and heavy neutral leptons. The $HC^2$ technology space, exemplified by the PROSPECT and Mobile Antineutrino Demonstrator detectors, offers strong rejection capabilities for the cosmic ray backgrounds that would normally dominate this search. By benchmarking on-surface cosmic ray signatures with data from PROSPECT at ORNL, we generate robust predictions for a multi-year SNS deployment of a range of $HC^2$ detector implementations. Results indicate the potential for order-of-magnitude improvements in sensitivity to axion-like particles and heavy neutral leptons in the 10-100 MeV mass regime compared to current global limits. We also comment on the neutrino detection possibilities of a $HC^2$ deployment at the SNS.

</details>

### [62] [akaitools: A Python package for parsing and analyzing AkaiKKR electronic structure calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18399)
*Doğuhan Sarıtürk,Raymundo Arróyave*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: akaitools 是一个用于解析 AkaiKKR 程序输出文件的 Python 包，它将非结构化的纯文本输出转换为类型注解（type-annotated）的 Python 对象，支持自洽场结果、态密度（density of states）和 Bloch 谱函数（Bloch spectral function）三种输出类型，并提供绘图、JSON 导出及输入文件生成功能，从而为基于 KKR 格林函数方法的第一性原理（first-principles）计算提供程序化接口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AkaiKKR 是基于 KKR 格林函数方法（Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker Green's function method）的第一性原理电子结构（electronic structure）计算软件，特别适用于通过相干势近似（Coherent Potential Approximation, CPA）处理替代无序合金（substitutionally disordered alloys）。然而，其输出为无结构的纯文本（unstructured plain text），缺乏程序化接口（programmatic interface），导致数据提取完全依赖用户手工操作，阻碍了系统化或高通量（high-throughput）研究的开展。

Method: akaitools 是一个 Python 包，可解析 AkaiKKR 的三种主要输出类型：自洽场（self-consistent field, SCF）结果（包含收敛历史和每个原子的电子与磁性性质）、自旋分辨且轨道投影的态密度（spin-resolved, orbital projected density of states），以及用户定义 k 点路径上的 Bloch 谱函数（Bloch spectral function）。解析结果以不可变数据类（immutable dataclass）形式返回，底层由 NumPy 数组支持。能量量纲同时提供 Rydbergs 和电子伏特（electronvolts）单位，结果可导出为 Pandas DataFrames。内置绘图模块支持 Matplotlib 图形绘制。命令行界面（command-line interface, CLI）提供文件摘要和 JSON 导出功能；程序化输入文件生成器允许从输入准备到输出分析的全流程在 Python 中运行。

Result: akaitools 实现了对 AkaiKKR 非结构化文本输出的结构化解析，覆盖自洽场结果、态密度和 Bloch 谱函数三种数据类型。解析后的对象具有类型注解（type-annotated）、不可变（immutable）且基于 NumPy 数组的特性，支持双能量单位（Rydbergs 与 eV）以及 Pandas DataFrame 导出。包内包含 Matplotlib 绘图模块、命令行接口（CLI）以及程序化输入文件生成器。

Conclusion: akaitools 为 AkaiKKR 提供了完整的程序化接口，弥补了原始软件在数据可编程访问方面的空缺，使得从输入生成到输出分析的全流程可在 Python 中自动化执行，从而显著提升了 KKR-CPA 方法在系统化和高通量研究场景中的可用性。

Abstract: The Korringa-Kohn-Rostoker (KKR) Green's function method is a first-principles electronic structure approach well suited to substitutionally disordered alloys through the Coherent Potential Approximation (CPA). AkaiKKR is a widely used implementation, known for efficient treatment of metallic systems and their magnetic properties. Its output, however, is unstructured plain text with no programmatic interface, leaving data extraction entirely to the user and making systematic or high-throughput studies impractical. akaitools is a Python package that parses AkaiKKR output files into structured, type-annotated Python objects. The package covers three output types: self-consistent field (SCF) results, which capture convergence history and per-atom electronic and magnetic properties; spin-resolved, orbital projected density of states for each CPA component; and Bloch spectral functions on a user-defined k-point path. Results come back as immutable dataclasses backed by NumPy arrays. Energy quantities are available in both Rydbergs and electronvolts, and results can be exported to Pandas DataFrames. A built-in plotting module produces Matplotlib figures for DOS curves and SCF convergence. A command-line interface provides file summaries and JSON export without any Python scripting. The package also includes a programmatic input file generator, so full calculation pipelines from input preparation to output analysis can be run in Python.

</details>


### [63] [Magnetotransport Measurements on Isolated Polycrystalline Grains of Type-II Silicon Clathrate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18449)
*Sam Saiter,Joseph P. Briggs,Yinan Liu,Audrey Faricy,Gavin Sher,Carolyn A. Koh,Reuben T. Collins,Meenakshi Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文首次报道了利用微加工技术分离的单个II型硅包合物（NaₓSi₁₃₆, x ≪ 1）多晶晶粒的低温柔电子输运表征。拉曼光谱证实晶粒基本不含非晶硅；变温电阻率显示了包括热激活冻结行为和低温低激活能跃迁传导在内的多重导电机制；霍尔测量确认n型传导并揭示了载流子浓度及迁移率与激活能的相关性；栅极依赖的电导测量展示了室温下的静电可调性。这些结果确立了单个II型硅包合物晶粒的磁输运参数，并展示了该材料在未来量子与光电器件中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: II型硅包合物（type-II silicon clathrate）是一种具有笼状结构的硅同素异形体，其电子输运性质此前主要在宏观样品中研究，缺乏对单个晶粒的本征电学表征。该工作旨在通过微加工技术分离并表征单个多晶晶粒，以消除非晶硅杂质和晶界效应的干扰，获取本征输运参数。

Method: 采用微加工技术（microfabrication techniques）从多晶样品中分离出单个NaₓSi₁₃₆晶粒；通过拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）确认晶粒基本不含非晶硅（amorphous silicon, a-Si）杂质；利用变温电阻率、霍尔测量（Hall measurements）和栅极依赖电导测量进行系统电子输运表征。

Result: 变温电阻率呈现多重导电机制，包括热激活冻结行为（thermally activated freeze-out behavior）以及低温下向低激活能输运的转变，符合跳跃传导（hopping conduction）机制；霍尔测量在290 K至3.5 K范围内揭示了n型导电的载流子浓度与迁移率趋势，且与提取的激活能一致；栅极依赖电导测量在室温下观察到静电可调性（electrostatic tunability）。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了单个、隔离的II型硅包合物晶粒的磁输运参数（magnetotransport parameters），证实其具有多导电机制、n型导电特性和静电可调性，表明该材料在未来的量子器件（quantum devices）和光电器件（optoelectronic devices）中具有应用潜力。

Abstract: The first low-temperature electronic transport characterization of individual polycrystalline grains of type-II silicon clathrate (Na$_x$Si$_{136}$, $x \ll 1$), isolated using microfabrication techniques, is reported. Structural characterization via Raman spectroscopy confirms that the isolated grains are largely devoid of amorphous silicon (a-Si). Temperature-dependent resistivity reveals multiple conduction regimes, including thermally activated freeze-out behavior and a transition to low-activation-energy transport at cryogenic temperatures, consistent with hopping conduction mechanisms. Hall measurements from 290 K to 3.5 K yield carrier concentration and mobility trends that correlate with the extracted activation energies, verifying $n$-type conduction. Additionally, gate-dependent conductivity measurements demonstrate electrostatic tunability at room temperature. Collectively, these results establish the magnetotransport parameters of single, isolated grains of type-II silicon clathrate and demonstrate the potential of this material for future quantum and optoelectronic devices.

### [64] [Hydration-controlled twist forms a moiré glass in charge-frustrated layered silicates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18477)
*Juhyeok Lee,Piotr Zarzycki,Colin Ophus,Jim Ciston,Benjamin Gilbert,Jillian F. Banfield,Mary C. Scott,Michael L. Whittaker*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现蒙脱石（montmorillonite），一种丰富的膨胀性黏土，能够自然形成可调的莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）。通过高分辨率透射电镜、几何相位分析和分子动力学模拟，揭示了其旋转无序（rotational disorder）偏向于由离散水合状态继承的低角度错向，多层堆叠优先采用1-2°、4°和10°附近的扭转角，形成无长程旋转序的长波长莫尔条纹。作者将这种动力学受阻状态定义为“莫尔玻璃（moiré glass）”，区别于无特征的无序堆叠。模拟表明晶格电荷无序稳定了角度偏好，而电荷有序则促进随机堆叠；水合作用屏蔽层间相互作用并润滑扭转，脱水则以离散步骤固定构型。这些结果将动态水合确立为编程层状物质扭转的宏观手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭转层状材料可产生莫尔超晶格，但通常需要精确的组装工艺来实现指定的扭转角。寻找一种能够自然形成可调莫尔超晶格的天然材料体系，并理解其背后的物理机制，是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 采用焦点系列高分辨率透射电子显微镜（focal-series high-resolution transmission electron microscopy, HRTEM）、几何相位分析（geometric phase analysis, GPA）和分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulation），对蒙脱石的旋转无序结构进行实验表征与理论模拟。

Result: 蒙脱石中观测到扭转角优先分布在1-2°、4°和10°附近，产生长波长莫尔条纹但缺乏长程旋转序。将该状态定义为莫尔玻璃。晶格电荷无序稳定了角度偏好，而电荷有序则导致随机堆叠；水合作用可屏蔽层间相互作用并润滑扭转，脱水则以离散步骤冻结构型。

Conclusion: 动态水合（hydration）可作为调控层状物质扭转角的宏观手段，为自然形成可调莫尔超晶格提供了新途径，并提出了莫尔玻璃这一介于有序与无序之间的新结构态。

Abstract: Twisting layered materials produces moiré superlattices, but prescribed twist angles are usually obtained by demanding assembly procedures. Here we show that montmorillonite, an abundant swelling clay, forms tunable moiré superlattices naturally. Focal-series high-resolution transmission electron microscopy, geometric phase analysis, and molecular dynamics simulation reveal that its apparent rotational disorder is biased toward low-angle misorientations inherited from discrete hydration states. Multilayer stacks preferentially adopt twists near 1-2°, 4°, and 10°, producing long-wavelength moirés without long-range rotational order. We define this kinetically trapped state as a moiré glass, distinct from featureless turbostratic stacking. Simulations indicate that lattice-charge disorder stabilizes the angular preferences, whereas charge ordering promotes random stacking. Hydration screens interlayer interactions and lubricates twist, while dehydration arrests the resulting configurations in discrete steps. These results establish dynamic hydration as a macroscopic handle for programming twist in layered matter.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用CVD法在SiO2/Si基底上合成了未掺杂与Ni掺杂的FGT纳米片；通过调节前驱体摩尔比，控制Fe浓度并实现4%的Ni/Fe比例；利用X射线光电子能谱（X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy, XPS）深度剖析确认Ni在晶体体相中的分布。

Conclusion: 该CMOS兼容的低成本CVD方法为Ni掺杂FGT纳米片的合成提供了简便途径，为后续表征及其在自旋电子学（spintronics）器件中的潜在集成奠定了基础。

Abstract: Iron germanium telluride (FGT; FemGenTe2) compounds have attracted significant interest due to their layered van der Waals structure, relatively high Curie temperature, and tunable magnetic properties. Chemical vapor deposition (CVD) is a particularly promising synthesis route owing to its simplicity, low cost, potential for scalability, and widespread adoption in the semiconductor industry, yet it has not been used previously to synthesize FGT with dopants. Here, we report CVD synthesis of both undoped and Ni-doped FGT nanosheets on SiO2/Si substrates. By adjusting precursor molar ratios, we synthesized Ni-doped FGT with multiple Fe concentrations and a 4% Ni-to-Fe ratio. X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy depth profiling further demonstrates that Ni is present in the bulk of the crystals. This straightforward, low-cost, and CMOS-compatible approach demonstrates a route to Ni-doped FGT nanosheets, establishing a foundation for future characterization of Ni-doped FGT and its potential integration into spintronic devices.

### [66] [Strain induced magnetic phase transition and anomalous transport phenomena in RuO$_2$ and MnF$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18603)
*Xiuxian Yang,Zhangqi Wu,Xiangju Wang,Shifeng Qian,Ping Yang,Xiaodong Zhou,Jian Hao,Wanxiang Feng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过紧束缚模型和第一性原理计算，展示了应变工程可以调控交错磁体（altermagnet）RuO₂和MnF₂的磁相变并激活横向响应（如反常霍尔效应、反常能斯特效应等），为反铁磁自旋电子学（antiferromagnetic spintronics）和磁光应用提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间反演对称性破缺的共线反铁磁体（collinear antiferromagnets）为自旋电子学提供了丰富的研究平台，但如何有效调控其磁相并激活本征禁戒的横向输运与磁光响应仍是一个关键问题。作者旨在探索应变工程作为一种简单手段来实现这一目标。

Method: 采用一般紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）和第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），以代表性交错磁体（altermagnet）RuO₂和MnF₂为研究对象，分析不同方向剪切应变对磁相和输运性质的影响。

Result: 在Néel矢量沿[001]方向的本征体系中，霍尔电导率张量（Hall conductivity tensor）的非对角元为零，反常输运和磁光响应被禁止。沿ac方向的剪切应变保持自旋对称性（spin symmetry），维持交错磁相；沿ab方向的剪切应变则破坏该对称性，在金属性RuO₂中驱动交错磁相转变为部分补偿的铁磁相（partially compensated ferrimagnetic phase），在半导体性MnF₂中转变为完全补偿的铁磁相（fully compensated ferrimagnetic phase）。同时，对称性降低使得反常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity）、反常能斯特电导率（anomalous Nernst conductivity）、反常热霍尔电导率（anomalous thermal Hall conductivity）以及磁光旋转角（magneto-optical rotation angle）等响应被激活，且随应变幅度增强而增大。

Conclusion: 应变工程是调控非常规反铁磁体中磁相和功能响应的有效手段，为反铁磁自旋电子学和磁光应用拓展了新的可能性。

Abstract: Collinear antiferromagnets with broken time-reversal symmetry have emerged as a fertile platform for spintronics. Using a general tight-binding model and first-principles calculations, we show that strain engineering provides a simple route to control magnetic phase transition and activate transverse responses in representative altermagnets RuO$_2$ and MnF$_2$. For pristine RuO$_2$ and MnF$_2$ with Néel vector $\mathbf{n}\parallel$ [001], symmetry constrains the off-diagonal elements of the Hall conductivity tensor to vanish, thereby forbidding anomalous transport and magneto-optical responses. Shear strain applied along the $ac$ direction preserves the spin symmetry relating the two spin-opposite magnetic sublattices and therefore maintains the altermagnetic phase. By contrast, shear strain applied along the $ab$ direction breaks this spin symmetry and drives a transition from an altermagnetic phase to a partially compensated ferrimagnetic phase in metallic RuO$_2$ and to a fully compensated ferrimagnetic phase in semiconducting MnF$_2$. In addition, the lowered symmetry enables finite anomalous Hall, anomalous Nernst, and anomalous thermal Hall conductivities, as well as magneto-optical rotation angles, which are prohibited in the pristine systems. These responses exhibit a clear strain dependence and become progressively stronger as the strain amplitude increases. Our results establish strain engineering as an effective route to manipulate magnetic phases and functional responses in unconventional antiferromagnets, thereby expanding opportunities for antiferromagnetic spintronics and magneto-optical applications.

</details>

TL;DR: 硅上氧化物的宽X射线光电子谱线源于核心能级结合能的连续统计分布；从Si到SiO₂的统计模拟再现了谱线展宽（最高达5 eV），与氩离子溅射数据重构的0.23 nm层分辨光谱定量吻合；该连续分布模糊了局部结构特征的光谱指纹，挑战了氧化物X射线光电子谱中传统的化学态归属方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释硅上氧化物的宽X射线光电子谱线（broad X-ray photoelectron lines）的物理起源，并揭示其对传统化学态归属（chemical state assignment）方法提出的挑战。

Method: 采用连续统计模拟（statistical simulations），覆盖从Si到SiO₂的组分范围；通过Ar⁺溅射（Ar⁺ sputtering）数据重构0.23 nm层分辨光谱（layer-resolved spectra），并与模拟结果进行定量对比。

Conclusion: 硅上氧化物的X射线光电子谱线展宽来自核心能级结合能（core-level binding energy）的连续统计分布，而非离散的化学态；这一分布会模糊局部结构基序（structural motifs）的谱学特征，因此传统化学态归属方法在氧化物X射线光电子谱（X-ray photoelectron spectra）中需被重新审视。

Abstract: We show that the broad X-ray photoelectron lines of silicon oxide on silicon arise from a continuous statistical distribution of core-level binding energies. Statistical simulations spanning compositions from Si to SiO$_2$ reproduce the full extent of this broadening, reaching 5 eV for SiO$_{1.0}$ , in quantitative agreement with 0.23 nm layer-resolved spectra reconstructed from Ar$^+$ sputtering data. This continuous distribution blurs distinct spectral fingerprints of local structural motifs, thereby challenging conventional chemical state assignment in oxide X-ray photoelectron spectra.

### [68] [Solution gate control of shallow silicon vacancy charge states in diamond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18819)
*Charlie Pattinson,Daniel J. McCloskey,Nikolai Dontschuk,Brett C. Johnson,Alexander A. Wood,David Simpson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过低能离子注入结合氧/氢终端的表面修饰，实现了超浅（<15 nm）金刚石硅空位色心（SiV）群的静态与动态电荷态调控；并利用水溶液电解门控在亚200 mV偏压下实现了可逆的SiV-到SiV0转换，为集成量子光子学和近红外生物电压成像提供了低功耗电控方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金刚石中的硅空位色心（SiV centers）兼具近红外发射与固态鲁棒性，但其性能受限于能否分离出有利的缺陷电荷态（charge states）。本研究旨在解决如何在超浅深度下静态和动态地控制SiV电荷态这一核心问题。

Method: 将低能离子注入（low-energy ion implantation）与定制的氧和氢终端（oxygen and hydrogen terminations）相结合，绘制出最大化荧光SiV-布居的相图；进一步采用水溶液电解门控（aqueous electrolytic gating），在亚200 mV偏压和低光功率下实现SiV-到SiV0的可逆转换。

Result: 成功识别出最大化SiV-布居、抑制暗电荷态的调控区间；实现了超低能耗（sub-200 mV）下可逆的电荷态转换，并验证了其与近红外生物兼容电压成像的兼容性。

Conclusion: 该工作为集成量子光子学和近红外生物电压成像提供了一种低功耗电控SiV群方案，展示了SiV在片上量子器件和生物传感中的应用潜力。

Abstract: Silicon-vacancy (SiV) centers in diamond combine near-infrared emission with solid-state robustness, but their performance hinges on isolating favorable defect charge states. We demonstrate static and dynamic control of ultra-shallow (<15 nm) SiV ensembles in type IIa diamond. By combining low-energy ion implantation with tailored oxygen and hydrogen terminations, we map regimes that maximise the fluorescent SiV- population over dark charge states. We then realize reversible SiV- to SiV0 conversion using aqueous electrolytic gating with sub-200 mV biases and low optical powers. Our results enable low-power electrical control of SiV ensembles for integrated quantum photonics and biologically compatible voltage imaging in the near-infrared.

Abstract: In this study, the structural, mechanical, electronic, optical, and thermoelectric properties of the novel lead-free halide double perovskite series beta2SnGeX6 (beta = K, Rb; X = Cl, Br, I) are systematically investigated using density functional theory (DFT). Mechanical analysis derived from elastic parameters characterizes the entire series as fundamentally ductile, ensuring high processing elasticity and resistance to micro-cracking during device manufacturing. Electronic band structures reveal direct bandgaps showing exceptional composition-dependent tunability from 1.44 eV down to 0.64 eV via progressive halogen substitution. The wide gap chloride variations are optimized for single-junction photovoltaic absorbers, while the narrower-gap bromide and iodide analogs show immense promise for tandem solar architectures and near-infrared photodetectors. Thermoelectrically, heavy constituent atoms introduce strong lattice anharmonicity and intense high-temperature Umklapp phonon scattering, significantly suppressing lattice thermal conductivity. Combined with low carrier effective masses that optimize electrical transport, the iodide compounds achieve higher power factors and outstanding dimensionless figures of merit (ZT = 2.4 for K2SnGeI6 at 1000 K). Ultimately, these lead-free double perovskite family emerges as an environmentally benign and versatile platform for next-generation green optoelectronics and solid-state waste-heat recovery.

Here, we show that crystal-facet engineering on curved Cu surfaces enables the stabilization, within a single preparation step, of two distinct 2D phosphorus phases with different electronic properties. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）是最近发现的一类磁体，其体相能带结构依赖特定的对称性，但表面和薄膜会破坏这些对称性。本文旨在探究这种对称性降低对表面附近体相交变磁体以及薄膜电子结构的影响。

Method: 基于对称性分析，研究表面取向与体相交变磁序对称平面之间的几何关系，考察不同表面和薄膜几何构型下布里渊区（Brillouin zone）的自旋简并性与自旋分裂（spin splitting）行为。

Result: 当表面与体相交变磁序的对称平面重合时，二维布里渊区呈现自旋简并能带，对应传统反铁磁行为；其他情况下对称性降低，自旋分裂发生改变。特别地，在g波交变磁体的特定表面取向薄膜中发现了d波自旋分裂，并伴随自旋分裂效应（spin-splitter effect）。

Abstract: Altermagnets are a newly identified class of magnetic materials that combine vanishing net magnetization within the unit cell with spin-split electronic states. Their theoretical description relies on symmetry properties of the bulk band structure. Surfaces and thin films, however, inherently break these symmetries. Here, we investigate the consequences of such symmetry reduction for the electronic structure of bulk altermagnets near the surface and of thin films. When the surface coincides with a symmetry plane of the bulk altermagnetic order, the resulting two-dimensional Brillouin zone exhibits spin-degenerate bands, corresponding to conventional antiferromagnetic behavior. In all other cases, the symmetry of the altermagnetic order is reduced, leading to modified spin splitting. Remarkably, we discover a thin-film geometry of a $g$-wave altermagnet with a particular surface orientation that enables a $d$-wave spin splitting, which is commonly accompanied by the spin-splitter effect, suggesting the functionalization of non-$d$-wave altermagnets by surfaces. Our findings demonstrate that symmetry breaking at surfaces and in thin films fundamentally reshapes altermagnetic spin textures, providing a tunable platform for controlling spin-dependent electronic phenomena.

Method: 第一种方法结合电子与不同声子模式耦合的模型，每个电子能带和声子模式仅需约10个第一性原理矩阵元，并推广了声学形变势模型（acoustic deformation potential model）以适用于任意晶体对称性和能带极值位置。第二种方法使用机器学习在布里渊区（Brillouin zone）中与输运相关的区域，对每个电子能带和声子模式约100个矩阵元进行插值。

Abstract: The ability to compute electron-phonon coupling from first principles, using density functional perturbation theory and interpolation techniques, has enabled predictive calculations of electronic transport coefficients in crystalline materials. However, these methods are still computationally expensive. Here we present two inexpensive methods to obtain thermoelectric transport properties of semiconductors using a small number of electron-phonon matrix elements calculated from first principles. The first method combines models for coupling of electrons with different phonon modes whose parameters are obtained from $\sim 10$ matrix elements per electronic band and phonon mode calculated from first principles. Within this method, we formulate the acoustic deformation potential model for arbitrary crystal symmetries and band extrema locations. The second method uses machine learning to interpolate $\sim 100$ electron-phonon matrix elements per electronic band and phonon mode on dense reciprocal space grids in the parts of the Brillouin zone relevant for transport. We apply both methods to two-dimensional MoS$_2$ and show very good agreement with the state-of-the-art method. The calculated thermoelectric properties also agree well with experiments. We find that the machine-learning method is more accurate and straightforward to implement compared to the model approach.

### [75] [AdsMind: A Physics-Grounded Multi-Agent System for Self-Correcting Discovery of Adsorption Configurations on Heterogeneous Catalyst Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19152)

Conclusion: AdsMind 同时实现了可靠性、自反思（self-reflection）与可解释性，能够支撑更多基于 DFT 的自主化学工作流。

Abstract: Identifying the lowest-energy surface-adsorbate configuration is critical for modeling heterogeneous catalysis, yet exhaustive exploration with ab initio calculations is computationally prohibitive. Machine-learning force fields (MLFFs) accelerate structural relaxation but leave the search over the vast configurational space a major bottleneck, and open-loop large language model (LLM) agents lack a physics-grounded feedback mechanism to correct erroneous initial guesses. We propose AdsMind (Adsorption configuration discovery with Machine intelligence and relaxation feedback), a closed-loop multi-agent framework that enables autonomous error correction through MLFF relaxation feedback. Across four LLM backends, AdsMind achieves consistently high search reliability, with success rates of 100% and 98.8% on the benchmarks AA20 and OCD-GMAE62. Relative to its single-pass (1-Shot) ablation it reduces cross-backend energy dispersion, and it uses only 4.11 and 4.67 MLFF relaxations per case, respectively -- an approximately 14-fold reduction over heuristic enumeration baselines. Density functional theory (DFT) validation using VASP/PBE on six representative AA20 systems shows that the reported open-loop Adsorb-Agent outputs exhibit qualitative adsorption-energy sign errors for molecular adsorbates, whereas AdsMind preserves the correct sign in all tested cases with closer quantitative agreement. TL;DR: 本文通过电子背散射衍射（electron backscatter diffraction, EBSD）测量，首次在大面积尺度上观察到高场 conditioning 处理前后铜电极内部晶粒取向差（intragrain misorientation）的显著差异，并发现该结构变化与蒙特卡罗模拟预测的 conditioning 状态变量 $E_S$ 的空间分布高度吻合，从而指向位错（dislocation）演化作为 conditioning 的物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高场 conditioning 是粒子加速器射频结构达到工作场强的关键过程，但其底层物理机制仍是开放问题。现有模型和间接测量指向亚表面位错动力学，但由于缺乏大面积结构测量的直接验证，该假说无法被确认。

Method: 采用电子背散射衍射（EBSD）技术，对在倾斜阳极几何结构（sloped-anode geometry）中经脉冲直流场（最高约 80 MV/m）conditioning 处理的铜阴极进行毫米尺度的大面积测量。在跨越场暴露梯度的九个感兴趣区域中，计算晶粒内平均取向差（mean intragrain misorientation），并使用三种独立取向差指标和 Kolmogorov–Smirnov 检验进行验证。

Result: 经场暴露区域的晶粒内平均取向差相比未暴露参考区域高出约 75%；该差异由三种独立取向差指标复现并经统计检验确认。取向差可分为三个层级（高场中心与边缘、低场外围、未暴露参考），与蒙特卡罗模拟预测的 conditioning 状态变量 $E_S$ 的空间轮廓相匹配。

Conclusion: 大面积结构观察首次直接表明 conditioning 过程与电极晶格微观结构的演化相关，特别是亚表面位错群体（subsurface dislocation population）的演变被认为是 conditioning 的候选物理基础。

Abstract: High-field conditioning is the process by which radio-frequency structures in particle accelerators and other high-gradient devices reach their operating fields, yet the underlying physical mechanism remains an open question. Models and indirect measurements point to subsurface dislocation dynamics, but large-area structural measurements have been missing. We present electron backscatter diffraction measurements spanning millimeter-scale regions on a copper cathode conditioned at pulsed direct-current fields up to $\sim$80~MV/m in a sloped-anode geometry, which imposes a known gradient of field exposure across a single electrode. Across nine regions of interest spanning this exposure range, the mean intragrain misorientation of field-exposed regions exceeds that of unexposed references by $\sim$75\%; the difference is reproduced by three independent misorientation metrics and confirmed by Kolmogorov--Smirnov tests. To our knowledge, this is the first large-area observation of structural differences between conditioned and unconditioned regions of a high-field electrode. The misorientation separates into three tiers (high-field center and edge, low-field periphery, and unexposed reference) that match the spatial profile of the conditioning-state variable $E_S$ predicted by Monte Carlo simulations. These observations point to the evolving subsurface dislocation population as a candidate physical basis of conditioning.

</details>


### [77] [Spin point group symmetry and classification of non-relativistic spin splitting in non-collinear magnetic structures: Identification of high-order spin splitting types (l=5,7, and 9)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19254)
*Luis Elcoro,Jesus Etxebarria,J. Manuel Perez-Mato,Emre S. Tasci*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于自旋群理论（spin-group theory），本文系统研究了共面（coplanar）和非共面（non-coplanar）磁性结构中电子能带的非相对论自旋劈裂（non-relativistic spin splitting）。作者编制了1249个非等价自旋点群（spin point groups, SpPGs）的表格，并作为在线数据库SPGENPOS发布在Bilbao晶体学服务器（Bilbao Crystallographic Server, BCS）上。针对每个SpPG，利用BCS中的STENSOR程序分析了对称性允许的自旋劈裂，发现除包含1'（时间反演与空间反演联合操作）的SpPG外，其余均允许自旋劈裂，最低阶单项式阶数l从0到9（l=8除外），并识别出l=5,7,9的新型自旋织构（spin textures），在真实材料LaMnAu5中验证了l=5的自旋劈裂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前对磁点群（magnetic point group）的枚举未考虑时间反演（time-reversal, TR）操作的可能存在，导致忽略了具有IV型磁空间群（magnetic space group）的大量磁性结构的完整自旋点群对称性。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统分析各类磁性结构中对称性允许的自旋劈裂类型。

Method: 以自旋群理论为基础，枚举所有非等价自旋点群，并将其表示为非平凡部分与自旋仅群（spin-only group）的直积，自旋仅群限定为平凡群或加入时间反演操作。利用BCS中的STENSOR程序，对每个共面和非共面SpPG进行对称性允许的自旋劈裂分析。

Result: 编制了1249个非等价自旋点群的完整列表及对称操作，并作为在线数据库SPGENPOS发布。除包含1'操作的SpPG外，其余所有共面和非共面SpPG均允许自旋劈裂，最低阶单项式阶数l覆盖0-9（l=8除外）。共线（collinear）情形中最低阶不超过l=6且TR禁止自旋劈裂，与此形成对比。识别出l=5,7,9的新型自旋织构，并在真实材料LaMnAu5中确认了l=5的自旋劈裂。

Conclusion: 自旋群理论揭示了共面和非共面磁性结构中远较共线情形丰富的自旋劈裂类型，尤其是奇次幂项的出现为新材料设计提供了新的对称性调控途径。所建立的SpPG数据库为相关材料的第一性原理研究和实验筛选提供了重要工具。

Abstract: A comprehensive study of the possible types of non-relativistic spin splitting of electronic bands in coplanar and non-coplanar magnetic structures is presented on the basis of spin-group theory. First, we tabulate all non-equivalent spin point groups (SpPGs) which can be expressed as a direct product of a nontrivial part and a spin-only group limited to be the intrinsic (trivial) one, or augmented by the time-reversal (TR) operation. This tabulation, which includes the listing of symmetry operations for 1249 nonequivalent SpPGs, is now available as an online database SPGENPOS in the Bilbao Crystallographic Server (BCS). This extends previous enumerations, in which the possible presence of TR in the magnetic point group was not taken into account, thus overlooking the full SpPG symmetry associated with the numerous magnetic structures which have a magnetic space group of type IV. For each of the listed coplanar and non-coplanar SpPGs, the spin-splitting that is symmetry allowed is analyzed in detail using the program STENSOR also in the BCS. Except for the SpPGs that include the operation 1', i.e., the combined operation of TR and space inversion, all other coplanar and non-coplanar SpPGs allow spin splitting at some order in a power expansion of the electron wave vector components. We find that, depending on the SpPG, spin-splitting terms can appear with the lowest-order monomials ranging from l=0 to 9, with the exception of l=8. This contrasts with the collinear case, where the lowest order is not higher than l=6, and where TR forbids any spin splitting. For the newly identified spin textures with powers l=5, 7, and 9, which are possible in some noncentrosymmetric SpPGs, the functional form of the spin splitting in terms of the components of the crystal momentum is given. One example of a real material, LaMnAu5, showing l=5 spin splitting is identified.

</details>

### [78] [Tunable Chaos in the Finite Mean SYK Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18529)
*Arkaprava Mukherjee,Sumilan Banerjee,Sandip P. Trivedi,Nandini Trivedi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过引入有限均值-标准差比g的耦合分布，推广了SYK模型（Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model），发现随着g增大，系统从最大混沌（maximal chaos）逐渐过渡到非混沌，但残余熵（residual entropy）始终存在且谱统计（spectral statistics）保持Wigner-Dyson分布，表明不同混沌度量（measures of chaos）可以解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准SYK模型具有最大混沌（Lyapunov指数λ_L=2πT）和有限零温残余熵等关键特征，但已有研究大多集中于零均值高斯分布耦合。为深入理解混沌的演化机制，本文研究了耦合分布具有有限均值-标准差比g的情形。

Method: 将标准SYK模型中耦合系数的零均值高斯分布推广为具有有限均值-标准差比g≡J_0/δJ的广义分布，通过改变g系统研究混沌行为及其相关物理量的演化。

Result: (i)系统仍是快速 scrambler，Lyapunov指数满足λ_L=A T，但系数A被抑制至小于2π；(ii)当g→∞时，无序时间序关联函数（out-of-time-ordered correlators, OTOCs）不再呈现指数增长，λ_L≈0；(iii)所有g值下谱关联（spectral correlations）均保持Wigner-Dyson能级间距统计；(iv)系统在所有g值下均保留有限残余熵，但幅度随g增大而减小。

Conclusion: 该广义SYK模型存在一个从混沌到非混沌的交叉（crossover），并且不同混沌度量之间发生了解耦——有限残余熵的存在并不严格意味着最大混沌。

Abstract: The complex Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model, featuring fermions with all-to-all interactions, serves as a dual paradigm for understanding non-Fermi liquid behavior and the holographic nature of charged black holes. Two defining characteristics of the standard SYK model are its maximal chaos (Lyapunov exponent $λ_{\mathrm{L}}=2πT$ at temperature $T$), and its finite zero-temperature residual entropy. While previous studies have largely focused on couplings drawn from a zero-mean Gaussian distribution, we investigate a generalized model with a finite mean-to-standard-deviation ratio, $g\equiv J_{0}/δJ$ of the coupling distribution in order to get deeper insight into the evolution of chaos. We find that increasing $g$ yields the following effects: (i) The system remains a fast scrambler with $λ_{\mathrm{L}}=A~T$, but with a suppressed coefficient $A<2π$. (ii) In the limit $g\to \infty$, out-of-time-ordered correlators (OTOCs) no longer exhibit exponential growth with $λ_{\mathrm{L}}\simeq 0$. (iii) The spectral correlations indicative of late-time chaos maintain Wigner-Dyson level spacing statistics for all values of $g$. (iv) The system preserves a finite residual entropy, albeit with reduced magnitude, for all $g$ values. We conclude that in this generalized SYK model, there is a chaotic to non-chaotic crossover. Moreover different measures of chaos decouple, demonstrating that the presence of finite residual entropy does not strictly imply maximal chaos.

</details>


### [79] [Hallmark Signatures of Electronic Pairing in Two-Photon Two-Electron Coincidence Angle-Resolved Photoemission Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18616)
*Janez Bonca,Alberto Nocera,Andrea Damascelli,Mona Berciu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文从理论和数值模拟上证明，双光子入双电子出（2γ→2e）的符合ARPES技术能够直接且无歧义地探测电子配对，其关键信号在光电子能量平面上的分离仅由能量守恒决定，无需材料特定假设或复杂数据分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联量子材料中的电子配对机制是凝聚态物理的核心难题，现有的角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）只能间接探测电子关联，缺乏直接探测电子配对的实验手段。

Method: 通过一般性理论论证，并对具有配对基态与未配对基态的强关联模型进行大规模数值模拟，对比单光子入双电子出（γ→2e）与双光子入双电子出（2γ→2e）两种符合ARPES方案。

Result: 在双光子入双电子出（2γ→2e）方案中，来自同一电子对的信号与来自不同电子对的信号在光电子能量平面（ω₁, ω₂）上可实现模型无关的分离，该分离仅源于能量守恒。

Conclusion: 双光子入双电子出（2γ→2e）符合ARPES能够直接识别电子配对，提取配对结合能（pair binding energy）及胶子玻色子（'glue' boson）能量，无需复杂数据分析或额外测量。

Abstract: Understanding strongly correlated quantum materials remains a central challenge in condensed matter physics and materials science. While angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) has become an indispensable probe of single-quasiparticle excitations, it accesses electronic correlations only indirectly. Here we show that unlike one-photon in, two-electrons out coincidence ARPES ($γ\!\rightarrow\!2e$ 2eARPES), the two-photon in, two-electron out $2γ\!\rightarrow\!2e$ 2eARPES provides a direct and unambiguous probe of electronic pairing. We establish this on general theoretical grounds and substantiate it through large-scale numerical simulations of strongly correlated models with both paired and unpaired ground states. The key result is a model-independent separation in the $(ω_1,ω_2)$ plane of the two photoelectrons' energies, between signal from electrons emitted from the \emph{same} pair and signal from electrons emitted from \emph{different} pairs; this follows from energy conservation alone and is independent of any material-specific assumptions. Our findings demonstrate that $2γ\!\rightarrow\!2e$ 2eARPES can identify pairing and extract the pair binding energy as well as the energy of the 'glue' boson without any sophisticated data analysis or complementary measurements.

### [80] [$d$-wave altermagnetism revealed by resonant inelastic X-ray scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18731)
*Guangkai Zhang,Yuehong Li,Xubin Ye,Vincent C. Morano,Sze Tung Li,Jaewon Choi,Rebecca Scatena,Shuai Tang,Maocai Pi,Mengqi Ye,Mirian Garcia-Fernandez,Alessandro Bombardi,Xiaomei Qin,Zhao Pan,Daniel G. Mazzone,Qisi Wang,Yi Lu,Yao Shen,Youwen Long*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）中的圆二色性实验，在强关联Lieb晶格磁体La₂O₃Mn₂Se₂中证明了d波交变磁性（d-wave altermagnetism）的存在，并通过对称性分析和精确对角化计算确认该二色性源于交变磁对称性约束，而非实验几何效应，从而解决了长期争议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁性（altermagnetism）作为第三类共线磁有序态，具有自旋极化能带和非寻常手性磁子（chiral magnons）等特性，是功能材料的重要平台。然而其实验验证长期存在争议——RIXS中的圆二色性是否是交变磁性的本征属性尚不明确，本文旨在解决这一争议并提供确凿的实验证据。

Method: 采用共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）实验测量La₂O₃Mn₂Se₂中的磁激发谱，结合RIXS算符对称性分析（RIXS-operator symmetry analysis）和精确对角化计算（exact-diagonalization calculations），验证观察到的圆二色性是否源于交变磁对称性约束。

Result: RIXS谱在磁激发中呈现d波对称的圆二色性（d-wave-symmetry circular dichroism），该二色性在顺磁相中消失。通过对称性分析和精确对角化证明，该二色性是交变磁对称性约束的直接结果，与磁子支分裂（magnon branch splitting）无关。

Conclusion: 研究提供了La₂O₃Mn₂Se₂中d波交变磁性实现的明确实验证据，并确立了圆偏振RIXS作为一种高度对称性敏感的光谱学框架，可用于探测传统探针难以检测的磁相。

Abstract: Altermagnetism defines a third fundamental class of collinear magnetic order, featuring compensated magnetic moments with antiparallel spin alignment, yet lifted Kramers degeneracy without the need for relativistic spin-orbit coupling. Its ability to host spin-polarized electronic bands and unconventional chiral magnons makes it a promising platform for functional materials. However, experimental verification has proven challenging; while circular dichroism in resonant inelastic X-ray scattering (RIXS) has been suggested as a signature of chiral magnons, it remains controversial whether this effect is an intrinsic property of altermagnetism or an artifact of experimental geometry. In this work, we resolve this debate and provide unambiguous experimental evidence of $d$-wave altermagnetism in the strongly correlated Lieb-lattice magnet La$_2$O$_3$Mn$_2$Se$_2$. The RIXS spectra exhibit a $d$-wave-symmetry circular dichroism in the magnetic excitations that vanishes in the paramagnetic phase. Through RIXS-operator symmetry analysis and exact-diagonalization calculations, we prove that the observed dichroism is a direct consequence of altermagnetic symmetry constraints, independent of magnon branch splitting. Our results provide definitive evidence for the experimental realization of $d$-wave altermagnetism in La$_2$O$_3$Mn$_2$Se$_2$ and establish circularly polarized RIXS as a highly symmetry-sensitive spectroscopic framework for detecting magnetic phases that evade conventional probes.

</details>


### [81] [Mimicry of chaos and $k$-design in higher order OTOCs of Luttinger liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18800)
*Balázs Dóra,Catalin Pascu Moca,Roderich Moessner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了Luttinger液体及其晶格实现（XXZ海森堡链）中的高阶时序关联子（higher-order OTOCs）序列，揭示了它们快速擦除初始态记忆并饱和到稳态值的行为。通过将高阶OTOC的晚期饱和值精确映射到非厄米Harper模型的配分函数，发现中等强度相互作用下稳态OTOC可小至七阶，模拟了更高阶的k-设计（k-design），表明Luttinger液体通过高阶OTOC视角展现出出人意料的信息加扰（scrambling）深度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 乱时序关联子（Out-of-time-order correlators, OTOCs）是量子混沌的基本度量，但捕捉信息加扰的精细结构需要探索其高阶推广。该研究旨在系统考察高阶OTOC序列在Luttinger液体及其晶格对应物中的完整时间动力学及其稳态行为。

Method: 采用玻色化（bosonization）与数值计算相结合的方法，提取了前三阶OTOC的完整时间动力学。通过将高阶OTOC的晚期饱和值计算映射到非厄米Harper模型（non-Hermitian Harper model）的配分函数（partition function），建立了严格的理论对应关系。

Result: 高阶OTOC快速擦除初始态记忆并迅速饱和至稳态值；在中等强度相互作用下，稳态OTOC值可参数化地小至第七阶，从而模拟了更高阶k-设计的行为。

Conclusion: 通过高阶OTOC的视角，Luttinger液体展现出意料之外的、更深层的信息加扰现象，表明该系统在量子混沌和信息加扰方面具有比先前认知更为丰富的结构。

Abstract: Out-of-time-order correlators (OTOCs) provide a fundamental metric for quantum chaos, but capturing the fine structure of information scrambling requires exploring their higher-order generalizations. Here, we systematically investigate the sequence of higher-order OTOCs in a Luttinger liquid and its lattice realization, the XXZ Heisenberg chain. Using bosonization and numerics, we extract the full temporal dynamics of the first three OTOCs, revealing that they rapidly erase memory of the initial state, and quickly saturate to their steady state values. Strikingly, we show that calculating the late time saturation values for the entire sequence of higher-order OTOCs maps exactly onto determining the partition function of a non-Hermitian Harper model. Through this mapping, we demonstrate that for moderately strong interactions, the steady-state OTOCs become parametrically small up to the seventh order, mimicking higher $k$-design. Our results reveal that Luttinger liquids exhibit an unexpectedly profound degree of apparent scrambling when viewed through the lens of higher-order OTOCs.

</details>


### [82] [Emergence of Resonating Valence-Bond Correlations in Stretched Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18973)
*Sam Azadi,A. Principi,T. D. Kühne,M. S. Bahramy*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）计算表明，拉伸蜂窝状晶格可以增强石墨烯（graphene）中的电子关联效应。研究发现共振价键（RVB）态相对于单行列式描述的能量增益随键长拉伸先增加后减小，在15%-20%的临界应变范围内出现交叉，预示着从弱关联狄拉克半金属到增强非动态关联与短程单态配对的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯中π电子的带宽较大，通常认为其电子关联（electronic correlations）效应较弱。本文旨在探索通过晶格拉伸增强关联效应的可能性，并检验共振价键（resonating-valence-bond, RVB）类关联在拉伸石墨烯中是否变得能量上更有利。

Method: 采用变分量子蒙特卡洛（variational quantum Monte Carlo）和扩散量子蒙特卡洛（diffusion quantum Monte Carlo）方法，对一系列拉伸石墨烯晶格比较了常规Jastrow-Slater行列式波函数与RVB Jastrow-反对称化双粒子乘积（Jastrow-antisymmetrized geminal product）变分波函数的性能。

Result: RVB态相对于单行列式描述的能量增益随键拉伸非单调演化：在达到临界应变δ_cr之前增加，之后减小。该交叉发生在15% < δ_cr < 20%的范围内，与机械稳定性极限一致。

Conclusion: 该行为表明体系从弱关联狄拉克半金属（weakly correlated Dirac semimetal）转变为增强非动态关联（non-dynamic correlation）和短程单态配对（short-range singlet pairing）的相。晶格膨胀可驱动石墨烯进入RVB类关联能量上有利的区域，为调控狄拉克材料（Dirac materials）中的关联效应提供了简单途径。

Abstract: Electronic correlations in graphene are generally considered weak due to the large bandwidth of its $π$ electrons. Here we show that tensile expansion of the honeycomb lattice provides a direct route to enhancing correlation effects. Using variational and diffusion quantum Monte Carlo, we compare a conventional Jastrow-Slater determinant wave function with a resonating-valence-bond (RVB) Jastrow-antisymmetrized geminal product ansatz for a series of stretched graphene lattices. We find that the energy gain of the RVB state relative to the single-determinant description increases with bond expansion up to a critical strain $δ_{\mathrm{cr}}$, and decreases beyond it, revealing a nonmonotonic evolution of electronic correlations. The crossover is found to occur in the range $15\% < δ_{\mathrm{cr}} < 20\%$, in agreement with mechanical stability limits. This behavior indicates a transition from a weakly correlated Dirac semimetal to a regime with enhanced non-dynamic correlation and short-range singlet pairing. Our results provide direct many-body evidence that lattice expansion drives graphene into a regime where RVB-like correlations become energetically favorable, offering a simple route to tuning correlation effects in Dirac materials.

</details>


### [83] [Mapping the non-equilibrium interacting Anderson Impurity Model to an effective Gaussian theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19206)
*Emmanuel Bogacz,Graham Kells,Andrew K. Mitchell*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明，安德森杂质模型（Anderson Impurity Model, AIM）在淬火后的时间演化动力学可以通过一个完全无相互作用的版本描述，代价是耦合到额外的静态辅助自由度；从而将相互作用的非平衡动力学简化为更大维度的有效无相互作用系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联量子杂质模型（quantum impurity model）在强非平衡条件下的物理学极为复杂且难以描述，而高斯型无相互作用费米子模型则易于求解。本文旨在建立两者之间的映射，以简化对非平衡动力学的理解。

Method: 从淬火AIM的精确对角化（exact diagonalization, ED）和密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）全解出发，通过数值优化研究该映射的性质，并探索辅助系统中隐藏的结构。

Result: 发现了辅助系统中具有启发性的结构，并成功将相互作用非平衡动力学映射为更大维度的有效无相互作用系统。

Conclusion: 该方法使得能够通过更简单的有效无相互作用系统（维度更高）的视角来理解相互作用的非平衡动力学。

Abstract: Quantum impurity models with strong electron correlations, such as the paradigmatic Anderson Impurity Model (AIM), are central to our understanding of a range of physical phenomena including local moment formation, Coulomb blockade and Kondo screening. They describe magnetic atoms and molecules on surfaces, quantum dot circuits, and correlated materials through dynamical mean field theory. The physics of such systems in strongly non-equilibrium conditions is particularly complex and challenging to capture, whereas Gaussian models of free fermions can be easily solved. Here we show that the time-evolving dynamics of the AIM after a quench can be described by a completely non-interacting version of the model, at the expense of coupling to additional static auxiliary degrees of freedom. Starting from the full solution of the quenched AIM using ED and DMRG, we study the properties of this mapping using numerical optimization, and uncover intriguing structure in the auxiliary system. The method allows us to understand interacting non-equilibrium dynamics through the simpler lens of an effective non-interacting system of larger dimension.

</details>

### [84] [Noise seeded oscillators: on the role of demographic fluctuations in a multi-populations model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19181)
*Francesca Di Patti,Duccio Fanelli,Perla Rosi*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文研究三群体随机动力学模型，证明第三种波动物种可增强或抑制由有限大小涨落引发的准周期振荡，扩展了Kuramoto同步理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统双群体模型已证明内源性有限大小涨落（finite size fluctuations）可触发随机振荡，但引入更多群体成分对振荡行为的影响尚不明确，需要系统分析第三种波动物种对原有准周期振荡（quasi-cycles）的调控机制。

Method: 采用解析分析与数值模拟相结合的方法，在原始双群体神经交互模型中引入第三种波动物种，通过人口统计噪声（demographic noise）驱动系统动力学，考察群体间耦合振荡的涌现与演化特征。

Result: 解析与数值结果一致表明，第三种添加的物种既能增强也能抑制两个原始群体的准周期振荡；该效应由人口统计噪声成分触发，且与群体间耦合动力学密切相关。

Conclusion: 所研究的耦合噪声振子动力学为同步化（synchronization）研究提供了超越Kuramoto奠基性框架的扩展理论体系，揭示了多群体随机振荡中丰富的调控可能性。

Abstract: Stochastic oscillations can emerge from a two-population model as triggered by endogenous finite size fluctuations. Here, an extended dynamical scenario is considered in which a third fluctuating species is added to a proto-typical scheme of neuronal interaction. As we shall prove both analytically and numerically, the third added species can enhance or even suppress the emergence of quasi-cycles, namely the coherent oscillations of the two original populations, as instigated by the demographic noise component. In general, investigating the coupled dynamics of noisy oscillators of the type considered could yield an extended framework for synchronization studies, beyond the pioneering setting introduced by Kuramoto.

### [85] [Extracting effective scaling exponents in finite-size hyperuniform systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18848)
*Yuan Liu,Xurui Li,Jianxiang Tian,Xunwang Yan,Ge Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文针对有限尺寸超均匀（hyperuniform）点构型中关键标度指数α的估计难题，提出了一个结合结构因子（structure factor）、数方差（number variance）和扩散可铺展性（spreadability）三种互补方法的实用协议，通过联合经验估计器（joint empirical estimator）和内部离散度评估确定稳健的最优估计值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限样本中准确估计超均匀性指数α面临诸多挑战：推断值强烈依赖于可访问的长度尺度范围、有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）以及所选用的表征方法（结构因子、数方差或扩散可铺展性）。现有每种单一方法均存在固有局限，例如结构因子法对低波数拟合截断敏感，数方差法依赖有限尺寸数据是否保留缩放信息，可铺展性法则需物理可行的长时拟合窗口。

Method: 开发了一种方法感知（method-aware）实用协议，将三种互补方法（结构因子法、数方差法、扩散可铺展性法）整合使用，每种方法扮演不同角色。协议通过联合经验估计器汇总各方法的特定估计值，并利用参与方法之间的内部离散度来确定最优估计。

Result: 该协议能够对有限尺寸超均匀点构型中的有效标度指数α进行稳健估计，通过多方法交叉验证降低了单一方法带来的偏差和不确定性。

Conclusion: 提出了一种系统性的多方法融合策略用于有限尺寸超均匀系统的指数估计，通过方法间的互补与内部一致性检验提升了估计的稳健性。

Abstract: Hyperuniform systems strongly suppress long-wavelength density fluctuations, which is quantitatively characterized by the small-wavenumber scaling. In finite samples, however, accurately estimating the hyperuniformity exponent α can be challenging. The inferred value depends strongly on the range of length scales accessible in the measurement, finite-size effects, and the specific characterization method employed, whether based on Fourier-space structure factors, real-space density fluctuations, or dynamical probes such as diffusion spreadability. In particular, the structure-factor method provides the most direct estimate of α, but is sensitive to empirical low-k fitting cutoffs. The number-variance method offers a real-space Class-like diagnosis, but contributes a numerical exponent only when the finite-size data retain Class III-like scaling information. The spreadability method provides a smoother dynamic estimate and reduces configuration-level fluctuations, but requires a physically admissible long-time fitting window. Here, we develop a practical method-aware protocol for robust estimation of the effective scaling exponent α in finite-size hyperuniform point configurations, combining three complementary methods with distinct roles. Our protocol summarizes the method-specific estimates through a joint empirical estimator and reports the internal dispersion among the participating methods to determine the optimal estimate.

</details>

*Shi-Hao Bi,Bo Fu,Shun-Qing Shen*
