Method: 采用解析分析方法，基于半磁拓扑绝缘体薄膜中无序奇偶异常半金属的模型，系统考察了外禀机制（侧跳与斜散射）对反常霍尔电导的贡献。

Result: 外禀机制（侧跳与斜散射）对反常霍尔电导无贡献；无质量狄拉克锥表面态（gapless Dirac cone surface state）对无序散射表现出显著的鲁棒性（robustness）。

Conclusion: 奇偶异常半金属是一种无序鲁棒的量子相，该结果为狄拉克费米子物理提供了新的认识。

Abstract: We present an analytical investigation of the extrinsic contributions to the anomalous Hall conductivity in the context of the half-quantized Hall effect observed in disordered parity anomalous semimetal emerged from semi-magnetic topological insulator thin films. The gapless Dirac cone surface state, which embodies the quintessence of the half-quantized Hall effect, exhibits remarkable robustness against disorder scattering. Two primary extrinsic mechanisms, the side-jump and skew-scattering, are deemed irrelevant and make no contributions. These results establish the parity anomalous semimetal as a disorder-resilient quantum phase, thereby providing insights into Dirac fermion physics.

### [87] [Prospects for Observing Gravity-gradient Noise and Earthquake Gravity Signals with CHRONOS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19124)
*Mario Juvenal S. Onglao,Yuki Inoue,Daiki Tanabe*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文研究了使用拟议的低温亚赫兹扭摆探测器CHRONOS（Cryogenic sub-Hz cROss torsion-bar detector with quantum NOn-demolition speed meter）作为平台，探测亚赫兹频段内的重力梯度噪声（Newtonian Noise）以及地震引发的瞬态引力信号（prompt gravitational signals）的可行性。建模结果表明，瑞利波牛顿噪声是主要环境贡献，而地震引力信号可在数十公里距离上达到可探测的信噪比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚赫兹频段的引力波探测器受到环境重力梯度涨落（即牛顿噪声，Newtonian Noise）的严重限制，但该频段同时也为探测与地震和大气过程相关的地面引力扰动提供了独特机会。现有工作缺乏对这类信号在实际探测器平台上可行性的系统评估。

Method: （1）对瑞利波诱导的地震场、大气次声涨落（atmospheric infrasound fluctuations）以及地震期间瞬态质量重新分布（transient mass redistribution）所产生的重力梯度贡献进行建模；（2）将这些贡献投影到CHRONOS扭摆响应函数上；（3）通过计算信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）评估地震引力信号的探测能力。

Result: CHRONOS在约2 Hz附近达到约1e-18 Hz^(-1/2)的峰值应变灵敏度。瑞利波牛顿噪声在约0.5 Hz以下占主导，大气牛顿噪声在整个频段内低数个量级。对于一个Mw = 5.2的代表性地震事件，约90 km以内的源可产生可探测信号；40 km距离上亚赫兹频段积分的信噪比约为3.62，对应应变振幅在0.2–0.6 Hz达到CHRONOS灵敏度曲线。

Conclusion: CHRONOS具有在亚赫兹频段同时探测重力梯度噪声和瞬态地球物理引力信号的潜力。地震引力信号预计比地震P波（P-wave）早到达数秒，表明该探测器可能为地震早期预警提供新的物理渠道。

Abstract: Ground-based gravitational-wave detectors operating in the sub-Hertz regime are expected to be strongly limited by environmental gravity-gradient fluctuations, commonly referred to as Newtonian Noise (NN). At the same time, this frequency band provides unique opportunities to probe terrestrial gravitational perturbations associated with seismic and atmospheric processes. In this work, we investigate the feasibility of using the proposed Cryogenic sub-Hz cROss torsion-bar detector with quantum NOn-demolition speed meter (CHRONOS) as a platform for studying gravity-gradient noise and detecting prompt gravitational signals from earthquakes.
  We model gravity-gradient contributions from Rayleigh-wave-induced seismic fields, atmospheric infrasound fluctuations, and transient mass redistribution during earthquakes, and project these onto the CHRONOS torsion-bar response. CHRONOS achieves a peak strain sensitivity of order ~1e-18 Hz^(-1/2) near ~2 Hz. Rayleigh-wave NN is found to be the dominant environmental contribution below approximately 0.5 Hz, while atmospheric NN remains several orders of magnitude smaller throughout the frequency range considered.
  We further assess the detectability of prompt gravitational signals from earthquakes. For a representative Mw = 5.2 event, sources within approximately 90 km may produce detectable signals. At 40 km distance, we obtain a signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) of approximately 3.62 integrated over the sub-Hz band, with a corresponding strain amplitude reaching the CHRONOS sensitivity curve around 0.2 to 0.6 Hz. The gravitational signal is expected to precede seismic P-wave arrival by several seconds, depending on the assumed propagation velocity.
  These results demonstrate the potential of CHRONOS to probe both gravity-gradient noise and transient geophysical gravity signals in the sub-Hertz regime.

### [89] [Dynamics of monohydroxy alcohols with chain-like structures: Hydrogen bonding lifetime, chain swapping, and Debye process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18626)
*Shiwang Cheng,Shalin Patil*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于可逆氢键（H-bonding）假设，在活链模型（LCM）框架下描述了单羟基醇（MAs）的超分子结构与动力学，揭示了四种时间尺度及其相互作用下的五个动力学区间，并成功解释了介电与线性粘弹性实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为单羟基醇（MAs）的超分子结构与动力学建立理论框架，链接可逆氢键（reversible H-bonding）相互作用与宏观性质（如介电和线性粘弹性）。

Method: 采用活链模型（living chain model, LCM），假设可逆氢键缔合与解离，从结构和动力学两方面分析超分子链的浓度分布与松弛行为。

Result: 结构上，氢键导致超分子链摩尔浓度呈单一指数分布；动力学上，揭示了除结构松弛时间（tau_a）和德拜松弛时间（tau_D）外的链断裂时间（tau_B）和氢键寿命（tau_H）。四种时间尺度定义了五个动力学区间；在形成超分子链的区间中，德拜松弛源于链端到端偶极重定向，标度关系为Nc~tau_D/tau_a。模型与单羟基醇的介电和线性粘弹性实验定量一致。

Conclusion: 可逆氢键相互作用可通过活链模型定量描述单羟基醇的超分子结构、动力学与宏观性质，建立了从分子间相互作用到材料性能的理论桥梁。

Abstract: By assuming reversible H-bonding association and dissociation, this work provides a description of the supramolecular structure and dynamics of monohydroxy alcohols (MAs) within the framework of a recently proposed living chain model (LCM). Structurally, reversible H-bonding leads to a single exponential distribution of the molar concentration of the supramolecular chain with length N. Dynamically, reversible H-bonding enables supramolecular chain breakage and recombination, which modifies the relaxation time of the supramolecular chains. In addition to the structural relaxation, tau_a, and the Debye relaxation, tau_D, two other relaxation times are revealed: the chain breakage time, tau_B, and the H-bonding lifetime, tau_H. The interplay among these four-time scales defines five distinct dynamics regimes. In Regimes I and V, no supramolecular chains form. In Regimes II and IV, supramolecular chains form and give a Debye relaxation. The characteristic chain length scales as Nc~tau_D/tau_a. In these two regimes, the H-bonding lifetime controls the Debye process. In Regime III, large supramolecular chains form. In all regimes with supramolecular chain formation, the Debye relaxation comes from the overall chain end-to-end dipole reorientation and scales with Nc. Excellent agreements between experiments and LCM have been observed, leading to quantitative descriptions of the dielectric and linear viscoelastic properties of MAs. These results thus establish a theoretical framework linking reversible H-bonding interactions to supramolecular structures, dynamics, and macroscopic properties of MAs.

</details>


### [90] [Chiral Packings in Cylinders are Ultrasensitive to Confinement Deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19082)
*Xuebin Wang,Jiahao Guo,Yao Li*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过模拟、理论和实验，研究了硬球在椭圆圆柱（elliptic cylinder）中的最密堆积（densest packing），发现从圆形圆柱出发，即使微弱的横截面变形也能引发全新相态，包括消除全局手性（global chirality）或显著增加手性结构复杂性的相。新理论成功预测了椭圆圆柱中的螺旋相（helical phase）和双振荡链相（double oscillated-chain phase），为理解各向异性圆柱中的堆积提供了新见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圆形圆柱中的球体堆积（sphere packing）已发现手性螺旋结构（chiral helical structure），但斑马鱼相关实验的结果与已知堆积结构不符。为解释生物管道的固有缺陷，本研究将椭圆圆柱视为圆形圆柱的规范变形，探究其最密堆积行为。

Method: 采用模拟（simulation）、理论（theory）和实验（experiment）相结合的方法，以椭圆圆柱作为圆形圆柱的规范变形，从圆形圆柱中的手性结构出发，系统研究横截面变形对硬球最密堆积的影响。

Result: 即使微弱的横截面变形也能触发全新相态：部分相消除全局手性，部分相显著复杂化手性结构。各向异性约束下的新螺旋相保持手性并发展出分层周期结构（hierarchical periodic structure）。新理论预测了椭圆圆柱中的螺旋相及无手性的双振荡链相，后者与模拟结果完美匹配。

Conclusion: 本工作揭示了圆柱各向异性（cylindrical anisotropy）对堆积结构的重要影响，为理解各向异性圆柱中的堆积提供了新见解，有助于新型材料设计和生物系统理解。

Abstract: Sphere packings in circular cylinders have attracted substantial research interest, among which the discovery of chiral helical structures is the most iconic. However, recent experimental results on zebrafish do not match the known packing structures in circular cylinders. To account for the inherent imperfections of biological tubes, we take elliptic cylinders as the canonical deformation of circular cylinders and investigate the densest packings of hard spheres in them using simulation, theory, and experiments. Starting from the chiral structures in circular cylinders, we demonstrate that even a weak cross-sectional deformation can trigger entirely new phases, including ones that either eliminate global chirality or significantly complicate the chiral structures. This reveals the significant effect of cylindrical anisotropy. The new helical phases under anisotropic confinement remain chiral and develop hierarchical periodic structures, which are difficult to obtain by simulations but are predicted by our newly developed theory for helical phases in elliptic cylinders. The theory also predicts double oscillated-chain phases without chirality, which perfectly match the simulations. Our work offers fresh insights into understanding packings in anisotropic cylinders, which will help researchers to design new materials and to understand many living systems.

</details>


### [91] [Ewald summing irreducible components of flow around active particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18742)
*Mayurakshi Deb,Rajesh Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于Ewald求和技术计算周期性边界条件下活性粒子周围流体流动不可约分量的方法，用于研究活性胶体悬浮液中的流体动力学相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在周期性几何（periodic geometry）的斯托克斯流（Stokes flow）中，活性粒子产生的流场需要高效精确的计算方法，以便研究活性胶体悬浮液中粒子间的流体动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）。

Method: 将活性粒子建模为具有表面滑移速度（surface slip velocity）的胶体球；通过Oseen张量（Oseen tensor）及其导数的晶格求和（lattice sum）得到活性流场的不可约表示（irreducible representation）；利用Ewald求和技术（Ewald summation technique）加速晶格求和收敛。

Result: 得到了活性粒子在周期性斯托克斯流中任意表面滑移模式下的流场解析表达式，并计算了流体动力学相互作用下活性粒子刚体运动（rigid body motion）的显式表达式。

Conclusion: 该方法为实现周期性边界条件下任意活性滑移模式的活性粒子动力学模拟提供了一条可行途径。

Abstract: We present a method to compute Ewald summation for the irreducible components of flow around active particles to study hydrodynamic interactions in active colloidal suspensions. An active particle is modeled as a colloidal sphere with a surface slip velocity. Using this model, we obtain an irreducible representation of the fluid flow produced by an active particle in periodic geometry of Stokes flow for an arbitrary surface slip. The solution of the active flow is obtained in terms of lattice sum of the Oseen tensor and their derivatives. The lattice sum is accelerated using the Ewald summation technique. We apply the method to compute explicit expression for rigid body motion of hydrodynamically interacting active particles. Our method presents a way for dynamic simulation of active particles due to arbitrary mode of active slip in periodic geometry of Stokes flow.

</details>


### [92] [On the emergence of molecular tilt in a ferroelectric smectic liquid crystal with broken director-inversion symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18870)

Abstract: The origin of some mesophases of the ferroelectric nematic realm is not yet well understood. In this work we study the highly polar liquid crystal MIO, a close structural analogue of the prototypical ferroelectric nematogen DIO, which exhibits a ferroelectric smectic A to ferroelectric smectic C (SmAF-SmCF) phase transition. Calorimetric, dielectric and light-scattering experiments reveal that it is a second-order phase transition with mean-field behavior, and is driven by the softening of the tilt elastic constant accompanied by the divergence of the amplitude of the associated dielectric mode.

### [93] [Enucleated incompressible red blood cells in shear flow: theoretical analysis of shape instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19072)
*Avraham Moriel,Howard A. Stone,Simon Mendez*

TL;DR: 本文通过微扰理论框架研究准球形红细胞在剪切流中的形状不稳定性，扩展了模型以考虑不同过剩面积，分析了多叶形状（如 stomatocyte 和 trilobe）的涌现机制，揭示了膜张力饱和与过剩面积再分布的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红细胞（RBC）在微循环中表现出显著的多叶状形变，标志着一种动态不稳定性（dynamic instability），而现有理论对其机制的理解尚不充分。

Method: 采用准球形红细胞在外部剪切流下的微扰理论框架（perturbative theoretical framework），首先扩展模型以显式考虑应力自由态与当前膜形态之间的不同过剩面积（excess area）；然后引入额外空间模态，分析不稳定性对剪切模量、弯曲模量、内外黏度比及过剩面积的依赖关系。

Result: 不同过剩面积和初始取向显著影响椭球状红细胞的动力学轨迹；不稳定性临界依赖于剪切模量、弯曲模量、内外黏度比及过剩面积（主要通过膜张力）；长时尺度下观察到膜张力饱和与过剩面积再分布。

Conclusion: 该理论框架揭示了红细胞在外部流动中呈现 stomatocyte 和 trilobe 形状的机制，为理解微循环中红细胞的形变不稳定性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Red blood cells (RBCs) are essential for oxygen transport, and their remarkable ability to undergo significant deformations during flow is a crucial feature for their physiological function. At intermediate shear rates typical of the microcirculation, RBCs can adopt complex, multi-lobed shapes, signifying a dynamic instability. Here we adopt a perturbative theoretical framework of a quasi-spherical RBC under external shear flow to study such shape instabilities. To better capture RBC maturation and enucleation, we first extend the framework to explicitly account for different excess areas between the stress-free and current membrane shapes. We revisit the reduced equations of motion obtained for an ellipsoidally-shaped RBC, and demonstrate the effect of different excess areas and initial orientation on the dynamical trajectories. Then, we introduce additional spatial modes and show that an emerging instability critically depends on the RBC's shear and bending moduli, the internal to external viscosity ratio, and the excess area, mainly through the RBC's membrane tension. We also study the instability-induced saturation of the membrane tension, and the resulting excess area redistribution at long times. The theoretical framework and the emerging picture of the different instabilities provide insights into the emergence of stomatocyte and trilobe shapes exhibited by RBCs under external flow.

### [94] [Pore-shape and its spatial organization control intrinsic permeability of porous media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19098)
*Wenqiao Jiao,Isaac Pincus,Chiara Recalcati,Alberto Guadagnini,Pietro de Anna*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过孔隙尺度流动模拟，研究了死端孔隙（dead-end pores）的密度、深度和取向对多孔介质固有渗透率（intrinsic permeability）的影响，发现死端孔隙沿渗流路径的密度增加会增强渗透率，而深度和取向影响可忽略，并提出将死端孔隙空间结构与宏观渗透率关联的有效公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多孔介质的结构，尤其是空间变异性，已知控制系统的固有渗透率。死端孔隙普遍存在于多孔介质中，但通常被视为水力学上不活跃的区域，其影响被认为可忽略或被吸收到有效孔隙度（effective porosity）描述中。本文旨在量化死端孔隙对固有渗透率的贡献，超越其对总孔隙体积的单纯影响。

Method: 采用孔隙尺度流动模拟（pore-scale flow simulations），在不同死端孔隙结构（包括非均匀排列、受控颗粒组装和最小单通道模型）上进行计算。通过该策略，在保持传输网络不变的前提下，孤立研究死端孔隙密度、深度和取向对系统宏观渗透率的影响。

Result: 死端孔隙可影响固有渗透率：沿渗流路径（percolating flow paths）增加死端孔隙密度会增强渗透率，而孔隙深度和连接处取向的影响可忽略。渗透率增强的机制源于传输孔隙与死端孔隙连接处（junction）的局部水动力学相互作用（localized hydrodynamic interactions）。

Conclusion: 基于结果，提出一个有效公式（effective formulation），将死端孔隙相对于传输网络的密度和空间组织与宏观渗透率相关联。死端孔隙结构提供了超越孔隙度（porosity）和孔径统计（pore-size statistics）的额外几何控制因素，可用于更准确地预测多孔介质的渗透特性。

Abstract: The structure of a porous material, and in particular its spatial variability, is known to control the intrinsic permeability of the system. We investigate how dead-end pores influence the intrinsic permeability of a porous medium beyond their contribution to total pore volume. Dead-end pores are ubiquitous in porous media, yet they are often treated as hydraulically inactive regions whose influence is assumed to be negligible or absorbed into effective-porosity descriptions. We perform pore-scale flow simulations across different dead-end pore structures, including heterogeneous arrangements, controlled granular assemblies, and a minimal single-channel model to study their impact on the system macroscopic permeability. This strategy allows us to isolate the effects of dead-end pore density, depth, and orientation while preserving the transmitting network. We find that dead-end pores can influence intrinsic permeability: increasing the density of dead-end pores along percolating flow paths enhances permeability, whereas pore depth and junction orientation have negligible effects. The observed permeability enhancement originates from localized hydrodynamic interactions at junctions between transmitting and dead-end pores. Based on these results, we propose an effective formulation that relates the density and spatial organization of dead-end pores relative to the transmitting network to macroscopic permeability. Our findings show that dead-end pore architecture provides an additional geometric control on intrinsic permeability beyond porosity and pore-size statistics.

</details>

### [95] [Stable size-biasing and the positive scale-mixture order of generalized Gaussian laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18458)
*Domingos S. P. Salazar*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明：对于中心化单位尺度广义高斯随机变量 $X_r \sim N_r(0,1)$，$X_p$ 可表示为 $X_q$ 乘以一个独立正随机变量 $V$ 当且仅当 $p \le q$，并给出了 $p<q$ 情形下 $V$ 的显式构造（基于 $\alpha$-稳定分布和 size-biased 变换）。该因子律构成乘法余链（multiplicative cocycle），证明了 Dytso 等人提出的 Mellin 商在 $p \le q$ 时为正定，从而完成了广义高斯分布的正尺度混合分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dytso, Bustin, Poor 和 Shamai 在研究广义高斯分布时发现了一个 Mellin 商（Mellin quotient）$\Phi_{p,q}$，但其正定性（positive definiteness）范围和对应的尺度混合（scale mixture）表示尚未被完整刻画。本文旨在严格确定 $X_p \stackrel{d}{=} V X_q$ 成立的参数条件，并给出 $V$ 的显式构造。

Method: 首先证明存在性条件：利用矩方法和特征函数分析，证明 $X_p \stackrel{d}{=} V X_q$ 成立当且仅当 $p \le q$。对于 $p<q$ 情形，设 $a=1/p$, $b=1/q$, $\alpha = p/q$，引入正 $\alpha$-稳定随机变量 $S_\alpha$，构造 $W_0 = S_\alpha^{-b}$，再取其 size-biased 版本（size-biased version）$W$，最终定义 $V_{p,q} = 2^{a-b}W$。对于 $p>q$ 情形，利用斯特林公式（Stirling's formula）证明候选 Mellin 商无界，不能作为特征函数。

Result: 严格证明了 $X_p \stackrel{d}{=} V X_q$ 成立当且仅当 $p \le q$，且 $V$ 的分布唯一。$p<q$ 时构造的 $V_{p,q}$ 满足乘法余链关系 $V_{p,r} \stackrel{d}{=} V_{p,q} V_{q,r}$（$p \le q \le r$，右侧因子独立），这意味着 $\Phi_{p,q}$ 在 $p \le q$ 时为正定，其逆傅里叶-梅林候选密度为合法概率密度。已知高斯基（Gaussian-base）和有界参数乘积（bounded-parameter product）情形被统一纳入该正尺度混合分类。

Conclusion: 本文完整刻画了广义高斯分布之间的尺度混合关系，证明了 Mellin 商的正定性恰好对应于 $p \le q$ 这一参数范围，并为 Dytso 等人提出的候选密度提供了严格的正则性证明。这一结果将分散的已知特例统一为一个完整的正尺度混合分类体系。

Abstract: Let $X_r\sim N_r(0,1)$ be the centered unit-scale generalized Gaussian random variable with density proportional to $\exp(-|x|^r/2)$. We prove that, for $p,q>0$, there exists a strictly positive random variable $V$, independent of $X_q$, such that $X_p\stackrel{d}{=}VX_q$ if and only if $p\le q$. Moreover, the law of $V$ is unique. For $p<q$, put $a=1/p$, $b=1/q$, and $α=b/a=p/q$. If $S_α$ is a positive $α$-stable random variable with Laplace transform $\mathbb{E}\exp(-uS_α)=\exp(-u^α)$, set $W_0=S_α^{-b}$, let $W$ be the $W_0$-size-biased version of $W_0$, and define $V_{p,q}=2^{a-b}W$. Then $X_p\stackrel{d}{=}V_{p,q}X_q$. For $p>q$, the required Mellin quotient, viewed as the candidate characteristic function of $\log V$, is unbounded by Stirling's formula, and hence cannot be a characteristic function. The factor laws form a multiplicative cocycle, $V_{p,r}\stackrel{d}{=}V_{p,q}V_{q,r}$, for $p\le q\le r$, where the factors on the right-hand side are independent copies. Thus the Mellin quotient isolated by Dytso, Bustin, Poor and Shamai is realized constructively throughout the $p<q$ branch. In particular, $Φ_{p,q}$ is positive definite exactly in the range $p\le q$, and the inverse Fourier--Mellin candidate density in the remaining $p<q$ branch is a genuine nonnegative probability density. The known Gaussian-base and bounded-parameter product cases are recovered as parts of a single positive scale-mixture classification.

</details>

### [96] [Magnetic field induced transition from nodeless to nodal superconductivity in $β$-PdBi$_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18482)
*Emmanouil K. Kokkinis,Joseph J. Betouras,Andrey V. Chubukov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文针对β-PdBi₂中磁场诱导从全能隙超导到节线超导的相变现象，发展了多带超导微观理论。通过考虑自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和塞曼劈裂（Zeeman splitting），发现体系存在s波和p波两个吸引配对通道。零磁场下s波占优，有限磁场下费米面劈裂使s波失稳，转变为p波；更高磁场下p波多带超导体的激发谱出现无隙节线（nodal points），解释了实验观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上已在β-PbBi₂中观测到磁场诱导从全能隙超导到节线超导的相变，但缺乏相应的微观理论解释。本文旨在发展一个多带超导微观理论，以揭示该相变的配对机制与物理根源。

Method: 构建了包含自旋-轨道耦合和塞曼劈裂的多带超导微观模型；分析了不同配对通道（s波与p波）的自由能竞争；通过考察费米面劈裂随磁场的变化，推导出能隙对称性转变及激发谱无隙化的条件。

Result: 零磁场下s波配对能量更优；有限磁场下费米面劈裂导致s波通道失稳，p波配对胜出；更高磁场下p波多带超导体的激发谱出现无隙行为，节线定位于劈裂的费米面之间。

Conclusion: 所提出的多带超导理论中p波配对机制与磁场诱导节线超导的行为，能够解释β-PdBi₂中实验观测到的磁场诱导从全能隙到节线超导的相变。

Abstract: Recent tunneling measurements on $β$-PdBi$_2$ reported a magnetic field induced phase transition from a fully gapped to a nodal superconducting state. We develop a microscopic theory of superconductivity in this multi-band material, taking into account spin-orbit coupling and Zeeman splitting. We show that there are two attractive pairing channels in this system: an s-wave and a p-wave. At zero magnetic field, s-wave superconductivity wins. At a finite field, this channel becomes less favorable because Fermi surfaces split, and the gap symmetry changes to p-wave. We show that at a higher field, the excitation spectrum of a p-wave multi-band superconductor becomes gapless, with nodal points located in between the split Fermi surfaces. We argue that this behavior accounts for the experimentally observed field-induced nodal superconductivity in $β$-PdBi$_2$.

### [97] [Time-resolved synchronization analysis of stacked intrinsic Josephson junctions of a cuprate superconductor with frequency-modulated terahertz radiation spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18563)
*Masashi Miyamoto,Keisuke Mizoguchi,Ryota Kobayashi,Nozomi Yagyu,Manabu Tsujimoto,Itsuhiro Kakeya*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究对与贴片天线耦合的Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ本征约瑟夫森结（IJJs）的调频太赫兹发射器进行光谱分析，发现双高斯峰结构及亚纳秒级非平衡动力学。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对与贴片天线（patch antennas）耦合的调频约瑟夫森等离子体发射器进行光谱分析（spectral analysis），测量未调制强度分布I_UM(ω)及不同调制频率f_m下的光谱；利用I_UM(ω)与频率梳（frequency combs）的乘积拟合低f_m下的光谱，并引入同步化弛豫时间τ_s定量描述光谱变换。

Result: 未调制强度分布I_UM(ω)呈现双高斯峰结构（double Gaussian peak structure）；低调制频率f_m下，光谱可由I_UM(ω)与频率梳的乘积很好拟合，得到同步化弛豫时间τ_s≃0.28 ns；引入τ_s可定量再现f_m∼1 GHz附近的光谱剧烈转变，揭示了耦合约瑟夫森等离子体的亚纳秒非平衡动力学（sub-nanosecond non-equilibrium dynamics）。

Conclusion: 双峰光谱表明存在快速时间分布的共振或由IJJ台面与天线间电磁耦合驱动的同步激发；亚纳秒尺度的弛豫时间揭示了耦合约瑟夫森等离子体体系的非平衡动力学特征。

Abstract: Terahertz radiation from $\text{Bi}_2\text{Sr}_2\text{CaCu}_2\text{O}_{8+δ}$ intrinsic Josephson junctions (IJJs) provides an ideal platform to study the synchronization of a macroscopic quantum system. Here, we present a spectral analysis of a frequency-modulated Josephson plasma emitter coupled with patch antennas. In the unmodulated intensity distribution as a function of radiation frequency $I_{\mathrm{UM}}(ω)$, we observe a double Gaussian peak structure. Crucially, double-peak spectra obtained at a constant bias voltage imply either a rapid temporal distribution of resonances or their simultaneous excitation, driven by the mutual electromagnetic coupling between the IJJ mesa and the antennas. At low modulation frequencies $f_m$, the spectra are well reproduced by the products of $I_{\mathrm{UM}}(ω)$ and frequency combs, yielding a synchronized relaxation time $τ_s \simeq 0.28\text{ ns}$. Incorporating $τ_s$ quantitatively reproduces a drastic spectral transformation observed around $f_m \sim 1\text{ GHz}$, unveiling the sub-nanosecond non-equilibrium dynamics of coupled Josephson plasma.

### [98] [Counterintuitive inverse superconducting transition beyond 4He-cooling limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18683)
*Haowen Han,Yi Bian,Tong Ma,Yusong Zhao,Nuofu Chen,Chuanying Xi,Ze Wang,Binghui Ge,Hongliang Dong,Jia-Cai Nie,Ho-Kwang Mao,Jikun Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究报告了在Eu基无限层镍氧化物（EuxNd1-xNiO2和EuxPr1-xNiO2）中观测到高于4He制冷极限的场调制逆超导转变（field-modulated inverse-superconducting-transition），其中零电阻超导态被限制在逆临界温度（Tc-inv，2.6-5.4 K）与另一个更高的正常态临界温度之间。该逆超导转变不仅由升温驱动，还受电流密度调控，并通过Eu²⁺ 4f⁷相关补偿引起的有效磁场（effective magnetic field）与上临界场（upper-critical-field）之间的温度依赖性交替主导来解释。此外，在磁场下低于300 mK时重新出现的超导电性揭示了前所未有的温度诱导重入超导（reentrant superconductivity），为逆转热退相干范式（thermal-decoherence paradigm）的量子现象提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热驱动量子序（thermally driven quantum-orders）在少数特例中的观测表明，热涨落（thermal fluctuation）可能从退相干（decoherence）源转变为相干态工程（coherent-state engineering）的资源。然而，此前在CeCu2Si2、ErRh4B4等材料中发现的升温触发超导电性，其逆临界温度（Tc-inv）均低于开尔文（Kelvin）量级，严重限制了实际应用，因此亟需寻找更高临界温度的超导体系。

Method: 本文在过掺杂（overdoped）和欠掺杂（underdoped）两种掺杂条件下，于衬底上生长Eu基无限层镍氧化物（EuxNd1-xNiO2和EuxPr1-xNiO2）薄膜，通过施加磁场调制，观测逆超导转变（inverse-superconducting-transition）的温度与电流密度依赖关系，并测量低于300 mK时磁场下的重入超导行为。

Result: 零电阻超导态被限制在Tc-inv（2.6-5.4 K）与另一个更高的正常态临界温度之间，前者随磁场升高而升高，后者随磁场升高而降低。逆超导转变不仅可由温度升高驱动，还受电流密度调控，在更高的温度和电流阈值处超导电性消失。在磁场下低于300 mK时，观测到超导电性的重新出现，形成温度诱导的重入超导（reentrant superconductivity）。

Conclusion: 上述结果表明，磁相互作用重构的高温超导（high-Tc）体系可作为探索逆转热退相干范式（thermal-decoherence paradigm）的量子现象的有效平台，并为量子相变器件（quantum-phase-transition devices）提供反直觉设计（antithetical-designs）思路，开拓此前未被开发的应用场景。

Abstract: Thermally driven quantum-orders observed in exceptional instances may redefine the role of thermal-fluctuation from a source of decoherence to a resource for coherent-state engineering. While preliminary signs of counterintuitive temperature-rise-triggered superconductivity manifested in CeCu2Si2, ErRh4B4, Ho1.2Mo6S8 and (La,Ce)Al2, their critical-temperatures (Tc-inv) remain below Kelvin-range, precluding substantial applications. Here, we report field-modulated inverse-superconducting-transitions above 4He-cooling-limit in Eu-based infinite-layer nickelates (EuxNd1-xNiO2 and EuxPr1-xNiO2) grown on a substrate under both overdoped and underdoped regimes. Paradigmatically, superconductivity with zero-resistance is confined between Tc-inv (2.6-5.4 K) and another higher normal-Tc, rising and decreasing with applied magnetic-field, respectively. Starting from the resistive-state below Tc-inv, the inverse-superconducting-transition is driven by not only temperature-rising, but also current-density, while superconductivity further vanishes at higher temperature and current thresholds. The Kelvin-range inverse superconducting transition is plausibly explained by temperature-induced alternating dominance of effective magnetic-fields arising from Eu2+4f7 related compensations relative to the upper-critical-field. Furthermore, an extended-phenomenological-framework is also supported by reemerged superconductivity below 300 mK under magnetic-field, giving rise to an unprecedented temperature-induced reentrant superconductivity. Our findings establish magnetic-interaction-reconfigured high-Tc systems as fertile platforms for exploring quantum phenomena that reverse thermal-decoherence paradigm, also enabling antithetical-designs to unlock untapped application-scenarios for quantum-phase-transition devices.

</details>


### [99] [The electric-field-driven intermediate state of three-dimensional superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18931)
*Ion Cojocari,Enzo Andreani,Paola Verniere,Florian Pallier,Marc Gabay,Miguel Monteverde,Claire Marrache-Kikuchi,Shamashis Sengupta*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过实验证明，在三维无图案超导系统中存在一种中间态，其中电场穿透系统而超导电性仍然保持，表现为超电流与耗散性电荷输运同时存在的非经典行为，该状态由电场驱动的序参量涨落产生，为研究远离平衡态带电量子流体的耗散态提供了平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导电性（superconductivity）与有限电场（finite electric fields）的共存可能打开通往奇异电子态的通道，但目前对此类中间态的认识尚不清晰，亟需实验验证。

Method: 在无图案（unpatterned）的三维（three-dimensional）超导系统中进行测量，通过施加电场并监测超电流与耗散性电荷输运的共存信号，捕捉序参量涨落驱动的非经典中间态。

Result: 观测到一个非经典区（nonclassical regime），其中超电流与耗散性电荷输运同时存在，电场穿透系统而超导电性并未被完全破坏。

Conclusion: 电场驱动的序参量涨落（order parameter fluctuations）是该中间态的起源；这一发现为探索远离平衡态（far from equilibrium）的带电量子流体（charged quantum fluids）的耗散态提供了实验平台。

Abstract: The coexistence of superconductivity and finite electric fields may enable access to intriguing forms of electronic states. We demonstrate the emergence of an intermediate state in which electric fields penetrate the system while superconductivity still persists. Our measurements reveal a nonclassical regime characterized by the simultaneous presence of supercurrent and dissipative charge transport. This state, realized in a pristine unpatterned three-dimensional system, arises from electric-field-driven order parameter fluctuations. It provides a platform to explore dissipative states of charged quantum fluids far from equilibrium.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为钙（Ca）嵌入石墨（C）需要高温条件，室温下极难发生。本文旨在验证钠（Na）催化能否在室温下实现CaC₆的形成，并探索该过程的超导特性及其潜在应用。

Method: 将Ca、Na与石墨混合，在室温下存储，利用超导抗磁性的逐步发展以及X射线衍射峰的出现来确认CaC₆的形成。

Result: 室温存储下观测到CaC₆的形成，其超导转变温度随时间增加而升高，且CaC₆的生成量与存储时间的平方根成正比。

Conclusion: Na催化使得室温下形成超导CaC₆成为可能，这一发现为超导机理和CaC₆的Na催化形成机制提供了新见解，并突显了该室温插层过程在Ca离子电池电极材料等实际应用中的潜力。

Abstract: Calcium (Ca) insertion into graphite (C) has been considered to require elevated temperatures, and its occurrence at room temperature (RT) has been regarded as highly unlikely. Here, we demonstrate that sodium (Na) catalysis enables the formation of superconducting CaC$_6$ even at RT. In mixtures of Ca, Na, and graphite, the gradual development of superconducting diamagnetism and the emergence of X-ray diffraction peaks confirm the formation of CaC$_6$ during storage at RT. The superconducting transition temperature increases with storage time, and the amount of CaC$_6$ scales proportionally to the square root of storage time. These findings provide new insights into the mechanism of superconductivity and Na-catalyzed formation of CaC$_6$, and highlight the potential of this RT intercalation process for practical applications such as electrode materials in Ca-ion batteries.

### [101] [Controlling magnetic domain walls with supercurrents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19078)
*Tim Kokkeler,Risto Ojajärvi,F. Sebastian Bergeret,Tero T. Heikkilä*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于超导体/磁性绝缘体双层结构中超流驱动自旋积累的新机制，利用吉尔伯特阻尼实现磁畴壁运动，从而为低温计算提供低功耗、可识别的磁存储器方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有室温磁性存储器在低温环境下无法工作或功耗过高，成为低温计算（cryogenic computing）的主要瓶颈。超导自旋电子学（superconducting spintronics）旨在通过等自旋三重态超流驱动磁存储器来克服该瓶颈，但铁磁体中自旋弛豫长度短且各向异性强，阻碍了这一路径。

Method: 在超导体/磁性绝缘体（superconductor/magnetic insulator bilayer）双层结构中，超流驱动的自旋积累（spin accumulation）与吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）共同作用，诱导磁畴壁（magnetic domain walls）运动。通过测量畴壁上的局域电压来识别其位置。

Result: 畴壁运动伴随局域电压产生，从而可识别其位置。该过程中焦耳功率（Joule power）通过吉尔伯特阻尼耗散，维持畴壁运动所需功率比正常态（normal state）低数个数量级。

Conclusion: 该机制为低温计算提供了低功耗、可识别位置的磁存储器方案，有望突破超导自旋电子学在铁磁体中面临的自旋弛豫短和各向异性强的限制。

Abstract: Establishing a versatile, fast and reliable magnetic memory technology is a giant bottleneck for cryogenic computing since present-day room-temperature solutions either cease to work or consume too much power. The long-term goal of superconducting spintronics has been to overcome this bottleneck by generating magnetic memories with equal-spin triplet supercurrent driven through them to control their magnetization direction. This path has been hampered by the short spin relaxation length and strong anisotropy in ferromagnets. Here we show how the supercurrent driven generation of spin accumulation in a superconductor/magnetic insulator bilayer, together with Gilbert damping of magnetization lead to a motion of magnetic domain walls. This manifests as a local voltage across the wall, which allows its position to be identified. Associated with this voltage and the current, there is Joule power which is dissipated via the Gilbert damping. The power required to maintain domain wall motion is orders of magnitude smaller than in the normal state, where most of the power is wasted in producing the current.

### [102] [Evidence for Multiband Superconductivity in 2H-NbSeS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19107)
*K. Yadav,M. Lamba K. Bhattacharya,M. Majumder,S. Patnaik*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过研究混合硫族元素化合物2H-NbSeS，发现其超导态具有双能隙特征，表明2H-NbSe2中观察到的多能隙超导现象本质上源于电荷密度波（CDW）对费米面的重构而非内禀多带配对。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 2H-NbSe2中超导性质的本质存在长期争论：角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）数据支持多带超导，而扫描隧道显微镜（STM）数据则指向强各向异性单带超导，后者中CDW序模拟了多能隙特征。由于CDW对费米面进行重构并改变超导能隙分布，难以区分内禀多带配对与CDW相关效应。

Method: 制备了混合硫族元素单晶2H-NbSeS，其中随机的Se/S替代抑制了长程CDW序，同时保持P63/mmc层状晶体结构。通过测量上临界场、下临界场、超流密度和电子比热，并采用脏极限双带模型（dirty-limit two-band model）对数据进行拟合分析。

Result: 2H-NbSeS在6.0 K以下进入超导态，具有适中的磁各向异性。上临界场呈现显著的上翘曲率，无法用单带框架描述，但被大扩散率比的脏极限双带模型很好地捕捉，表明存在强带依赖散射。面内上临界场超过弱耦合帕乌利极限（Pauli limit）。下临界场、超流密度和电子比热测量结果与具有两个不同大小的无能节点（nodeless）能隙的全能隙超导态解释一致。

Conclusion: 2H-NbSeS的超导行为支持双能隙超导图像，这暗示2H-NbSe2中观察到的多能隙特征可能由CDW效应诱导，而非内禀多带配对。

Abstract: The nature of superconductivity in 2H-NbSe2 has generated sustained debate in the recent past. While angle resolved photoemission spectroscopy data have been interpreted as evidence for multiband superconductivity, the data from scanning tunneling microscope experiments relate to strongly anisotropic single-band superconductivity. In the later case, the charge density wave (CDW) order mimics the multigap character. Because the CDW reconstructs the Fermi surface and modifies the superconducting gap distribution, disentangling intrinsic multiband pairing from CDW-related effects is challenging. To address this issue, we investigate single-crystalline 2H-NbSeS, a mixed-chalcogen analogue of 2H-NbSe2 in which random Se/S substitution suppresses long-range CDW order while preserving the layered crystal structure P63/mmc. The material becomes superconducting below 6.0 K with moderate magnetic anisotropy. The upper critical field exhibits a pronounced upward curvature that cannot be described within a single-band framework but is well captured by a dirty-limit two-band model with a large diffusivity ratio. This indicates strong band-dependent scattering. The in-plane upper critical field exceeds the weak-coupling Pauli limit. Measurements of the lower critical field, superfluid density, and electronic specific heat are consistent with an interpretation of a fully gapped superconducting state with two nodeless gaps of different magnitudes.

### [103] [Cavity Enhanced Superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19171)
*Hanxiang Zhang,Zexin Feng,I-Te Lu,Zhiwei Li,Songhao Guo,Qiuyu Shang,Dening Luan,Mingcheng Panmai,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Angel Rubio,Weibo Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过在太赫兹（terahertz）腔中耦合少层二硒化铌（NbSe₂），首次实验证明了真空电磁场可以增强超导性（superconductivity），使三层NbSe₂的超导转变温度从3.02 K提升至3.41 K（约10%）。增强效应具有空间依赖性和非单调频率依赖性，在约2 THz时达到最大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然腔诱导的超导性修改已被广泛理论预测，但此前实验研究仅报道了超导性质的抑制。本文旨在通过精确调控太赫兹腔与少层NbSe₂中关键声子模式（phononic modes）的共振，验证真空电磁场能否实现超导增强。

Method: 将少层NbSe₂耦合到互补开环谐振器（complementary split-ring resonator）上，精细调节太赫兹腔使其与关键声子模式共振，并测量不同腔共振频率和空间位置下的超导转变温度。

Result: 在2.04 THz共振腔中，三层NbSe₂的超导转变温度从3.02 K升至3.41 K（~10%增强）。增强效应在空间上随腔场分布变化，在频率上呈非单调依赖，于约2 THz附近达到峰值。

Conclusion: 该结果提供了真空电磁场可增强超导性的实验证据，将腔工程（cavity engineering）确立为调控量子材料（quantum materials）的有力平台。

Abstract: Vacuum electromagnetic fluctuations have recently emerged as a promising means of controlling collective quantum phases. Although cavity-induced modifications of superconductivity have been widely predicted, experimental studies have so far reported only suppression of superconducting properties. Here, by carefully tuning a terahertz cavity to resonate with key phononic modes in few-layer niobium diselenide (NbSe2), we demonstrate cavity-enhanced superconductivity in few-layer NbSe2 coupled to a complementary split-ring resonator. In trilayer NbSe2, the superconducting transition temperature increases by ~10%, from 3.02 K to 3.41 K, when coupled to a cavity resonant at 2.04 THz. The enhancement exhibits a clear spatial dependence following the cavity field profile and a non-monotonic frequency dependence, with maximal enhancement near 2 THz. These results provide experimental evidence that vacuum electromagnetic fields can enhance superconductivity and establish cavity engineering as a powerful platform for tailoring quantum materials.

Abstract: Advances in novel materials science enable structures to function as intelligent machines by embedding memory and learning capabilities directly into materials. These material actuators are assembled into a motor unit-like structure inspired by muscle contraction trigger, forming an intelligent machine capable of dynamic shading control that can be used, for example, in buildings. The machine is governed by a neural network trained on over 350 experimental data points collected under diverse environmental conditions. By establishing a new data-aware backpropagation training, we show that the machine predicts shading responses and learns to predict appropriate behaviour incrementally as the database expands. We also demonstrate the ability of the machine to optimise configurations to achieve similar shading outputs under two distinct conditions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）背景下，给出了功（work）、热量（heat）和熵产生（entropy production）的轨迹级（trajectory-level）定义，并推广了Jarzynski恒等式（Jarzynski identity）和类第二定律不等式（second-law-like inequality），将原始Jarzynski框架扩展至时变浴温度（time-dependent bath temperature）和非保守驱动力（nonconservative driving forces）情形。

Result: 建立了基于SDE的生成模型与随机热力学之间的理论联系，提出了轨迹层面的热力学量定义，并获得了推广的Jarzynski恒等式和类第二定律不等式。

Conclusion: 该热力学视角有助于从非平衡统计力学角度加深对扩散模型和薛定谔桥的理解。

Abstract: SDE-based generative models, including diffusion models and the Schrödinger bridge, have found broad applications in signal processing tasks such as speech enhancement, image restoration, and time-series generation. This note presents a modeling framework for such models within the context of stochastic thermodynamics. The main results of this note are trajectory-level definitions of work, heat, and entropy production, along with a generalized Jarzynski identity and a second-law-like inequality. The proposed framework extends the original Jarzynski setup to accommodate time-dependent bath temperature and nonconservative driving forces. This thermodynamic perspective may deepen our understanding of diffusion models and the Schrödinger bridge from a nonequilibrium statistical mechanics viewpoint.

### [106] [Classical dissipative search of unstructured database](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18835)
*A. E. Allahverdyan,Y. Bisharyan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于经典耗散球型自旋模型（dissipative model of spherical spins）的物理实现，用于无结构数据库搜索，通过自旋耦合实现数据库编码，并证明其搜索速度在标度律上优于量子Grover搜索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索经典耗散模拟计算机在无结构数据库搜索问题上是否能够超越量子酉计算机（quantum unitary computer）的已知界限，即Grover搜索的O(√M)速度。

Method: 采用经典耗散球型自旋模型，通过自旋-自旋耦合（spin-spin couplings）编码数据库，选定的耦合对应两个选定自旋之间的铁磁相互作用（ferromagnetic interaction）；系统从均匀初始状态通过朗之万方程（Langevin equations）描述的弛豫过程演化至低温平衡态。

Result: 低温平衡态下，磁化强度（magnetization）高度集中在选定的自旋上，表明搜索是完备的。搜索时间对应弛豫时间，标度为O(M^a)，其中a < 1/2，M为数据库体积（database volume）。

Conclusion: 该经典耗散模拟方法在搜索速度上快于量子Grover搜索，表明经典耗散模拟计算机可以超越量子酉计算机在该任务上的性能。

Abstract: We propose a physical realization of the unstructured database search that works via classical, dissipative model of spherical spins. The database is implemented via spin-spin couplings, where the selected coupling refers to a larger ferromagnetic interaction between two selected spins. The low-temperature equilibrium of this model leads to magnetization strongly concentrated on the selected spins, which means that the search is complete. The search time refers to the relaxation time to equilibrium from a homogeneous initial state, and is described via Langevin equations. This time scales as ${\cal O}(M^a)$ with $a<1/2$, where $M$ is the database volume. This is faster than Grover's search, showing how a dissipative, classical analog computer can overcome the quantum unitary computer.

### [107] [Thermodynamics of photonic nonlinear Aharonov-Bohm cages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18896)
*Stefano Iubini,Carlo Danieli*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有Kerr非线性的二维光子钻石晶格（photonic diamond lattice）在平衡态与非平衡态下的热力学行为，发现合成磁通（synthetic magnetic flux）可在线性区诱导Aharonov-Bohm笼蔽（Aharonov-Bohm caging）使系统绝缘，而非线性可打破该笼蔽恢复导电性；在适中的非线性强度下，笼蔽条件反而增强了塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）和热电优值（thermoelectric figure of merit），揭示了一条通过合成磁通调控线性与非线性输运通道来优化耦合输运器件的新路线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用合成磁通调控光子钻石晶格中线性与非线性输运通道的机制，以优化热电耦合输运器件的性能。

Method: 通过理论分析研究一维光子钻石晶格在Kerr非线性下的平衡态相图与非平衡稳态热电输运，系统边界施加固定的温度差和化学势差，分析不同非线性强度下磁通对输运性质的影响。

Result: 磁通可在线性区诱导Aharonov-Bohm笼蔽，使所有Bloch带（Bloch band）平坦化并抑制粒子流与能量流；非线性可在此笼蔽区恢复非零电流；弱非线性下精细调节磁通到笼蔽条件可将系统从导体转变为绝缘体；中等非线性下，系统在所有磁通下保持导电，但笼蔽条件显著提升塞贝克系数与热电优值。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，通过合成磁通调控线性与非线性输运通道，可实现热电性能的增强，为设计新型耦合输运器件提供了新思路。

Abstract: We investigate equilibrium and non-equilibrium thermodynamics of one-dimensional photonic diamond lattices with Kerr nonlinearity. The equilibrium phase diagram is obtained as a function of the synthetic magnetic flux acting on each plaquette. In the linear regime, the magnetic flux can induce Aharonov-Bohm caging, flattening all Bloch bands and suppressing particle and energy currents. In this caging regime, non-vanishing currents are enabled by nonlinearity. By imposing stationary temperature- and chemical potential- imbalances at the system boundaries, we show that at weak nonlinearity fine tuning the flux at the Aharonov-Bohm caging transforms the system from a conductor to an insulator. For intermediate nonlinear strength, the system remains conducting for all magnetic fluxes; however, the caging condition significantly enhances the Seebeck coefficient and thermoelectric figure of merit, improving the thermoelectric features of the system. Our results give evidence of a novel route towards optimization of coupled transport devices, based on the control of linear versus nonlinear conduction channels via a synthetic magnetic flux.

</details>


### [108] [Nonequilibrium nucleation theory for nonconserved fields: from active matter to population dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18911)
*Michalis Chatzittofi,Noah Ziethen,Cesare Nardini,Michael E. Cates*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对非守恒序参量系统构建了非平衡成核理论（NNT），揭示了界面密度分布偏差对成核势垒的深刻影响，并通过反应坐标投影方法给出解析预测，与数值模拟高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典成核理论（CNT）仅适用于平衡体系，而现有的非平衡成核理论（NNT）局限于守恒序参量（conserved order parameter）情形（如活性流体相分离）。本文旨在为非守恒序参量（nonconserved order parameter）系统建立通用的NNT框架。

Method: 通过重新定义反应坐标（reaction coordinate）即液滴半径（droplet radius），将界面密度分布（interfacial density profile）在确定性液滴弛豫（deterministic droplet relaxation）与非平衡噪声驱动生长之间的偏差投影掉，从而解析分析成核势垒（nucleation barrier）。

Result: 在非守恒序参量系统中，噪声驱动（noise-driven）液滴生长的成核势垒与守恒情况有本质不同，界面密度分布的偏差会显著改变势垒大小。基于种群动力学（population dynamics）和活性物质（active matter）模型给出的理论预测与数值结果高度吻合。

Conclusion: 成功将非平衡成核理论扩展到非守恒序参量系统，证明界面密度分布偏差是决定势垒的关键因素，且通过恰当的反应坐标定义可实现精确的解析描述。

Abstract: Classical nucleation theory (CNT) describes the formation of a stable phase from a metastable one. In equilibrium systems, it quantifies the free-energy competition between a favorable bulk gain and an unfavorable interfacial cost. For systems without detailed balance, the corresponding nonequilibrium nucleation theory (NNT) was so far developed only for cases with a conserved order parameter, such as active fluid-fluid phase separation. Here we construct the NNT for systems with a (single, scalar) nonconserved order parameter. Unlike in the conserved case, the nucleation barrier controlling (noise-driven) droplet growth is profoundly altered by deviations in the interfacial density profile from the one arising during (deterministic) droplet relaxation. The barrier can nonetheless be analysed by carefully defining the reaction coordinate (droplet radius) to project out those deviations. We give explicit NNT predictions for models drawn from population dynamics and active matter, finding excellent agreement with numerical studies.

</details>


### [109] [Topological spectral form factor reveals emergent non-Hermitian single-particle $\mathcal{PT}$ transitions from many-body quantum chaos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19331)
*Daniel Harkin,Chun Y. Leung,Amos Chan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文定义拓扑谱形因子（topological spectral form factor, TopSFF），通过在双配分函数中插入拓扑缺陷来探测非平衡量子动力学中的相变，并解析证明了其与(3+1)维非厄米单粒子问题的等价性以及PT对称性破缺导致的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平衡态物理中，拓扑缺陷插入（topological defect insertions）提供了超越局域观测量的非微扰探针；非平衡态中，谱形因子（spectral form factor）是描述普适量子动力学的最小探针。本文旨在将拓扑缺陷插入与谱形因子结合，定义一种新的非平衡探针。

Method: 通过在配分函数乘积中插入非平凡作用的拓扑缺陷，定义拓扑谱形因子。对于最小Z₂空间扩展缺陷（即全局交换算符），将一般一维多体混沌系统的TopSFF精确映射为(3+1)维非厄米单粒子问题，描述时间畴壁（temporal domain wall, tDW）动力学。对于时间扩展拓扑缺陷，利用时间反演或时间平移对称性推导出普适标度形式。

Result: 有效tDW动力学在有限相互作用强度ε_EP处发生PT对称性破缺相变：低于ε_EP时，主导模式极化到高斯或非高斯tDW扇区，TopSFF随系统大小单调指数变化；高于ε_EP时，tDW扇区混合，TopSFF随系统大小振荡；在例外点（exceptional point）ε_EP处，约当非对角性（Jordan non-diagonality）产生随系统大小线性的增强。

Conclusion: 拓扑谱形因子提供了一种新的非微扰探针，能够揭示非平衡量子动力学中的PT对称性破缺相变和普适标度行为，并在具有时间反演或时间平移对称性的系统中通过数值模拟验证了解析推导的普适标度形式。

Abstract: In equilibrium physics, topological defect insertions in quantum and classical partition functions provide non-perturbative probes of phase transitions beyond local observables. In non-equilibrium physics, the spectral form factor provides a minimal probe of universal quantum dynamics, and admits a representation as a product of two partition functions at imaginary inverse temperature. We define the topological spectral form factor (TopSFF) by inserting topological defects acting non-trivially on the doubled partition functions, producing mismatched spacetime world-sheet topologies. For the minimal $\mathbb{Z}_2$ spatially extended defect, implemented by the global swap operator, we derive an exact mapping of the TopSFF of a generic 1D many-body chaotic system to an emergent $(3+1)$D non-Hermitian single-particle problem describing a temporal domain wall (tDW). We show analytically that the effective tDW dynamics undergoes a $\mathcal{PT}$ symmetry breaking transition at a finite interaction strength $ε_{\mathrm{EP}}$: below $ε_{\mathrm{EP}}$, the leading modes are polarized into Gaussian or non-Gaussian tDW sectors and the TopSFF varies monotonically and exponentially with system size; above $ε_{\mathrm{EP}}$, the tDW sectors hybridize and the TopSFF oscillates with system size; at the exceptional point $ε_{\mathrm{EP}}$, Jordan non-diagonality produces a linear-in-system-size enhancement. For temporally extended topological defects, we derive exact universal scaling forms for the TopSFF free energy in systems with time reversal or time translation symmetry, and verify them numerically in independent models.

</details>


### [110] [Large-deviation tails of critical order-parameter distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19030)
*Jinhong Zhu,Yihao Xu,Abbas Ali Saberi,Youjin Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本论文通过研究临界渗流（critical percolation）和Fortuin–Kasteleyn (FK) Ising模型在二维、三维晶格及完全图上的大偏差尾（large-deviation tails），揭示了超出标准有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）的普适性特征。研究表明，序参量分布的大偏差尾能捕捉到平均可观测量无法反映的临界涨落普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准有限尺寸标度分析主要关注分布的中心区域，但临界概率分布的大偏差尾可能提供更敏感的普适性探针。作者旨在系统研究这些尾部的标度行为，从而揭示临界涨落中非平凡的全新普适特征。

Method: 研究了两类重整化后的序参量：磁化类变量 $x_m=|M|/\langle |M|\rangle$（对渗流模型还包含有符号的集团质量类比量）和最大集团变量 $x_C=C_1/\langle C_1|\rangle$。对于 $x_m$，测试了预期的拉伸指数大偏差尾形式；对于 $x_C$，基于完全图精确解和标度论证，提出了累积分布双侧尾部的普适标度形式，并通过大规模蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟进行检验。

Result: $x_m$ 的拉伸指数大偏差尾形式得到验证，且该形式同样适用于渗流的集团质量类比量。在完全图FK-Ising模型中，$x_C$ 的左尾由具有渗流类标度的稀有序构主导，而非典型的Ising标度行为。

Conclusion: 序参量分布的大偏差尾揭示了平均可观测量无法捕获的临界涨落普适性特征，提供了超越标准有限尺寸标度的新视角。

Abstract: Large-deviation tails of critical probability distributions provide a sensitive probe of universality beyond standard finite-size scaling. We study these tails for critical percolation and Fortuin--Kasteleyn Ising models on two-dimensional lattices, three-dimensional lattices, and complete graphs. We consider two rescaled order parameters: the magnetization-like variable $x_m=|M|/\langle |M|\rangle$, including a signed cluster-mass analogue for percolation, and the largest-cluster variable $x_C=C_1/\langle C_1\rangle$. For $x_m$, we test the expected stretched-exponential large-deviation tail and show that the same form applies to the percolation analogue. For $x_C$, guided by the exact complete-graph result and scaling arguments, we propose universal scaling forms for both tails of the cumulative distribution and test them by extensive Monte Carlo simulations. In the complete-graph FK-Ising model, the left tail is governed by rare configurations with percolation-like scaling rather than by the typical Ising scaling. Our results show that the tails of order-parameter distributions reveal universal features of critical fluctuations that are not captured by averaged observables alone.

</details>

### [111] [Quantum Geometry and Topology of Bulk Plasmons in Weyl Metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18346)
*Hong-Yi Xie,Peter Abbamonte,Bruno Uchoa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了环绕拓扑荷（topological charge）的费米面中等离激元（plasmon）的量子几何结构，证明Weyl费米子等离激元具有单极子结构、拓扑性质及有限涡量，并发现其与光的耦合具有量子几何起源的选择性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索拓扑材料中等离激元的量子几何（quantum geometry）性质，特别是环绕拓扑荷的费米面（Fermi surface）中等离激元是否具有非平凡的拓扑结构和光学响应特性。

Method: 通过理论分析Weyl费米子等离激元在费米面包围Weyl点情况下的量子几何结构，推导其涡量（vorticity）与陈数（Chern number）之间的关系，并分析等离激元与线性偏振光的耦合机制。

Result: Weyl费米子等离激元具有单极子（monopole）结构，是拓扑的，且具有有限涡量 ζ=2C_w，其中C_w为包围Weyl点的费米面的陈数。该等离激元仅选择性地与沿其有效偶极矩（effective dipole moment）d方向线性偏振的光耦合，而d具有量子几何起源，指向等离激元质心动量Q̂方向。

Conclusion: Weyl金属拓扑等离激元（topological plasmons）相比传统等离激元具有独特的光学性质，为理解拓扑等离激元的光学响应提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We address the quantum geometric structure of plasmons in Fermi surfaces enclosing a topological charge. We demonstrate that Weyl fermion plasmons have monopole structure, are topological and have a finite vorticity $ζ=2\mathsf{C}_{\text{w}}$, where $\mathsf{C}_{\text{w}}$ is the Chern number of the Fermi surface enclosing the Weyl point. We show that these plasmons selectively couple to light linearly polarized along the plasmon effective dipole moment $\mathbf{d}$, which has quantum geometric origin and points along the direction of the plasmon center of mass momentum $\hat{\mathbf{Q}}$. We suggest that Weyl metal topological plasmons have distinctive optical properties compared to conventional plasmons.

</details>


### [112] [Negative diffusivity of excitons in electron-hole plasmas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18401)
*H. Terças,V. N. Mantsevich*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套最小流体动力学（minimal hydrodynamic framework）来描述二维半导体中电子-空穴等离子体（electron-hole plasma）存在下的激子（exciton）输运。研究表明，激子与等离子体之间的动量交换会强烈重整化激子扩散，在考虑等离子体惯性和集体电荷振荡时，激子扩散模式与声学等离子体模式（acoustic plasma modes）杂化，导致动力学不稳定性（dynamical instability），表现为有效负扩散系数（negative diffusion coefficient）。该机制为近期实验中观测到的负激子扩散率提供了统一的物理解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维半导体中激子输运的实验观测发现了异常的负扩散系数现象，但其微观物理起源尚不明确。本文旨在揭示电子-空穴等离子体与激子之间的动量交换及集体动力学效应如何导致这一反常输运行为，建立统一的物理机制。

Method: 将激子、电子和空穴视为耦合流体（coupled fluids），构建最小流体动力学框架。分别分析碰撞主导（collisional regime）和考虑等离子体惯性及集体电荷振荡两种情形下的激子扩散行为。

Result: 在碰撞主导下，互扩散（mutual diffusion）会重新分布输运系数，但激子扩散率保持为正。当计入等离子体惯性和集体电荷振荡时，激子扩散模式与声学等离子体模式杂化，产生动力学不稳定性，表现为有效负扩散系数。该不稳定性源于非平衡态下慢激子与快等离子体自由度之间的耦合，而非非线性扩散或热力学效应。

Conclusion: 本文为近期实验中报告的负激子扩散率提供了统一的物理机制，确立了集体等离子体动力学（collective plasma dynamics）作为二维材料中激子输运的关键控制参数。

Abstract: We develop a minimal hydrodynamic framework to describe exciton transport in the presence of an electron hole plasma in 2D semiconductors. Treating excitons, electrons, and holes as coupled fluids, we show that exciton diffusion is strongly renormalized by momentum exchange with the plasma. In the collisional regime, mutual diffusion leads to a nontrivial redistribution of transport coefficients but preserves the positivity of the exciton diffusivity. In contrast, when plasma inertia and collective charge oscillations are accounted for, the exciton diffusive mode hybridizes with acoustic plasma modes, giving rise to a dynamical instability manifested as an effective negative diffusion coefficient. We demonstrate that this instability originates from the nonequilibrium coupling between slow excitons and fast plasma degrees of freedom, rather than from nonlinear diffusion or thermodynamic effects. Our results provide a unified physical mechanism for negative exciton diffusivity reported in recent experiments and establish collective plasma dynamics as a key control parameter of exciton transport in 2D materials.

</details>


### [113] [Persistent current and orbital magnetization along a valley-contrasting junction in bilayer graphene in a magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18461)
*K. Shizuya*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了门控双层石墨烯中线结（line junction）所束缚的扭结态（kink states）的能谱与电磁响应，发现该扭结态中存在两种谷电流（valley current）：由偏压梯度驱动的漂移电流（drift current）和来自回旋运动的环流电流（circulating current）。两者流向基本一致，环流电流具有区别于其他高能级的磁性特征，在平衡态下形成准一维轨道磁化通道。通过门控结网络对轨道磁化与谷电流进行电控，有望应用于谷电子学（valley electronics）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层石墨烯在磁场中具有由赝零模（pseudo-zero-mode）电子构成的八重态，这些能级在谷和自旋上近乎简并，但可通过静电门控（electrostatic gating）实现谷分裂。当层间偏压（interlayer bias）在一条线上发生符号翻转时，会形成线结（line junction），将部分赝零模电子束缚在绝缘体体带隙内部，产生沿结局域化的电子态——即扭结态（kink states）。本文旨在深入分析这种扭结态的能谱及其电磁响应特性。

Method: 从理论上研究了门控双层石墨烯中线结处形成的扭结态的能谱和电磁响应，分析了与此类扭结态相关的两种谷电流：由偏压梯度驱动的漂移电流和源自回旋运动（cyclotron motion）的环流电流，并比较了它们的方向与磁性特征。

Result: 研究发现，漂移电流与环流电流的流动方向基本一致；环流电流展现出与其他更高能级不同的磁性特征。在平衡态下，环流电流在扭结态内部空间上循环流动，形成准一维（quasi-one-dimensional）的轨道磁化（orbital magnetization）通道。

Conclusion: 通过门控结（gated junction）网络对轨道磁化与谷电流进行电控，将为谷电子学（valley electronics）领域提供有用的应用前景。

Abstract: In a magnetic field bilayer graphene hosts an octet of pseudo-zero-mode electron levels nearly degenerate in orbitals $n=(0,1)$, valleys and spins. They split in valleys by electrostatic gating. In gated bilayer graphene, in which the interlayer bias is set up to flip sign across a line, one has a line junction that traps a portion of pseudo-zero-mode electrons inside the insulating bulk band gap, giving rise to electron states localized along the junction, known as kink states. A close look is made into the spectra and electromagnetic response of such kink states. There are two species of valley current associated with them, a drift current driven by the bias gradient and a circulating current coming from cyclotron motion. It turns out that they both flow in essentially the same direction, with the circulating current exhibiting a magnetic character distinct from those of other higher levels. In equilibrium they spatially circulate within the kink states, creating a quasi-one-dimensional channel of orbital magnetization. The electric control of the orbital magnetization and valley currents via a network of gated junctions will find useful applications in valley electronics.

</details>


### [114] [Magnon-dislon hybridization in magnetic insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18513)
*Carlos Saji,Nicolas Vidal-Silva,Roberto E. Troncoso*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了有序磁体中含拓扑晶格缺陷的自旋动力学，利用分形子-弹性对偶性（fracton–elasticity duality）发展了磁振子（magnon）与量子化位错（dislon）耦合的有效场论，揭示了位错拓扑结构决定的磁振子-位错杂化行为及其对自旋动力学的调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有序磁体中拓扑晶格缺陷（位错）对自旋动力学的影响，旨在建立磁振子与位错耦合的理论框架，并揭示缺陷拓扑如何调控磁激发行为。

Method: 采用分形子-弹性对偶性（fracton–elasticity duality）构建有效场论（effective field theory），将磁振子与绝缘磁体中的量子化位错耦合，引入弹性规范场（elastic gauge field）来中介位错与磁化梯度之间的非定域相互作用。

Result: 螺型位错（screw dislocations）表现出螺旋性选择杂化（helicity-selective hybridization）和对称性保护的暗位错子扇区（symmetry-protected dark dislon sectors）；刃型位错（edge dislocations）通过滑移约束（glide constraint）产生各向异性杂化激发（anisotropic hybrid excitations）和有限的自旋进动椭圆度（spin-precession ellipticity）。

Conclusion: 位错是可在磁振子谱中留下可观测极化指纹（polarization fingerprints）的动态拓扑缺陷，磁振子-位错杂化（magnon-dislon hybridization）为调控自旋动力学提供了新途径。

Abstract: Spin dynamics in ordered magnets with topological lattice defects is investigated. Using fracton--elasticity duality, we develop an effective field theory of magnons coupled to quantized lattice dislocations (dislons) in magnetic insulators. Within this framework, an elastic gauge field mediates a nonlocal interaction between dislocations and magnetization gradients. The resulting magnetoelastic coupling gives rise to coherent magnon-dislon hybridization whose properties are dictated by dislocation topology. Screw dislocations exhibit helicity-selective hybridization and symmetry-protected dark dislon sectors, while edge dislocations generate anisotropic hybrid excitations with finite spin-precession ellipticity through the glide constraint. Our results establish dislocations as dynamical topological defects with directly observable polarization fingerprints in magnon spectra, and reveal magnon-dislon hybridization as a new route to control spin dynamics.

</details>


### [115] [Trion Hall effect in electron-hole double layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18647)
*Raghav Chaturvedi,Phuong X. Nguyen,Patrick Knüppel,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Kin Fai Mak,Jie Shan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道在MoSe₂/WSe₂异质双层中观测到三子（trion）的霍尔效应（Hall effect），该效应源于垂直磁场对三子的洛伦兹力（Lorentz force），并在霍尔拖曳（Hall drag）和标准霍尔测量中均有体现，为三子量子振荡和量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effect）的实现提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在二维半导体异质结构中，通过库仑耦合的电子-空穴双层（electron-hole double layers）实现平衡激子（exciton）流体的热力学与输运研究；进一步掺入额外电子/空穴后形成三子（trion）流体，需要探索这类复合粒子（composite particles）的新输运现象。

Method: 在支持密度可调的库仑耦合电子和空穴流体的MoSe₂/WSe₂异质双层（heterobilayers）中，施加垂直磁场，通过霍尔拖曳测量和单层半导体层的标准霍尔效应测量来观察三子的霍尔效应。

Conclusion: 该工作为实验上实现三子的量子振荡（quantum oscillations）和量子霍尔效应打开了大门。

Abstract: The realization of Coulomb coupled electron-hole double layers in 2D semiconductor heterostructures has enabled the thermodynamic and transport studies of equilibrium exciton fluids without a magnetic field. By doping the exciton fluid with additional electrons/holes, an equilibrium fluid of trions - three particle bound states of electrons and holes - further emerge, providing the platform to explore new transport phenomena associated with such composite particles. Here we report the observation of a Hall effect for trions in MoSe2/WSe2 heterobilayers, which support Coulomb-coupled electron and hole fluids with tunable densities. The Hall effect arises from a Lorentz force on trions under a perpendicular magnetic field. It is manifested in both Hall drag measurements and standard Hall effect measurements on just one of the semiconductor layers. For negatively charged trions, an electron Hall effect is observed even in a hole doped WSe2 monolayer due to the presence of trion drags. The trion Hall effect also disappears when the trions are ionized at elevated temperatures and/or high trion densities. Our work opens the door for realizing quantum oscillations and the quantum Hall effect for trions.

Method: 采用计算模拟方法，研究由电流诱导的自旋转移矩（spin-transfer torque）和自旋轨道矩（spin-orbit torque）驱动的反铁磁斯格明子动力学，并结合Thiele方法（Thiele approach）进行理论分析。

Result: 在低电流密度下反铁磁斯格明子沿单一方向运动，但当驱动电流超过某一阈值时，运动方向发生反转；该双向运动源于自旋转移矩和自旋轨道矩所对应的两种有效力相对强度的变化。

Abstract: Antiferromagnetic skyrmions are swirling topological spin textures with rich dynamics and intriguing transport properties, yet their bidirectional dynamics remain largely unexplored. Here, we investigate the dynamics of antiferromagnetic skyrmions driven by current-induced spin-transfer and spin-orbit torques. We computationally demonstrate that antiferromagnetic skyrmions moving in one direction at low current densities can reverse their motion direction when the driving current is above a threshold. Based on the Thiele approach analysis, we show that this bidirectional motion originates from a change in the relative strengths of two effective forces arising from spin-transfer and spin-orbit torques. Furthermore, exploiting this bidirectional motion on a single racetrack, we design programmable logic gates. Our results not only uncover a hidden mechanism for bidirectional skyrmion motion but also facilitate the development of antiferromagnet-based logic devices.

In particular, the field evolution and the characteristic isotropic ring-type feature of the spin-flip scattering intensity at intermediate momentum transfers are in line with the formation of flux-closure states. Abstract: Characterizing electronic band structures requires precise knowledge of wave functions and their quantum geometry. We consider two-orbital models on a honeycomb lattice, relevant to graphene heterostructures and direct-gap semiconductors. For on-site impurities, backscattering between time-reversed states directly maps the density matrix populations and coherences into distinct orbital contributions in the interference map. While local probes usually lack orbital resolution, these orbital contributions transform under distinct symmetry group representations and can thus be disentangled to reveal the density matrix and quantum geometric tensor of the scattering states. This establishes impurities as tomographic probes for band structures in scanning tunneling microscopy using conventional, unpolarized tips.

Method: 从电流环（current-loop）图像出发，构建面内轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）算符，并基于此推导轨道磁矩（orbital magnetic moment）和面内轨道磁化率（in-plane orbital magnetic susceptibility）的精确表达式。

Abstract: The modern theory of orbital magnetization successfully describes the response of Bloch electrons to magnetic fields in fully periodic crystals, but it does not directly address the distinct regime of an in-plane field in multilayer systems with layer hybridization. Coherent interlayer tunneling allows electrons to form circulating current loops, producing an in-plane orbital response that is absent in a strictly two-dimensional limit and qualitatively different from the conventional three-dimensional one. Here we develop a theory of in-plane orbital magnetization for this {\it transdimensional} regime, where the layer thickness is comparable to the vertical mean free path. Starting from the current-loop picture, we construct the in-plane orbital angular momentum operator and derive exact expressions for the orbital magnetic moment and the in-plane orbital magnetic susceptibility. As an application, we predict a gate-tunable in-plane orbital magnetoelectric effect in layered materials. Our framework establishes a general foundation for in-plane orbital responses and suggests new opportunities for orbitronics in layer-hybridized quantum materials.

### [120] [From Localized Packets to Plane Waves: A Time-Domain Approach to Transport in Mesoscopic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19012)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Landauer–Büttiker散射框架虽然成功描述了介观系统（mesoscopic systems）中的稳态量子输运，但它掩盖了单个费米子激发在时域中的动力学及其建立宏观输运过程的具体机制。

Method: 从二次量子化（second-quantized）表述出发，通过有限输运能量窗上的连续傅里叶变换定义波包产生算符。利用泡利不相容原理（Pauli exclusion principle）强制执行基本时间间隔 $Δt = h/eV$，并基于正交波包严格构造多体费米子态（many-body fermionic state）。

Result: 在该表示下，无噪声电流表现为确定性的电荷携带事件序列，无需动用动量空间运动学即可得到Landauer电导 $G_0 = e^2/h$。该构造对任意能量色散（energy dispersion）均保持精确；Fock空间分解为有限不相交能量子带的方法具有高度可扩展性，适用于高性能计算平台。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个从连续散射描述到基于费米子波包的离散、时间分辨图像之间直接且严格的桥梁，为理解量子输运的时域微观机制提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Quantum transport in mesoscopic systems is conventionally formulated within the Landauer--Büttiker scattering framework, where steady-state currents emerge from the transmission of plane waves representing propagating carriers. While highly successful, this description obscures the explicit time-domain dynamics of individual fermionic excitations and their role in establishing macroscopic transport. Here, we present an exact and self-contained time-domain construction of Landauer transport based on a discrete basis of orthogonal fermionic wave packets. Starting from a second-quantized formulation, we define packet creation operators via a continuous Fourier transform over a finite transport energy window. By encoding the Pauli exclusion principle, which enforces a fundamental temporal spacing $Δt = h/eV$, the current is reproduced in terms of orthogonal wave packets that are used for the rigorous construction of the many-body fermionic state. In this representation, a noiseless current emerges as a deterministic sequence of charge-carrying events, yielding the Landauer conductance $G_0 = e^2/h$ without invoking momentum-space kinematics. We further demonstrate that this construction remains exact for arbitrary energy dispersion. Additionally, the underlying Fock space decomposition into finite disjoint energy sub-bands renders the numerical approach highly scalable for high performance computing platforms. Our results establish a direct and rigorous bridge between the continuous scattering description of quantum transport and a discrete, time-resolved picture based on fermionic wave packets.

### [121] [Constriction-induced modulation of charging energy in a quantum Hall cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19187)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 充电能量在仅100 mT的磁场范围内变化高达60%，且该效应仅在QPC弱夹断（即强腔-引线耦合）条件下出现。充电能量的调制与QPC磁导存在关联，其根源是QPC收缩区域内不可压缩分数量子霍尔态（incompressible fractional quantum Hall state）的形成，导致局域可压缩性与静电屏蔽随磁场变化。

Conclusion: 量子霍尔腔的QPC收缩应被视为活跃的静电元件（active electrostatic element）而非被动边界，其动态屏蔽机制（dynamic screening mechanism）对于正确解释干涉测量结果和提取任意子统计（anyonic statistics）具有直接影响。

Abstract: Electronic Fabry-Pérot interferometers (FPIs) operating in the fractional quantum Hall regime are a key platform for probing anyonic braiding statistics, yet interpreting their interference signals is complicated by Coulomb charging effects, which are commonly treated as parasitic, static properties governed by the cavity's geometry and electrostatics. Here, using a gate-defined quantum Hall cavity tuned to the Coulomb-dominated regime, we demonstrate that the charging energy is in fact strongly and non-monotonically modulated by the magnetic field, varying by up to 60% over a range of only 100 mT. The effect appears exclusively when the quantum point contacts (QPCs) forming the cavity are weakly pinched off, i.e., in the strong cavity-to-lead coupling regime. By correlating the charging energy modulation with the QPC magneto-conductance, we attribute this behavior to field-dependent changes in local compressibility and electrostatic screening between the cavity and the leads, driven by the formation of incompressible fractional quantum Hall states within the constrictions. This result establishes QPC constrictions of quantum Hall cavities as active electrostatic elements rather than passive boundaries, revealing a dynamic screening mechanism, with direct consequences for the interpretation of interference measurements and the extraction of anyonic statistics.

Method: 提出一个非平衡态（non-equilibrium）理论框架，将CISS效应与轨道埃德尔斯坦效应（orbital Edelstein effect）联系起来。在轨道埃德尔斯坦效应中，驱动电流可诱导出有限轨道磁化（orbital magnetization），即使在不存在自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的情况下也是如此。

Abstract: The chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS) effect, discovered by Naaman and collaborators in 1999, describes the emergence of a finite spin polarization in response to current flow through a chiral electronic system. While extensive experimental studies have verified the presence of CISS in molecular systems and, more recently, in chiral materials, a complete microscopic understanding of this effect remains elusive. In this work, we propose a theoretical framework linking the CISS effect to the orbital Edelstein effect. In the latter, a drive current induces a finite orbital magnetization, even in the absence of spin-orbit coupling. Our non-equilibrium theory naturally explains key features of the CISS effect: its persistence in systems with weak or vanishingly small spin-orbit coupling and its connection to natural optical activity, a distinctive signature of chiral systems.

### [123] [Exclusion Statistics as a Thermodynamic Resource in Quantum Heat Engines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19310)
*Sampurna Karmakar,Aziz Hasan,Sourin Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明了量子热电热机的最大功率上限并非普适，而是由工作介质的统计性质决定：玻色子工质的最大功率约为费米子工质的1.52倍，并通过Haldane分数排除统计实现连续插值，表明量子统计排除是一种独立可调的热力学资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往认为量子热电热机存在普适的Whitney极限（universal Whitney limit），但该极限是否真正普适尚不清楚；本文旨在检验该极限的统计依赖性，并探索通过改变粒子统计类型（费米子→玻色子→分数统计）来突破极限的可能性。

Method: 采用非线性Landauer-Büttiker框架（nonlinear Landauer-Büttiker framework）分别计算费米子与玻色子工作介质的最大输出功率；引入Haldane分数排除统计（Haldane fractional exclusion statistics）参数g，在g=0（玻色子）到g=1（费米子）之间进行连续插值分析。

Result: 费米子最大功率 $P_{\text{fermion}}^{\max} \simeq 0.0321π^2 k_B^2(T_L-T_R)^2/h$，玻色子最大功率 $P_{\text{boson}}^{\max} = (\ln 2)^2 k_B^2(T_L-T_R)^2/h$，后者约为前者的1.52倍。对于g<1的分数统计，最大功率随g减小而单调增强，且偏压成本降低。

Conclusion: 量子统计排除（quantum statistical exclusion）是一种此前未被认识、可独立调谐的热力学资源（thermodynamic resource），能够打开传统载流子工程方法无法企及的性能区间；实验上可通过铁磁自旋链中的磁振子输运（magnon transport）实现玻色子方案。

Abstract: The maximum power extractable from a quantum thermoelectric heat engine operating with free fermion carriers is bounded by the universal Whitney limit, $P_{\text{fermion}}^{\max} \simeq 0.0321π^2 k_B^2(T_L-T_R)^2/h$. We demonstrate that this bound is not fundamental to quantum heat engines but is instead an artifact of fermionic statistics. Within the nonlinear Landauer-Büttiker framework, a bosonic working medium yields a strictly enhanced universal maximum power, $P_{\text{boson}}^{\max} = (\ln 2)^2\, k_B^2(T_L-T_R)^2/h$, exceeding the fermionic limit by a factor of $(\ln 2)^2/(0.0321π^2) \approx 1.52$. We propose magnon transport through a ferromagnetic spin chain as an experimentally viable bosonic realization. Incorporating Haldane fractional exclusion statistics with parameter $g$ provides a continuous interpolation between the bosonic ($g = 0$) and fermionic ($g = 1$) limits, revealing a monotonic enhancement of maximum power for $g < 1$ at reduced bias cost. These results establish quantum statistical exclusion as a previously unrecognized and independently tunable thermodynamic resource, opening performance regimes inaccessible to conventional carrier-engineering approaches.

</details>

### [124] [A Numerical Rosenblatt Method for Forced Variable Independence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.25521)

TL;DR: 提出一种新颖的数值技术，可将系统中的某一随机变量转化为与其他任意随机变量统计准独立（statistical quasi-independence），并通过粒子物理中的分类器对可观测量准独立的实例验证了该方法的可行性。

Method: 提出了一种新颖的数值技术（novel numerical technique），通过对系统中的随机变量进行变换，使其与系统中任意其他随机变量达到统计准独立（statistical quasi-independence）。

Result: 以一个粒子物理（particle physics）实例展示了该方法的有效性：将分类器（classifier）变换为与可观测量（observable quantity）准独立的形式。

Conclusion: 该数值技术能够实现变量间的统计准独立，并具备在粒子物理学领域的实际应用可行性，为解除系统内变量依赖性提供了新的通用工具。

Abstract: A novel numerical technique is presented to transform one random variable within a system toward statistical quasi-independence from any other random variable in the system. The method's applicability is demonstrated through a particle physics example where a classifier is rendered quasi-independent from an observable quantity.

### [125] [Resolving the Hubble Tension in the Early Dark Energy Framework with JWST and DESI Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19090)
*Guo-Hong Du,Tian-Nuo Li,Lu Yin,Sheng-Han Zhou,Hao Wang,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用Planck、ACT、SPT的宇宙微波背景数据、DESI的重子声学振荡数据以及JWST的紫外光度函数观测数据，探索早期暗能量模型缓解哈勃常数张力的能力。在标准轴子EDE框架下，CMB+DESI+JWST联合数据将哈勃常数值提升至$71.58\pm1.05\,\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$，将$H_0$张力缓解至$1.0\sigma$水平，同时模型对JWST数据的拟合优于$\Lambda$CDM模型（$\Delta\chi^2_{\mathrm{tot}}=-18.26$, $\Delta\mathrm{DIC}=-11.89$），揭示了JWST高红移星系数据在检验EDE模型及缓解$H_0$张力方面与早期和晚期观测的互补优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在JWST和DESI时代，JWST高红移星系观测与DESI重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation, BAO）测量对标准$\Lambda$CDM模型构成了严峻挑战，同时哈勃常数（$H_0$）张力问题日益突出，亟需探寻能够缓解该张力的新物理模型。

Method: 在规范轴子（axion）早期暗能量（early dark energy, EDE）理论框架下，联合使用Planck、ACT和SPT的宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）数据、DESI的BAO数据以及JWST的紫外光度函数（ultraviolet luminosity function）观测数据进行统计分析。

Result: CMB+DESI+JWST联合数据将$H_0$值显著提升至$71.58\pm1.05\,\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$，将$H_0$张力缓解至$1.0\sigma$水平；同时该模型对JWST数据的拟合优于$\Lambda$CDM模型，总卡方差值$\Delta\chi^2_{\mathrm{tot}}=-18.26$，偏差信息准则差值$\Delta\mathrm{DIC}=-11.89$，统计表现显著更优。

Conclusion: JWST高红移星系数据与早期（CMB）及晚期（BAO）观测在检验EDE模型和缓解$H_0$张力方面具有互补优势，EDE模型能够同时改善对JWST观测的拟合效果并缓解哈勃常数张力问题。

Abstract: In the JWST and DESI era, the JWST high-redshift galaxy observations and DESI baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) measurements severely challenge the standard $Λ$CDM model, while the $H_0$ tension becomes increasingly prominent. In this work, we investigate the capability of the early dark energy (EDE) model to alleviate the $H_0$ tension utilizing cosmic microwave background data from Planck, ACT, and SPT, BAO data from DESI, and ultraviolet luminosity function observations from the JWST. Within the canonical axion EDE framework, the CMB+DESI+JWST data significantly increase the $H_0$ value to $71.58\pm1.05\,\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$, alleviating the $H_0$ tension to the $1.0σ$ level. Simultaneously, this model improves the fit to the JWST data and exhibits statistical performance significantly better than the $Λ$CDM model, with $Δχ^2_{\mathrm{tot}} = -18.26$ and $Δ\mathrm{DIC} = -11.89$. Our results highlight the complementary advantages of JWST high-redshift galaxy data alongside early- and late-time observations in testing EDE and alleviating the $H_0$ tension.

### [126] [Constraints on Cosmic Strings from the Curl-Mode CMB Lensing Power Spectrum measured by ACT DR6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19337)
*A. I. Lonappan,K. Ramesh,T. Namikawa,F. J. Qu,B. Keating*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究利用阿塔卡马宇宙学望远镜（ACT）第六次数据发布（DR6）的旋度模式透镜重构，对宇宙弦的无量纲张力 $Gμ$ 和互交换概率 $P$ 施加了迄今为止来自旋度模式宇宙微波背景（CMB）透镜功率谱的最强约束：在规范Nambu-Goto值 $P=1$ 下，$Gμ\le 5.0\times 10^{-5}$（$2σ$）；结合Planck 2013数据后约束进一步收紧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙弦网络是最大可观测尺度上矢量与张量度规扰动（vector and tensor metric perturbations）的少数几个有充分动机的宇宙学源之一。这类扰动会在宇宙微波背景（CMB）光子的偏折角中留下特征性的旋度分量（curl component），该分量在绝热密度涨落（adiabatic density fluctuations）的线性阶为零，因此为探测宇宙弦提供了独特的探针。

Method: 利用ACT DR6基于五个季节的温度与极化数据覆盖 $9400~\mathrm{deg}^2$ 天区的旋度模式透镜重构（curl-mode lensing reconstruction），并在速度依赖单标度框架（velocity-dependent one-scale framework）内对宇宙弦诱导的旋度功率谱进行建模。同时将ACT DR6数据与覆盖到 $L_{\rm min}=2$ 的Planck 2013旋度模式重构结果进行联合分析。

Result: 在$2σ$置信水平下，从小$P$区间的数据得到组合参数 $GμP^{-1}\le 3.5\times 10^{-5}$，在规范Nambu-Goto值 $P=1$ 下得到 $Gμ\le 5.0\times 10^{-5}$。联合ACT DR6与Planck 2013数据后，约束分别收紧至 $GμP^{-1}\le 3.2\times 10^{-5}$ 和 $Gμ\le 4.3\times 10^{-5}$。与ACT 2008年季的分析相比，ACT DR6对 $GμP^{-1}$ 的约束提升了近一个数量级。

Conclusion: 这些结果是迄今为止从旋度模式CMB透镜功率谱导出的宇宙弦最强约束，展示了高灵敏度CMB透镜数据在限制早期宇宙拓扑缺陷（topological defects）方面的潜力。

Abstract: A network of cosmic strings is one of the few well-motivated cosmological sources of vector and tensor metric perturbations on the largest observable scales. Such perturbations imprint a characteristic curl component in the deflection angle of cosmic microwave background (CMB) photons that, unlike the scalar lensing potential, vanishes for adiabatic density fluctuations at linear order. We exploit the curl-mode lensing reconstruction released as part of the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) Data Release~6 (DR6), based on five seasons of temperature and polarization data covering $9400~\mathrm{deg}^2$ of sky, to set new constraints on the dimensionless string tension $Gμ$ and the inter-commutation (reconnection) probability $P$. Modelling the string-induced curl power spectrum within the velocity-dependent one-scale framework, we obtain a $2σ$ upper bound on the combination $GμP^{-1}\le 3.5\times 10^{-5}$ in the small-$P$ regime, and $Gμ\le 5.0\times 10^{-5}$ at $2σ$ assuming the canonical Nambu-Goto value $P=1$. Combining the ACT DR6 curl bandpowers with the Planck 2013 curl-mode reconstruction, which extends down to $L_{\rm min}=2$, tightens these bounds to $GμP^{-1}\le 3.2\times 10^{-5}$ and $Gμ\le 4.3\times 10^{-5}$ ($2σ$). These represent the tightest constraints on cosmic strings derived from the curl-mode CMB lensing power spectrum to date. Using the ACT data alone, compared to the ACT 2008-season analysis, the ACT DR6 constraint on $GμP^{-1}$ is nearly an order of magnitude tighter.

</details>


### [127] [Data-Driven Discovery of a Simple Phantom-Crossing Dark Energy Parametrization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17951)
*Giulia Borghetto,Ameek Malhotra,Simran Arora,Antonio De Felice,Shinji Mukohyama,Gianmassimo Tasinato,Ivonne Zavala*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究在VCDM修正引力框架下，结合贝叶斯样条重建（Bayesian spline reconstruction）与穷举符号回归（Exhaustive Symbolic Regression），发现当前宇宙学观测支持一种极其简单的暗能量动力学形式：单参数状态方程 $w(a)=w_0/\sqrt{a}$。该模型可自然穿越幻影分界线（phantom divide），不包含未来大撕裂奇点（big-rip singularity），并在贝叶斯模型比较中优于标准二参数参数化（如CPL）以及ΛCDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗能量状态方程 $w(a)$ 的参数化形式（如CPL）自由度较多，而当前观测数据可能支持更简单的动力学。此外，在修正引力框架下实现自洽的幻影分界线穿越是一个理论挑战。因此，本文旨在构建一个数据驱动的、可解释的暗能量模型发现框架，以检验数据是否偏好更简单的暗能量动力学。

Method: 首先，在VCDM（一种最小修正引力框架）中，利用CMB、BAO和Ia型超新星数据，采用贝叶斯样条重建方法对暗能量状态方程 $w(a)$ 进行非参数化重构。然后，应用穷举符号回归（Exhaustive Symbolic Regression）——一种可解释的机器学习技术——系统搜索固定复杂度的解析表达式，最终识别出单参数形式 $w(a)=w_0/\sqrt{a}$。

Result: 贝叶斯样条重建显示数据偏好光滑、单调的幻影穿越轨迹，且贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）不支持复杂样条模型。识别的单参数模型 $w(a)=w_0/\sqrt{a}$ 可与标准二参数参数化（CPL）媲美，自然穿越幻影分界线（$w_0<0$），抑制早期暗能量（early dark energy），且无未来大撕裂奇点。贝叶斯模型比较对该参数化相对于二参数备选模型呈中等支持，相对于ΛCDM呈更强支持。

Conclusion: 当前观测数据偏好极其简单的暗能量动力学，表明贝叶斯重建与符号回归可以结合成一种有原则的宇宙学模型发现框架（principled model-discovery framework）。该单参数模型是宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的真正动力学变形，但不包含宇宙学常数作为其极限情形，因而具有高度可预测性。

Abstract: We develop a data-driven reconstruction programme for the dark-energy equation of state within VCDM, a minimally modified gravity framework in which both background and linear perturbations can be consistently evolved across the phantom divide. Using CMB, BAO, and type-Ia supernova data, we first perform a Bayesian spline reconstruction of $w(a)$, finding a preference for smooth, monotonic phantom-crossing trajectories. Bayesian evidence disfavors increasingly complex spline models, indicating that current observations exhibit a statistical preference for low-complexity dark-energy dynamics. Motivated by this result, we apply Exhaustive Symbolic Regression, an interpretable machine-learning technique that systematically searches over analytic expressions of fixed complexity, identifying the remarkably simple one-parameter form $w(a)={w_0}/{\sqrt a}$, which reproduces the reconstructed behaviour and fits the data at a level comparable to standard two-parameter parametrizations such as CPL. The model naturally crosses the phantom divide for $w_0<0$, suppresses early dark energy, and predicts a transient accelerating and phantom phase without a future big-rip singularity. As a one-parameter model, it is highly predictive, being a genuinely dynamical deformation of the cosmological constant rather than containing it as a limit. Bayesian model comparison yields mild-to-moderate support for this parametrization relative to standard two-parameter alternatives, and stronger evidence relative to $Λ$CDM. Our results suggest that current observations favour surprisingly simple dark-energy dynamics and illustrate how Bayesian reconstruction and symbolic regression can be combined into a principled model-discovery framework for cosmology.

</details>
