### [128] [Polyconvexity implies Hill's inequality in ${\rm SL}(2)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18879)
*Ionel-Dumitrel Ghiba,Patrizio Neff,Maximilian P. Wollner*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文澄清了不可压缩非线性弹性中Legendre-Hadamard椭圆性、多凸性与Hill不等式之间的内在联系，并通过多种替代证明表明，在二维不可压缩情形下，LH-椭圆性（秩一凸性）与多凸性均蕴含弱Hill不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在可压缩非线性各向同性弹性理论中，秩一凸性（rank-one convexity）、多凸性（polyconvexity）以及柯西应力张量关于对数拉伸张量的单调性（TSTS-M⁺）是彼此独立的本构条件，但对于物理上有意义的理想弹性材料描述，这些条件应同时满足。在不可压缩情形下，TSTS-M⁺退化为Hill不等式。然而，对于这些先验独立的概念之间究竟存在何种深层联系，尚不明确，亟需澄清。

Method: 本文采用多种替代证明（alternative proofs）的方法，系统分析Legendre-Hadamard椭圆性、多凸性与Hill不等式在不可压缩二维情形下的逻辑蕴含关系。

Result: 研究表明，在二维不可压缩情形下，Legendre-Hadamard椭圆性（即秩一凸性）与多凸性均蕴含弱Hill不等式（weak Hill inequality）。

Conclusion: 这些先验独立的本构条件之间存在深层次的内在连接：在二维不可压缩非线性弹性中，Legendre-Hadamard椭圆性和多凸性均足以导出弱Hill不等式，从而为不可压缩弹性材料的本构约束提供了更为统一的理论框架。

Abstract: For compressible nonlinear isotropic elasticity it is well known that rank-one convexity, polyconvexity and the monotonicity of the Cauchy stress tensor with respect to the logarithmic stretch tensor (the true stress-true strain monotonicity, TSTS-M$^+$) are independent constitutive conditions which should, however, all together be satisfied for a physically meaningful description of idealized elastic materials. In the incompressible case, TSTS-M$^+$ turns into Hill's inequality since the Cauchy stress $σ$ reduces to the Kirchhoff stress $τ$. Hill's inequality requires then monotonicity of the Kirchhoff stress in terms of the logarithmic stretch tensor evaluated for incompressible response. In this paper we clarify how the a priori independent notions of Legendre-Hadamard ellipticity (LH), polyconvexity and Hill's inequality are nevertheless intimately connected. More precisely, by providing several alternative proofs, we show that both LH-ellipticity (rank-one convexity) and polyconvexity imply the weak Hill inequality in the incompressible two-dimensional case.

</details>


### [129] [Rigorous analysis for the Dirac system on the quarter-plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19326)
*Hassan Babaei,Jerry L. Bona,Andreas Chatziafratis*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对定义在半无界空间直线（spatial half-line）上的完全非齐次狄拉克系统（fully non-homogeneous Dirac system），通过Fokas统一变换方法（unified transform methodology）推导了解析解公式并进行了严格后验验证，进而研究了解的正则性、边界行为、长程渐近性以及长时间周期性等定性性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克系统（Dirac system）在量子力学等领域具有基础性地位，但半无界区域上的完全非齐次初边值问题（non-homogeneous initial-boundary-value problems）的解析求解与定性分析仍缺乏系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，为后续非线性系统的研究提供工具。

Method: 采用Fokas统一变换方法（Fokas' unified transform methodology）形式化推导解析解公式；利用复分析工具（complex-analytic tools）对获得的积分表示（integral representations）进行严格后验验证；结合定性理论（qualitative theory）分析解的正则性与唯一性。

Result: 获得了完全非齐次狄拉克系统在半无界区域上的封闭形式解析解；发现解的平滑性（smoothness）严重依赖于初值、边值与外力数据之间的相容性条件（compatibility conditions）；建立了解的正则性（regularity）与唯一性（uniqueness）结论；揭示了边界行为、长程渐近性（long-range asymptotics）及长时间周期性（long-time periodicity）等定性性质。

Conclusion: 本文为半无界狄拉克系统提供了严格的解析求解与定性分析框架，所得封闭形式表达式不仅适用于线性系统本身，也可为非线性对应系统（non-linear counterparts）的研究提供有价值的工具。

Abstract: Considered and analyzed below are fully non-homogeneous initial-boundary-value problems for the celebrated Dirac system, formulated on the spatial half-line. Analytical solution formulae are derived formally via suitable implementation of the well-known Fokas' unified transform methodology, and rigorously verified a posteriori. The latter substantial task relies on complex-analytic tools and careful interpretation of the obtained integral representations. These valid solutions are then used for investigating qualitative properties. These include boundary behavior near the axes of the domain as well as long-range asymptotics and long-time (eventual) periodicity. Notably, smoothness of the solution, both within and upto the boundary of the domain, depends heavily on certain compatibility conditions between initial, boundary and forcing data. Further results pertaining to solution's regularity and uniqueness are thence established based on the qualitative theory. The closed-form expressions reported here are also useful in the study of non-linear counterparts.

</details>

### [130] [Dynamical axion quasiparticles: an open quantum system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18493)
*Daniel Boyanovsky*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该论文研究了与光子浴耦合的动态轴子准粒子（DAQ）的非平衡动力学，推导了部分马尔可夫近似下的量子主方程（QME），发现了反芝诺动力学、费米黄金定则的瞬态违反以及详细平衡破坏等非马尔可夫效应，并建立了QME与量子多体线性响应理论之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动态轴子准粒子（dynamical axion quasiparticle, DAQ）作为量子开放系统（quantum open system）与平衡态光子浴（photon bath）通过陈-西蒙斯项（Chern-Simons term）耦合时的非平衡动力学，该量子开放系统描述尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 在仅实施部分马尔可夫近似（partial Markov approximation）的条件下，推导了二阶耦合下的量子主方程（quantum master equation, QME），其林德布拉德（Lindblad）形式的衰变率由陈-西蒙斯密度的平衡关联函数决定且具有时间依赖性；同时采用量子多体线性响应（quantum many body linear response）方法，建立了两种方法的桥梁，并给出了费曼图（Feynman diagram）解释。

Result: 发现早期时间演化呈现量子反芝诺动力学（quantum anti Zeno dynamics），表现为准粒子衰变增强和布居数增长加快；观察到费米黄金定则（Fermi's Golden rule）和细致平衡（detailed balance）的瞬态违反，这些现象是直接与陈-西蒙斯关联函数谱密度相关的非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）效应；此外，线性响应下DAQ凝聚体诱导的陈-西蒙斯密度的期望值表明拓扑磁化率（topological susceptibility）正比于DAQ的多体自能（many body self-energy）。

Conclusion: 部分马尔可夫近似下的QME能够捕捉短时间尺度的瞬态非马尔可夫动力学，且QME与量子多体线性响应方法在描述凝聚态动力学方面相互一致；高阶系统-浴相关修正可通过费曼图进行系统理解。

Abstract: We study the non-equilibrium dynamics of emergent dynamical axion quasiparticles (DAQ) coupled to a photon bath in equilibrium via a Chern-Simons term as a quantum open system. A quantum master equation (QME) is derived up to second order in this coupling implementing only a \emph{partial} Markov approximation, allowing time dependent rates in the Lindblad (QME). These are determined by the equilibrium correlation functions of the Chern-Simons density, and their time dependence allows us to explore transient dynamics in coherences and population: the formation of the quasiparticle on short time scales and its decay, and the build-up of population with an effective time dependent rate. Early time evolution features quantum \emph{anti} Zeno dynamics with enhanced quasiparticle decay and population growth. These phenomena describe transient violations of Fermi's Golden rule and of \emph{detailed balance}, and are distinct \emph{non-Markovian} effects directly related to the spectral density of the Chern-Simons correlators. We obtain the equation of motion of coherent (DAQ) condensates both with the (QME) and with quantum many body linear response establishing a direct bridge between both methods. As a corollary we obtain the expectation value of the Chern-Simons density \emph{induced} by a (DAQ) condensate in linear response, the topological susceptibility is shown to be proportional to the (DAQ) many body self-energy. We provide a Feynman diagram-based interpretation of approximations invoked in the (QME) and corrections from system-bath correlations in higher order.

</details>

### [131] [GRMHD and GRRT Simulations of Black Hole Accretion: Flares, Precession, and Complex Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19320)
*Hong-Xuan Jiang*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本学位论文通过广义相对论磁流体动力学（general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic, GRMHD）模拟和协变辐射传输（covariant radiative transfer）计算，建立了统一数值框架来建模孤立Kerr黑洞、非Kerr黑洞及双黑洞时空中的吸积、喷流、耀发活动与多波段光变，并揭示了磁场几何、量子引力修正和引力自透镜等物理效应对电磁信号的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对超大质量黑洞（supermassive black hole）的电磁观测日益精细，但理论模型仍缺乏统一且充分的数值框架来同时处理不同时空背景下的吸积盘（accretion disk）、喷流（jet）和瞬变耀发（transient flare）等过程，尤其对非Kerr黑洞和双黑洞系统的研究尚不充分。

Method: 采用广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟与协变辐射传输（covariant radiative transfer）计算相结合的方法，构建统一的数值框架，并将其分别应用于Kerr黑洞、环圈量子黑洞（loop-quantum black hole）及超大质量双黑洞（supermassive binary black hole）等不同时空结构。

Result: 对于孤立Kerr黑洞，多环磁场配置可自然产生重联事件和磁绳（flux-rope）结构，解释人马座A*（Sagittarius A*）的近红外耀发和延迟毫米辐射；倾斜磁 arrested盘中磁转矩可驱动逆行盘和喷流进动。对于环圈量子黑洞，量子引力修正会改变光子环大小、偏振结构和喷流功率，可受到事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）数据的观测约束。对于双黑洞，引力自透镜（gravitational self-lensing）、激波活动和自旋-轨道耦合共同塑造多波段光变曲线和喷流进动。

Conclusion: 该工作将相对论性等离子体动力学与当前及未来的黑洞系统观测联系起来，表明不同时空的修正（如量子引力、双黑洞动力学）均可产生可探测的电磁特征，为利用多波段观测检验广义相对论和黑洞天体物理提供了理论工具。

Abstract: This dissertation studies the electromagnetic signatures of accreting supermassive black holes using general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic simulations and covariant radiative-transfer calculations. It develops a unified numerical framework for modeling black-hole accretion, jet launching, flaring activity, and multi-band variability in Kerr, non-Kerr, and binary black-hole spacetimes.
  For isolated Kerr black holes, I investigate how magnetic-field geometry affects accretion dynamics and transient emission. Multi-loop magnetic configurations naturally produce reconnection events and flux-rope structures that can power near-infrared flares from Sagittarius A*, while the evolving optical depth of expanding plasma explains delayed millimeter emission. I also show that in tilted magnetically arrested disks, magnetic torques can drive retrograde disk and jet precession.
  The dissertation then applies the same framework to more complex spacetimes. Simulations of accretion onto regular loop-quantum black holes show that quantum-gravity corrections can modify photon-ring size, polarization structure, and jet power, leading to observational constraints from Event Horizon Telescope data. Finally, simulations of supermassive binary black holes in time-dependent spacetimes reveal how gravitational self-lensing, shock activity, and spin-orbit coupling shape multi-wavelength light curves and jet precession. Together, these results connect relativistic plasma dynamics with current and future observations of black-hole systems.

</details>

### [132] [Orbital evolution of asymmetric binaries within accreting environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18341)
*Albert Radulea,Marcelo E. Rubio,Konstantinos Kritos,Andrea Maselli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究建立了一个框架，分析致密天体反复穿越吸积盘时的长期轨道演化，发现盘诱导耗散驱动轨道面快速对齐与随后偏心率缓慢衰减的两阶段演化，并证明相对论效应和吸积盘结构模型选择对轨道演化有显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端质量比旋进（extreme mass-ratio inspirals）嵌入吸积盘（accretion disks）为研究相对论轨道动力学（relativistic orbital dynamics）与环境效应的相互作用提供了天然场景，现有研究对此类长期演化的系统性建模尚不充分。

Method: 轨道运动通过Kerr测地线（Kerr geodesics）建模，盘相互作用通过质量吸积（mass accretion）和动力摩擦（dynamical friction）的有效描绘（effective prescriptions）编码，并比较了Sirko-Goodman与Novikov-Thorne两种吸积盘模型。

Result: 盘诱导耗散驱动两阶段演化：轨道面快速与盘面对齐，随后偏心率（eccentricity）缓慢阻尼。与开普勒（Keplerian）处理相比，累积相对论效应即使在轨道分离较大的区域也会产生偏差，且偏差随盘穿越次数增大。相对论性吸积盘结构导致更低密度和更大标高，削弱轨道耗散。中心黑洞自旋对整体圆化效率（circularization efficiency）影响较小。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了在研究嵌入AGN盘的致密天体时，需要一致地同时建模相对论轨道动力学和盘结构，该框架为探索长期演化和与准周期爆发（quasi-periodic eruptions）的可能联系提供了基础。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals embedded in accretion disks provide a natural arena for studying the interplay between relativistic orbital dynamics and environmental effects. In this work, we develop a framework to investigate the secular evolution of compact objects repeatedly crossing an accretion disk around a supermassive black hole. The orbital motion is modeled through Kerr geodesics, while disk interactions are encoded through effective prescriptions for mass accretion and dynamical friction. We find that disk-induced dissipation generically drives a two-stage evolution characterized by rapid alignment of the orbital plane with the disk, followed by slower eccentricity damping. By systematically comparing the dynamics with a purely Keplerian treatment, we show that cumulative relativistic effects produce deviations even at large orbital separations, where the Keplerian approximation would naively be expected to remain accurate. These discrepancies grow through repeated disk crossings and become increasingly pronounced in more relativistic orbital configurations. We further investigate the impact of the accretion-disk model by comparing the Sirko-Goodman and Novikov-Thorne prescriptions. Relativistic disk structures predict systematically lower densities and larger scale heights, leading to weaker orbital dissipation and slower secular evolution. By contrast, the spin of the central black hole has only a minor effect on the overall circularization efficiency. Our results demonstrate the importance of consistently modeling both relativistic orbital dynamics and disk structure when studying compact objects embedded in AGN disks, and provide a framework for exploring their long-term evolution, as well as a possible connection to quasi-periodic eruptions.

</details>


### [133] [A matrix free action of the Ashtekar-Lewandowski volume operator of loop quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18397)
*Waleed Sherif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对圈量子引力中的Ashtekar-Lewandowski体积算符，提出了一种无矩阵（matrix-free）作用方法，利用移位-预解求积（SRQ）和Brunnemann-Thiemann表达式，避免了稠密谱分解，实现了高自旋截断下的高效数值计算与谱估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圈量子引力中的Ashtekar-Lewandowski (AL) 体积算符是哈密顿约束的核心，但其顶点作用通常依赖有限再耦合矩阵的稠密集谱分解，这阻碍了大运动学希尔伯特空间（kinematical Hilbert space）或高价顶点上的数值分析。

Method: 利用Brunnemann-Thiemann表达式在标准再耦合基（recoupling basis）中构造取向AL体积密度$Q_v$的局域矩阵元；基于Balakrishnan-Stieltjes表示将$(Q_v^2)^{1/4}$近似为移位-预解求积（shifted-resolvent quadrature, SRQ），仅需重复应用$Q_v$和移位正线性求解，兼容多移位Krylov方法。

Result: 严格证明了体积核（volume kernel）的精确保持，给出了算子范数和残差误差估计，讨论了扇区尺度缩放边界；在嵌入$K_5$图上对小自旋截断的验证显示顶点期望值快速收敛、零体积模精确保持；在自旋截断$2j=250000$下实现了无矩阵蒙特卡洛估计，并可将SRQ与随机Lanczos求积结合以估计固定扇区体积谱测度。

Conclusion: 所提出的无矩阵SRQ方法有效克服了AL体积算符在大尺度或高价顶点下的稠密矩阵瓶颈，实现了高自旋截断下的数值计算与谱分析，为圈量子引力的大规模数值研究提供了可行工具。

Abstract: The Ashtekar-Lewandowski (AL) volume operator of loop quantum gravity is central to the Hamiltonian constraint, but its vertex action is usually obtained from dense spectral decompositions of finite recoupling matrices, obstructing numerical analysis on large kinematical Hilbert spaces or high-valence vertices. We formulate a matrix free action of the $SU(2)$ AL vertex volume operator in standard recoupling basis, making use of the Brunnemann-Thiemann expression for the oriented AL volume density $Q_{v}$ whose matrix elements can be generated locally from recoupling theory without forming the full matrix. Based on the Balakrishnan-Stieltjes representation of $(Q_{v}^{2})^{1/4}$ we approximate the volume by shifted-resolvent quadrature (SRQ). The resulting action uses only repeated applications of $Q_{v}$ and shifted positive linear solves, making it compatible with multi-shift Krylov methods. We prove exact preservation of the volume kernel, provide operator-norm and residual error estimates, discuss sector-wise scaling bounds, and validate the method on an embedded $K_{5}$ graph at small spin cutoffs against exact dense local-block operators. Numerical simulations show rapid convergence of vertex expectation values, controlled dependence on bound parameters, and exact preservation of zero-volume modes. We further demonstrate matrix free Monte Carlo estimates at doubled-spin cutoff $2j=250000$ beyond dense materialisation, and show that SRQ can be combined with stochastic Lanczos quadrature to estimate fixed-sector volume spectral measures without dense volume matrices.

</details>


### [134] [Implications of Adler-Finch-Skea solution on charged dark energy star satisfying Karmarkar Condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18775)
*Pramit Rej*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文在爱因斯坦引力框架下，利用Adler-Finch-Skea解和Karmarkar条件，结合暗能量（dark energy）的物态方程（equation of state），构建了一个各向异性暗能量耦合带电奇异星（charged strange star）模型，并以Her X-1为观测实例验证了模型的无奇点性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为避免致密天体引力塌缩形成奇点，提出暗能量可能介入其中。由于暗能量主导宇宙加速膨胀，它可能与致密恒星发生相互作用，因此需要构建一个更简单的、包含暗能量耦合的带电奇异星模型来研究此类天体的结构。

Method: 采用Karmarkar条件确定径向度规分量，Adler方法选取时间度规分量，得到Adler-Finch-Skea解；利用暗能量的物态方程（EoS）假设其密度与各向同性完美流体物质密度成正比；通过Darmois-Israel匹配条件平滑连接内外度规以确定未知常数；以Her X-1（质量$0.85 \pm 0.15 M_{\odot}$，半径$8.1_{-0.41}^{+0.41}$ km）为例进行数值验证。

Result: 模型通过了度规函数、压强、密度、质量-半径关系及暗能量参数等物理特性的检验；稳定性与力平衡分析表明该星体框架满足稳定性要求；模型无奇点，符合物理上真实且稳定的恒星模型条件。

Conclusion: 所提出的带电奇异星模型在暗能量耦合下无奇点，且满足所有稳定性判据，是一个物理自洽且稳定的恒星模型。

Abstract: A possible approach for preventing compact astrophysical objects from gravitational collapse into singularities is the idea of dark energy. Since it is the cause of our universe's accelerated expansion, it has the greatest impact on the cosmos. As a result, it appears that dark energy can interact with any compact astrophysical stellar object [Phys. Rev. D 103, 084042 (2021)]. In this study, our primary objective is to develop a simpler model of a charged strange star coupled with anisotropic dark energy admitting the Adler-Finch-Skea solution [J. Math. Phys. 15, 727 (1974); Class. Quantum Grav. 6, 467 (1989)] within Einstein gravity. To develop this model, the Karmarkar condition was employed to determine the radial metric component, while Adler's methodology was used to choose the time-metric component. For this purpose, we explored a particular strange star, Her X-1, with observed values of mass $(0.85 \pm 0.15)M_{\odot}$ and radius $= 8.1_{-0.41}^{+0.41}$ km. In this context, we proceeded to model dark energy using the equation of state (EoS), such that the density of dark energy is proportional to the density of isotropic perfect fluid matter. The unknown constants in the metric were determined by smooth matching using the Darmois-Israel criterion. We conduct an in-depth examination of the stability and force equilibrium of our suggested star framework, as well as several physical characteristics of the model such as the metric function, pressure, density, mass-radius relation, and dark energy parameters. Thus, the physical consistency and stability of the present model are investigated. Therefore, following a comprehensive theoretical investigation, we discovered that our proposed model is singularity free and meets all the stability requirements to be a stable and physically realistic stellar model.

</details>


### [135] [Non-trivial boundary conditions in general-relativistic models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18868)
*Davide Astesiano,Matteo Luca Ruggiero,Federico Re*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论（General Relativity）框架下提出对暗物质效应（dark matter effects）的一种替代解释，主张通过选择合适的初始条件和边界条件（initial and boundary conditions）来再现通常归因于额外物质的天体物理现象，并以轴对称旋转尘埃流体（axially symmetric rotating dust fluid）的自引力系统为例进行论证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，天体物理和宇宙学观测中与预期不符的引力效应被归因于暗物质（dark matter）的存在。本文质疑这一默认解释，认为不同的初始假设会导致对同一现象的不同理解，因而需要从广义相对论的理论框架内部寻找替代解释路径。

Method: 在广义相对论框架下，通过分析轴对称旋转尘埃流体（axially symmetric rotating dust fluid）的自引力系统，检验不同初始条件与边界条件对系统动力学行为的影响，并将这些效应与通常归因于暗物质的效应进行对比。

Result: 研究表明，通过适当选择系统的初始条件和边界条件（initial and boundary conditions），可以再现那些通常被归因于额外物质（即暗物质）的引力效应。

Conclusion: 暗物质效应未必需要引入未知物质粒子来解释，而可能源于广义相对论框架下对系统初始假设的不同选择。这为理解宇宙中缺失质量（missing mass）问题提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We propose an alternative interpretation of dark matter effects within the framework of General Relativity. In particular, we suggest
  that, in astrophysical and cosmological contexts, different initial assumptions about a system inevitably lead to different interpretations of the same phenomena. As a concrete example, we examine self-gravitating systems composed of an axially symmetric rotating dust fluid and show that effects typically attributed to the presence of additional matter, can instead be reproduced through an appropriate choice of initial and boundary conditions for the equations governing the system.

</details>


### [136] [Kiselev black hole and the ultra-slow evaporating behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19110)
*Chen-Hao Wu,Xiao Liang,Ya-Peng Hu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究Kiselev黑洞的蒸发行为，发现状态参数$w_q$的降低会降低非最终阶段温度并显著延长蒸发寿命；同时指出Kiselev黑洞的超慢蒸发机制与完美流体暗物质黑洞和Horndeski黑洞存在本质差异，揭示了动态暗能量背景对黑洞蒸发的影响，并可能为约束$w_q$提供潜在实验途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kiselev解描述的是浸没在类精质暗能量（quintessence-like dark energy）背景中的黑洞，通过引入动态状态参数$w_q$，旨在帮助理解精质物质（quintessential matter）对黑洞的影响。

Method: 通过变化状态参数$w_q$，研究Kiselev黑洞的蒸发行为。

Result: 降低状态参数$w_q$会降低非最终阶段温度，并显著延长蒸发寿命；Kiselev黑洞的超慢蒸发机制与完美流体暗物质（perfect fluid dark matter, PFDM）黑洞和Horndeski黑洞存在本质差异，尽管后两者也具有类似的超长寿命。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了动态暗能量背景对黑洞蒸发的影响，为约束$w_q$提供了潜在实验途径，并可能补充宇宙学和天体物理学观测，例如DESI对解冻暗能量（thawing dark energy）的偏好以及基于超慢蒸发的爆炸黑洞观测。

Abstract: Kiselev solution is a metric that describes black holes immersed in a quintessence-like dark energy background. By introducing a dynamic state parameter $w_q$, the Kiselev solution is supposed to help comprehend the effect of quintessential matter on black holes. In this work, we study the evaporation behaviors of Kiselev black holes. By varying the state parameter $w_q$, we find that the decreasing state parameter lowers the non-final stage temperature and markedly prolongs the evaporation lifetime. We also find that the ultra-slow evaporation mechanism of Kiselev black holes differs vastly from the perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) black holes and Horndeski black holes, which share the analogous ultra-long lifetime. These results illuminate the effects of dynamic dark energy background on black hole evaporation, provide a potential laboratory to constrain the value of $w_q$, and may complement cosmological and astrophysical observations, e.g., the DESI's preference for thawing dark energy and the observation of exploding black holes based on ultra-slow evaporation.

</details>


### [137] [Impact of the Einstein Telescope's duty cycle on the estimation of binary black holes parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19201)
*Luca Negri,Thomas C. K. Ng,Thibeau Wouters,Tim J. Kuhlbusch,Harsh Narola,Robin Chan,Kailib Ryan Doney,Francesco Cireddu,Isaac C. F. Wong,Fabian Gittins,Peter T. H. Pang,Anuradha Samajdar,Achim Stahl,Justin Janquart,Chris Van Den Broeck,Tjonnie G. F. Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过全贝叶斯参数估计（full Bayesian parameter estimation）对比了下一代欧洲引力波天文台——爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）的两种候选设计（嵌套三角形ET-Δ与分离L形ET-2L），发现ET-Δ的冗余结构使其在多探测器运行时间上显著优于ET-2L，从而对光度距离和源帧质量分量（component masses）给出更紧的约束，即使在信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）较低的情况下也是如此。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）的几何构型尚未最终确定，存在嵌套三角形（ET-Δ）与分离L形（ET-2L）两种竞争方案。先前的比较工作基于Fisher信息矩阵（Fisher-information-matrix formalism）近似，但在占空比（duty cycle）导致的单探测器运行等场景下该近似可靠性不足，亟需一种更精细、有原则的处理方式。

Method: 采用全贝叶斯参数估计（full Bayesian parameter estimation）方法，对双黑洞并合（binary black-hole mergers）的引力波信号进行分析；将信号投影到模拟的爱因斯坦望远镜上，并使用连续时间马尔可夫链（continuous-time Markov chains）建模精细化的占空比，同时测试不同的探测器维护策略。

Result: ET-Δ的冗余性使其在大部分观测时间内至少保持两个探测器运行，而ET-2L常限于单探测器工作。在部分网络运行期间，ET-Δ的性能通常优于ET-2L；多探测器运行时间的增加转化为对光度距离（luminosity distance）和源帧质量分量（source-frame component masses）更紧的约束，且这一优势在ET-Δ的信噪比低于ET-2L时仍然成立。

Conclusion: ET-Δ设计在多探测器运行时间和参数估计精度方面优于ET-2L，为下一代引力波天文台的选型提供了基于贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）的有力证据。

Abstract: The geometry of the Einstein Telescope, the proposed next-generation European gravitational-wave observatory, is yet to be finalized. Two competing designs are under consideration: a nested triangular configuration (ET-Δ) and two separated L-shaped detectors (ET-2L). Extensive prior comparisons of ET designs established the scientific landscape using the Fisher-information-matrix formalism and identified that duty-cycle-induced single-detector operation is precisely the regime where this approximation becomes less reliable, underscoring the need for a refined, principled treatment of the duty cycle. In this manuscript, we build on that foundation by revisiting the comparison with full Bayesian parameter estimation of gravitational-wave signals from binary black-hole mergers, projected onto a simulated Einstein Telescope that incorporates a refined duty cycle modelled via continuous-time Markov chains and testing different detector maintenance strategies. We find that the redundancy inherent in the ET-Δ design enables it to maintain at least two operational detectors for the majority of the observing time, whereas the ET-2L configuration is often limited to a single detector. Crucially, we show that, during partial network operation, ET-Δ often outperforms ET-2L, and that the increased multi-detector uptime translates into tighter constraints on the luminosity distance and source-frame component masses. Notably, this remains true even when gravitational-wave events have a lower signal-to-noise ratio in ET-Δ than in ET-2L.

</details>


### [138] [Distinct Near-Horizon Trend of Synchrotron Polarization in Kerr Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19229)
*Yehui Hou,Jiewei Huang,Bin Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明克尔（Kerr）背景下同步辐射（synchrotron emission）线性偏振矢量（linear polarization vector）的近地平展开（near-horizon expansion）具有独特的解析形式，其领先阶偏振模式仅依赖于克尔自旋和源极角，次领先阶修正则编码电磁场的几何与旋转结构，从而为研究旋转黑洞基本性质及引力-电磁相互作用提供潜在探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展已有工作[Hou et al. (2024)]的赤道面分析和[Chael et al. (2026)]的离赤道领先阶结果，建立更完整的近地平偏振解析理论，以探测旋转黑洞基本性质及引力-电磁相互作用。

Method: 在克尔背景下，对静止、轴对称、简并电磁场（degenerate electromagnetic field）中的同步辐射线性偏振矢量进行近地平展开解析分析，分别得到领先阶（leading-order）和次领先阶（next-to-leading-order）修正的解析形式。

Result: 领先阶偏振模式仅依赖于克尔自旋参数和源极角（polar angle）；次领先阶修正进一步包含电磁场的几何与旋转结构信息。

Conclusion: 近地平偏振可为研究旋转黑洞的基本属性及引力-电磁相互作用提供潜在的观测探针。

Abstract: We show that the near-horizon expansion of the linear polarization vector for synchrotron emission in a Kerr background admits a distinct analytic form. For emission from a stationary, axisymmetric, degenerate electromagnetic field, the leading-order polarization pattern depends only on the Kerr spin and the source polar angle, while the next-to-leading-order correction further encodes the geometric and rotational structure of the electromagnetic field. Our result extends the equatorial analysis of [Hou et al. (2024)] and the off-equatorial leading-order result of [Chael et al. (2026)]. Near-horizon polarization thus offers a potential probe of the fundamental properties of rotating black holes and of gravito-electromagnetic interactions.

</details>


### [139] [A Potential Black Hole Mimicker From Non-Minimal Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19291)
*Debanjan Debnath,Rikpratik Sengupta,Kaushik Bhattacharya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类基于曲率-流体耦合（curvature-fluid coupling）引力理论的无视界正则超致密天体：内部由类真空状态方程（vacuum-like equation of state）驱动，外部为精确Schwarzschild解，通过一个具有刚性物质（stiff-matter）状态方程的壳层连接。该模型自然选择出$1.4$-$2.1 M_\odot$、半径5-7 km的质量-半径窗口，并在超致密极限下预言了与Hawking温度不同的几何热力学壳层温度以及质量无关的光度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一类无视界（horizonless）、正则（regular）的超致密天体（ultra-compact objects），以期在不引入事件视界（event horizon）的前提下模仿黑洞（black hole）的观测量行为。

Method: 在允许曲率-流体耦合（curvature-fluid coupling）的引力理论中构建内部类真空状态方程的解，外部保持精确Schwarzschild度规（Schwarzschild metric），两者通过一个壳层（shell）在连接处粘合。

Result: 壳层获得刚性物质（stiff-matter）状态方程；模型自然选择出质量$1.4$-$2.1 M_\odot$、半径5-7 km的典型超致密质量-半径窗口；超致密极限下预言了与Hawking温度不同的几何热力学壳层温度以及质量无关的光度（mass independent luminosity）。

Conclusion: 该模型与Mazur-Mottola引力星（gravastar）及其变体不同，能够自然选择出特定的质量-半径窗口，并且在观测量上具有区别于标准黑洞的独特温度与光度特征。

Abstract: We present a class of horizonless, regular ultra-compact objects arising in a theory of gravity which allows curvature-fluid coupling. The non-minimal interaction between fluid variables and the Ricci scalar generates a vacuum-like equation of state in the interior, while the exterior remains exactly Schwarzschild. The two spacetimes are glued through a shell at the junction. The interior metric is non-singular, the shell acquires a stiff-matter equation of state, and near-horizon compactness can potentially mimic black-hole phenomenology without event horizons. Unlike the Mazur-Mottola gravastar and its variants, the present model naturally selects a typical ultra-compact mass-radius window, with masses in the range $1.4$-$2.1 M_\odot$ and radii in the range 5-7 km. This framework predicts a unique geometric-thermodynamic shell temperature in the ultra-compact limit distinctly different from the Hawking expression and the other unique observational feature of the model is the prediction of mass independent luminosity.

### [140] [Standard Candles for Supernova Neutrino Detection at DUNE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18337)
*Ting Cheng,Matheus Hostert,Pedro A. N. Machado,Nityasa Mishra,Adrian Thompson*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种数据驱动策略，利用$^8$B太阳中微子和μ子静止衰变中微子作为标准烛光（standard candles），校准DUNE远探测器对超新星中微子（$ν_e$）的探测，从而降低核模型依赖带来的高达300%的光谱参数提取偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DUNE远探测器虽能通过$ν_e$带电电流反应（charged-current reaction）探测银河系核心坍缩超新星中微子，但$ν_e$-Ar截面的不确定性严重限制了超新星光谱参数的提取。

Method: 采用数据驱动策略，利用$^8$B太阳中微子和μ子静止衰变中微子（muon-decay-at-rest neutrinos）作为标准烛光，分别约束与超新星探测相关的低能和高能截面分量，从而减少对核模型（nuclear models）的依赖。

Result: 该方法可将依赖核模型所导致的光谱参数提取偏差降低最多300%。

Conclusion: 所提出的校准策略有效减轻了截面不确定性对超新星中微子物理分析的影响，为DUNE实验从超新星爆发中提取$ν_e$光谱信息提供了更可靠的途径。

Abstract: The Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment (DUNE) far detector is sensitive to $\mathcal{O}(10)$ MeV electron neutrinos through $ν_e$ charged-current reaction with argon. This capability is a unique window into the $ν_e$ component of a Galactic core-collapse supernova flux. Extracting the properties of the supernova spectrum is, however, limited by the poorly-known $ν_e$-Ar cross section. We propose a data-driven strategy that leverages $^8$B solar neutrinos and muon-decay-at-rest neutrinos as standard candles for this process. These calibration samples constrain both the low-energy and high-energy components of the cross section relevant for supernova detection. Our method reduces the reliance on nuclear models, which can bias the extraction of the spectral parameters by as much as 300$\%$.

### [141] [The Landscape of Composite Higgs Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18364)
*Daniel Murnane*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文围绕粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的自然性（naturalness）问题，提出了一种基于贝叶斯（Bayesian）框架的新调谐度量，并将其应用于复合希格斯模型（Composite Higgs models）的分析。通过对最小4D复合希格斯模型（M4DCHM）及其扩展（如轻子化M4DCHM和近最小4DCHM）进行全局拟合与排除界限分析，评估这些扩展对自然性的改善程度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型虽预测精度极高，但希格斯粒子（Higgs particle）的参数需经过极其精细的调谐（fine-tuning）才能解释宇宙结构的存在，这一“自然性”危机促使作者探寻无需精细调谐的自然解释。

Method: 全面探索自然性概念，提出一种基于贝叶斯统计（Bayesian statistics）的新调谐度量（tuning measure）；将该度量应用于复合希格斯模型（Composite Higgs models）分析，对最小4D复合希格斯模型（M4DCHM）进行全局拟合（global fit），并考察轻子化M4DCHM（Leptonic M4DCHM）和近最小4DCHM（Next-to-Minimal 4DCHM）等扩展的贡献。

Result: 对M4DCHM施加了强排除界限（exclusion bounds）；分析了不同扩展（如嵌入复合τ轻子的轻子化M4DCHM、含有暗物质候选者的近最小4DCHM）对调谐改善的潜力。

Conclusion: 明确了上述扩展能否以及如何在多大程度上改善复合希格斯部门（Composite Higgs sector）的自然性。

Abstract: While the Standard Model (SM) of particle physics contains the most precise set of predictions ever devised by humanity, that precision comes at a cost. The strange nature of the Higgs particle requires its parameters to be tuned so precisely that if the SM is indeed the true description of reality, one is forced to wonder how such a miracle as galactic structure and life could occur. Instead, we search in this work for a natural explanation. The concept of naturalness is comprehensively explored, and a new tuning measure proposed, with an aim to place it on well-defined Bayesian footing. We then turn this measure on to the analysis of a class of intriguing new physics - Composite Higgs models. These effective models are the result of a plethora of underlying theories, and they allow the production of a naturally light Higgs particle, appearing as the SM Higgs at low energy. We establish the background required to appreciate the N-site 4D Composite Higgs model, and subsequently focus on the simplest incarnations of this class. A global fit is performed on the Minimal 4D Composite Higgs model (M4DCHM), with strong exclusion bounds placed on collider search channels. We analyse any improvement in tuning that could be gained from several extensions to this model. The Leptonic M4DCHM is explored, with a composite tau lepton embedded in various representations. The possibility of a dark matter candidate existing in the Next-to-Minimal 4DCHM is considered. Ultimately, we are able to define what, if any, benefit to naturalness can come to the Composite Higgs sector by introducing these extensions.

</details>


### [142] [Semi-leptonic decays $B \to D^{(*)}(1S,2S)\ell ν_{\ell}$ within the covariant light-front approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18576)
*Zhi-Jie Sun,Zhi-Qing Zhang,Shi-Chen Xue,Feng-Zhou Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在协变光前夸克模型（CLFQM）框架下，系统分析了$B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(1S,2S)\ell\nu_\ell$和$B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(1S,2S)\ell\nu_\ell$等半轻子衰变过程。计算得到的分支比与轻子（$e,\mu$）的实验数据吻合良好，而与$\tau$轻子相关的分支比则系统性地小于实验测量值，由此自然引出了所谓的$\mathcal{R}(D)$和$\mathcal{R}(D^*)$反常。此外，还计算了前后不对称性$\mathcal{A}_{FB}$和纵向极化分数$f_L$，结果与大多数理论计算和实验数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半轻子衰变$B\to D^{(*)}\ell\nu_\ell$是检验标准模型（Standard Model）以及探究轻子味道普适性（lepton flavor universality, LFU）的重要探针。实验上观测到的$\mathcal{R}(D)$和$\mathcal{R}(D^*)$比值与标准模型预言之间存在偏差（即反常），亟需从不同理论模型角度进行系统检验。本文旨在利用协变光前夸克模型（CLFQM）统一描述$B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(1S,2S)$和$B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(1S,2S)$的跃迁形状因子（form factors），并系统计算对应的半轻子衰变可观测物理量，以检验理论模型对反常的解释能力。

Method: 采用协变光前夸克模型（covariant light-front quark model, CLFQM），计算$B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(1S,2S)$和$B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(1S,2S)$的跃迁形状因子（form factors）。在此基础上，推导并计算各半轻子衰变的分支比（branching ratios）、前后不对称性$\mathcal{A}_{FB}$以及纵向极化分数$f_L$。通过比较轻子通道（$e,\mu,\tau$）的结果，分析$\mathcal{R}(D)$和$\mathcal{R}(D^*)$反常问题。

Result: 对于$\ell^\prime=e,\mu$通道，$Br(B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}\ell^\prime\nu_{\ell^\prime})$和$Br(B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}\ell^\prime\nu_{\ell^\prime})$与实验数据高度吻合；而对于$\tau$通道，分支比系统性地小于实验测量值。预测的比值$\mathcal{R}(D)=0.261\pm0.013$和$\mathcal{R}(D^*)=0.228\pm0.026$分别与HFLAV世界平均值存在$3.1\sigma$和$2.1\sigma$偏差，但与LHCb最新测量值的偏离仅为$0.16\sigma$和$1.5\sigma$。对于$B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(2S)\ell\nu_\ell$和$B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(2S)\ell\nu_\ell$，分支比在$10^{-4}\sim10^{-3}$量级，远大于Bethe-Salpeter（BS）方程的结果，但与相对论性夸克模型（RQM）一致。

Conclusion: 协变光前夸克模型（CLFQM）能够较好地描述$B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}^{(*)}$半轻子衰变中与轻子$e,\mu$相关的过程，但对$\tau$通道分支比的系统低估自然导致了$\mathcal{R}(D)$和$\mathcal{R}(D^*)$反常的出现。模型对激发态（2S）衰变的预测支持相对论性夸克模型的计算结果。整体上，本工作的理论预言与大多数已有理论结果和实验数据一致。

Abstract: We present a systematic analysis of the semi-leptonic decays $B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(1S,2S)\ellν_\ell$ and $B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(1S,2S)\ellν_\ell$ with $\ell=e,μ,τ$ within the covariant light-front quark model (CLFQM). Using the form factors of the transitions $B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(1S,2S)$ and $B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(1S,2S)$, we calculate the branching ratios of the relevant semi-leptonic decays and find that $Br(B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}\ell^\primeν_{\ell^\prime})$ and $Br(B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}\ell^\primeν_{\ell^\prime})$ with $\ell^\prime=e,μ$ are agree well with the data, while $Br(B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}τν_τ)$ and $Br(B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}τν_τ)$ are systematically smaller than the experimental measurements. This naturally gives rise to the so-called $\mathcal{R}(D)$ and $\mathcal{R}(D^*)$ anomalies. Our predictions $\mathcal{R}(D)=0.261\pm0.013$ and $\mathcal{R}(D^*)=0.228\pm0.026$ show $3.1σ$ and $2.1σ$ deviations from the current experimental world averages compiled by the Heavy Flavor Averaging Group (HFLAV), respectively, yet only deviate by $0.16σ$ and $1.5σ$ from the latest LHCb measurements. For the decays $B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(2S)\ellν_\ell$ and $B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(2S)\ellν_\ell$, their branching ratios lie in the range $10^{-4}\sim10^{-3}$, which are much larger than the results from the Bethe Salpeter (BS) equation , but agree with the relativistic quark model (RQM) calculations. Furthermore, we also calculate the forward-backward asymmetries $\mathcal{A}_{FB}$ and longitudinal polarization fractions $f_L$ for the corresponding decays. Our predictions are consistent with most other theoretical results and experimental data

</details>


### [143] [Polarization analysis of $χ_{cJ}$ decay into octet baryonic pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18690)
*Cai-Ying Pang,Rong-Gang Ping,Dai-Hui Wei*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了在极化正负电子对撞环境下，χ_{cJ}(J=0,1,2)衰变到重子-反重子对过程中的极化转移机制，利用自旋密度矩阵形式追踪从初态束流到末态重子系统的极化传播，并探讨了纵向束流极化对自旋可观测量的影响及其在量子信息领域的潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用自旋密度矩阵形式（spin density matrix formalism），追踪极化从初态束流经产生链 e⁺e⁻ → ψ(2S) → γχ_{cJ} 直至末态重子-反重子系统的完整传播过程；对χ_{c2}衰变，结合夸克模型（quark model）进行计算。

Result: χ_{c1} → B\bar{B}的螺旋度振幅分析（helicity amplitude analysis）确认了由电荷共轭螺旋度选择定则（charge-conjugation helicity selection rule）决定的普适角分布参数α = -1/3。χ_{c2}衰变的α及横向极化依赖于两个独立振幅，夸克模型计算与现有数据吻合。纵向束流极化P_z可改变χ_{c1}和χ_{c2}的自旋可观测性。

Conclusion: 纵向极化束流为未来极化设施（如STCF）提供了新的实验手段，可用于检验χ_{cJ}衰变机制并探索重子自旋纠缠作为量子信息资源的可能性。

Abstract: This work presents a comprehensive analysis of polarization transfer in the decays \(χ_{cJ}\) (\(J=0,1,2\)) to octet baryon-antibaryon pairs within a polarized electron-positron collision environment. Using the spin density matrix formalism, we trace the polarization from the initial beams through the production chain \(e^+e^- \to ψ(2S) \to γχ_{cJ}\) to the final-state baryon-antibaryon system. The helicity amplitude analysis for \(χ_{c1} \to B\bar{B}\) confirms the universal angular distribution parameter \(α= -1/3\), as dictated by the charge-conjugation helicity selection rule. For \(χ_{c2}\) decays, \(α\) and the transverse polarization depend on two independent amplitudes, and our quark-model calculations agree with existing data. We demonstrate that the longitudinal beam polarization \(P_z\) modifies the spin observables for \(χ_{c1}\) and \(χ_{c2}\), offering new experimental handles at future polarized facilities like the Super \(τ\)-Charm Facility(STCF) to test decay mechanisms and explore baryonic spin entanglement as a quantum information resource.

</details>


### [144] [Three-body unitary determination of the $f_1(1285)$ and $f_1(1420)$ pole positions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19040)
*Tao-Ran Hu,Hai-Long Fu,Feng-Kun Guo,Ulf-G. Meißner,Xu Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文在无穷体积三体幺正性框架下研究了 $I^G(J^{PC})=0^+(1^{++})$ 的 $K\bar K\pi$ 系统，聚焦于 $f_1(1285)$ 和 $f_1(1420)$ 共振区的极点结构。通过构造耦合的 $\pi a_0$-$K\bar K^*$ 振幅并拟合 BESIII 实验数据，发现 $f_1(1285)$ 源于裸态的“穿衣”（dressing），而 $f_1(1420)$ 主要由动力学生成，支持其强子分子态（hadronic-molecule）解释。此外，在最佳拟合振幅中还在相同黎曼面上发现了一个由 $P$ 波 $\pi a_0$ 接触相互作用单独产生的额外极点，该极点对截断和双体输入有较大依赖，但对物理谱线形几乎没有可辨影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实验和理论对 $f_1(1285)$ 和 $f_1(1420)$ 共振的起源存在争议，尤其是 $f_1(1420)$ 是否可解释为强子分子态。摘要旨在通过三体幺正框架精确分析 $K\bar K\pi$ 系统的极点结构，厘清这两个共振的产生机制，并考察可能存在的额外极点。

Method: 采用无穷体积三体幺正框架（infinite-volume three-body unitary framework），在旁观者-同位素表示（spectator-isobar representation）下构造耦合的 $\pi a_0$-$K\bar K^*$ 振幅。单粒子交换相互作用由三体幺正性自动引入，并包含三角奇异性机制（triangle-singularity mechanism）。短程三体相互作用通过拟合 BESIII 实验中 $J/\psi\to\gamma(K^0_SK^0_S\pi^0)$ 衰变中 $0^+(1^{++})$ 分量的 $K^0_SK^0_S\pi^0$ 不变质量分布来确定。随后将拟合后的振幅解析延拓到相关的非物理黎曼面（unphysical Riemann sheets）以提取极点，并追踪极点轨迹以判断共振起源。

Result: 提取到两个稳健的极点：$f_1(1285)$ 的极点为 $(1277\pm2\pm1)-i(12\pm1\pm0)\,{\rm MeV}$，$f_1(1420)$ 的极点为 $(1435\pm2\pm7)-i(40\pm2\pm1)\,{\rm MeV}$。极点轨迹表明 $f_1(1285)$ 来源于势中引入的裸态被“穿衣”，而 $f_1(1420)$ 主要是动力学生成（dynamically generated）。单道分析将其追溯到与附近裸态混合的 $S$ 波 $K\bar K^*$ 准束缚态（quasi-bound state）。此外，在最佳拟合振幅中于 $f_1(1285)$ 所在的同一黎曼面上发现一个额外的更深极点，该极点仅由 $P$ 波 $\pi a_0$ 接触相互作用产生，对截断（cutoff）和双体输入有较大依赖，但在物理线形上几乎没有可辨印记。

Conclusion: $f_1(1285)$ 和 $f_1(1420)$ 具有不同的起源：前者是裸态穿衣的结果，后者是动力学生成的强子分子态。三体幺正框架中的单粒子交换和三角奇异性机制对于正确描述这些共振至关重要。额外发现的深极点虽然存在，但对物理观测影响极小。论文还提供了关于三体割（three-body cuts）如何影响积分方程解的详细教学性附录。

Abstract: We study the $I^G(J^{PC})=0^+(1^{++})$ $K\bar Kπ$ system in an infinite-volume three-body unitary framework, focusing on the pole content of the region of the $f_1(1285)$ and $f_1(1420)$ resonances. The coupled $πa_0$-$K\bar K^*$ amplitude is constructed in the spectator-isobar representation, where the one-particle-exchange interaction required by three-body unitarity automatically incorporates the triangle-singularity mechanism. The short-range three-body interaction is constrained by fitting the $0^+(1^{++})$ component of the BESIII $K^0_SK^0_Sπ^0$ invariant-mass distribution in the $J/ψ\toγ(K^0_SK^0_Sπ^0)$ decay. Analytically continuing the fitted amplitude to the relevant unphysical Riemann sheets, we find two robust poles: \begin{align} \sqrt{s_{f_1(1285)}}&= \left(1277\pm2\pm1\right) -i\left(12\pm1\pm0\right)\text{MeV}\,,\notag\\ \sqrt{s_{f_1(1420)}}&= \left(1435\pm2\pm7\right) -i\left(40\pm2\pm1\right)\text{MeV}\,.\notag \end{align} The pole trajectories indicate that the $f_1(1285)$ originates from dressing a bare state introduced in the potential. In contrast, the $f_1(1420)$ is predominantly dynamically generated, and a single-channel analysis traces it to an $S$-wave $K\bar K^*$ quasi-bound state mixed with the nearby bare state, supporting its hadronic-molecule interpretation. We also find an additional pole deeper in the complex plane in the best-fit amplitude on the same Riemann sheet as the $f_1(1285)$. This additional pole is generated by the $P$-wave $πa_0$ contact interaction alone. It has a sizable cutoff and two-body-input dependence, and leaves little visible imprint on the physical lineshape. Finally, we provide a detailed and pedagogical appendix on how three-body cuts affect the solution of the integral equation.

</details>


### [145] [The $Z'$-boson of the $B-L$ Supersymmetric Standard Model and its Large Hadron Collider Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19293)
*Waleed Abdallah,AseshKrishna Datta,Stefano Moretti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了B-L超对称标准模型（BLSSM）中的Z'玻色子如何通过变“胖”、轻子恐惧症（leptophobia）、或对BLSSM特有态（包括超对称态）具有较大衰变分支比（BR）等方式，显著规避LHC当前约5 TeV的质量下限，在有利参数下将允许的Z'质量压低至2.24 TeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准大质量Z'玻色子受LHC实验约束，质量下限约为5 TeV；本文旨在探索BLSSM框架下Z'玻色子是否能够通过特殊性质显著降低这一约束上限。

Method: 通过对BLSSM参数空间进行彻底扫描（thorough scan），系统性考察Z'玻色子变“胖”、轻子恐惧症、对BLSSM特有态的大衰变分支比等现象及其相互作用，并同时确保满足LEP和SLC在Z-极点（Z-pole）的精密约束以及LHC多用途实验的共振搜索约束。

Conclusion: BLSSM框架中的Z'玻色子可通过上述多种机制的组合效应显著规避当前LHC的质量下限，物理上允许远低于5 TeV的Z'质量存在。

Abstract: We discuss how the $Z'$-boson of the $B-L$ Supersymmetric (SUSY) Standard Model (BLSSM) could evade the current lower bound of around 5 TeV on the mass of such a resonance (of sequential nature) from the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) by a significant margin. This happens when the experimental sensitivities are critically impaired as the $Z'$-boson becomes `fat' or develops some leptophobia or possesses an optimally large decay Branching Ratio (BR) to BLSSM-specific states (including the SUSY ones) or when some or all of these are at play simultaneously. We describe how such a $Z'$-boson could acquire there features while still respecting the non-negotiable precision constraints from the LEP and the SLC experiments running at the $Z$-pole as well as those from the multi-purpose experiments at the LHC that search for such a resonance. We explore the interplay of the aforementioned phenomena and identify the regions of the BLSSM parameter space that give rise to the described situation by carrying out a thorough scan of it. We find that $M_{Z'}$ masses as low as 2.24 TeV may still be allowed in the BLSSM under favorable circumstances.

### [146] [Transient Bias for CP Domain Wall Decay and Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18669)
*Sally Yuxuan Hao,Fangchao Liu,Shota Nakagawa,Yuichiro Nakai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种动力学机制，通过在早期宇宙引入一个具有大场值和非平凡相位的新标量场，借助与CP破缺标量场的高维相互作用产生瞬态CP真空偏置，从而消除暴胀后自发CP破缺（SCPV）导致的CP畴壁宇宙学约束，并使该标量场的相干振荡自然成为暗物质候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暴胀后的自发CP破缺（spontaneous CP violation, SCPV）会导致CP畴壁（CP domain walls）的形成，从而对宇宙最高温度施加了严苛的约束（必须低于CP破缺标度）。现有机制要么引入永久性的显式CP破缺（explicit CPV），要么无法同时满足理论自洽性和宇宙学观测。因此，需要一种不破坏低能CP结构且能有效消除畴壁的动力学方案。

Method: 引入一个在早期宇宙中获得大场值并携带非平凡相位的新标量场。该场通过一个高维相互作用（higher-dimensional interaction）与CP破缺标量场耦合，从而在退化的CP真空之间诱导出瞬态的能量偏置（transient bias）。该偏置在CP畴壁形成后触发其衰变。随着新标量场演化为零（向原点演化），偏置自行消失，低能CP结构保持不变。

Result: 推导了CP畴壁成功衰变所需的条件，并确定了可行的参数空间（viable parameter space）。指出该新标量场的相干振荡（coherent oscillation）自然存活下来，可作为暗物质（dark matter）的候选者。

Conclusion: 所提出的动力学机制在不引入永久性显式CP破缺的前提下，有效消除了SCPV的宇宙学畴壁约束，并将CP畴壁问题的解决与暗物质起源联系起来，提供了一个自洽的框架。

Abstract: Spontaneous CP violation (SCPV) provides an attractive solution to the strong CP problem. However, SCPV after inflation suffers from the formation of CP domain walls, requiring the maximal temperature of the Universe to lie below the CP-breaking scale. In the present work, we then propose a dynamical mechanism that removes this cosmological constraint without introducing permanent explicit CPV. We consider a new scalar field that acquires a large field value with a nontrivial phase in the early Universe and induces a transient bias among degenerate CP vacua through a higher-dimensional interaction with a CP-breaking scalar field. This bias triggers the decay of CP domain walls after they form. As the new scalar field evolves toward the origin, the bias disappears, leaving the low-energy CP structure intact. We derive the conditions for successful domain wall decay and identify the viable parameter space. Furthermore, we point out that the coherent oscillation of the new scalar field naturally survives as dark matter, linking the resolution of the CP domain wall problem to the origin of dark matter.

### [147] [Diffractive Production of Heavy Quarkonia at the Electron Ion Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18854)
*Mohammad Yousuf Jamal,Ajaharul Islam,Aritra Bandyopadhyay,Santosh K. Das*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究针对电子-离子对撞机（EIC）能区的S波重夸克偶素衍射光产生与电产生过程，在保留双胶子硬核完整横向动量依赖性的全ℓ_t解析框架下进行计算，不采用小尺度色偶极极限中撞击参数贝塞尔核的展开近似。通过结合基于Cornell势的轻锥波函数与现代共线胶子分布，在基准化到HERA粲偶素截面比数据后，提供了EIC运动学下底偶素截面比的一致预测，并发现全ℓ_t处理显著改善了径向激发态的描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中，衍射重夸克偶素产生的计算通常采用小尺度色偶极（color-dipole）极限下的撞击参数贝塞尔核展开近似，这可能会丢失重要的横向动量（transverse-momentum ℓ_t）信息。为精确预测电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider，EIC）能区的重夸克偶素产生截面，需要保留完整的ℓ_t依赖性。

Method: 生产振幅计算中保留了硬双胶子核（hard two-gluon kernel）的完整横向动量ℓ_t依赖性，未采用小尺度色偶极极限的展开近似。夸克偶素轻锥波函数（light-cone wave functions）由Cornell势的薛定谔方程解构建，并归一化到实测轻子宽度（leptonic widths），结合现代共线胶子分布（collinear gluon distribution）进行计算。

Result: 全ℓ_t解析处理方法相对于主导偶极极限（leading dipole limit），系统地改善了径向激发态（radially excited states）的描述。研究确定了二者差异最大的运动学区窗口，并在HERA粲偶素截面比数据基准化后，给出了EIC运动学下底偶素（bottomonium）截面比的一致预测。

Conclusion: 全ℓ_t解析框架对于重夸克偶素衍射产生过程是必要且更精确的处理方式，尤其对径向激发态的描述改进显著。该研究为EIC实验提供了可靠的底偶素截面比理论预测，有助于未来实验的规划与数据分析。

Abstract: We study diffractive photo- and electroproduction of the $S$-wave heavy quarkonia $J/ψ$, $ψ(2S)$, and $Υ(nS)$ at energies relevant for the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC). The production amplitude is evaluated while retaining the full transverse-momentum ($\ell_t$) dependence of the hard two-gluon kernel, that is, without expanding the impact-parameter Bessel kernel as is done in the small-size color-dipole limit. The quarkonia light-cone wave functions are built from Cornell-potential solutions of the Schrödinger equation, normalized to the measured leptonic widths, and combined with a modern collinear gluon distribution. After benchmarking the framework against the full set of HERA charmonium cross-section ratio data, we provide a consistent set of bottomonium cross-section ratio predictions in EIC kinematics. We find that the full $\ell_t$-resolved treatment systematically improves the description of the radially excited states relative to the leading dipole limit, and we identify the kinematic windows where this difference is largest.

### [148] [Thermodynamic-Kinetic Decoupling Enables Stable Excitonic Emission in Defect-Tolerant Cu-Based Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18939)
*Haoran Chen,Zhipeng Xu,Chunjian Li,Lei Hou,Dechao Yu,Xiaobin Xie,Yue Liu,Bohua Dong,Lixin Cao,Chenghui Xia*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种热力学-动力学解耦策略，通过对CuInS2量子点进行Zn2+合金化和Ga3+掺入，分别从热力学上抑制铜空位缺陷、动力学上固定阳离子亚晶格阻止缺陷再生，最终实现了无镉、高量子产率（约98%）、窄线宽（约120 meV）且具备室温单光子发射纯度（g2(0)=0.06）的量子点，并在发光太阳能聚光器中展现了低重吸收损耗的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体量子点（colloidal quantum dots）需同时具备室温单光子纯度（room-temperature single-photon purity）和高光致发光量子产率（photoluminescence quantum yield）以满足量子光学应用需求，但在环境友好型材料中实现这一目标仍面临挑战。

Method: 采用热力学-动力学解耦策略（thermodynamic-kinetic decoupling strategy）：首先通过Zn2+合金化引起晶格应变，热力学上抑制本征铜空位（copper vacancies），将发射从约300 meV的宽缺陷带收窄至约120 meV的激子线（excitonic line）；随后引入Ga3+在动力学上固定阳离子亚晶格（cation sublattice），阻止Cu+迁移，从而在ZnS壳层生长过程中防止缺陷再生。

Result: 所得无镉（Cd-free）核/壳量子点实现了约98%的近单位量子产率（near-unity quantum yield），同时保持窄激子发射。室温单点光谱（single-dot spectroscopy）显示均匀线宽（homogeneous linewidth）低至约58 meV，闪烁（blinking）显著抑制，单光子发射纯度g2(0)=0.06。此外，稳定的激子发射直接降低了发光太阳能聚光器（luminescent solar concentrator）中的重吸收损耗，实现了12.68%的外部光学效率。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种可推广的框架，用于在离子迁移活跃、易产生缺陷的半导体中释放本征激子光物理特性，为开发用于量子光源的高性能无重金属发射器（heavy-metal-free emitters）开辟了可行路径。

Abstract: Colloidal quantum dots that simultaneously offer room-temperature single-photon purity and high photoluminescence quantum yield are sought for quantum optics, but remain elusive in environmentally benign materials. We introduce a thermodynamic-kinetic decoupling strategy that transforms defect-tolerant CuInS2 quantum dots into bright, narrowband, and photostable single-photon emitters. Zn2+ alloying strains the lattice, thermodynamically suppressing native copper vacancies and narrowing the emission from a broad defect band of approximately 300 meV to an excitonic line of approximately 120 meV. Ga3+ incorporation then kinetically pins the cation sublattice against Cu+ migration, preventing defect regeneration during ZnS shell growth. The resulting Cd-free core/shell dots achieve near-unity quantum yield of approximately 98% while retaining narrow excitonic emission. Critically, room-temperature single-dot spectroscopy reveals homogeneous linewidths as low as approximately 58 meV, strongly suppressed blinking, and high-purity single-photon emission with g2(0) = 0.06. This stabilized excitonic emission directly reduces reabsorption losses in luminescent solar concentrators, yielding an external optical efficiency of 12.68%. Our work establishes a generalizable framework to unlock intrinsic excitonic photophysics in ion-mobile, defect-prone semiconductors, opening a viable path toward high-performance heavy-metal-free emitters for quantum light sources.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将等变图神经网络（equivariant graph neural network, EGN）GotanNet适配至光学光谱预测任务，利用其等变几何特征提取能力，在包含10,533个结构以及随机相位近似（random phase approximation, RPA）级别光谱的数据集上进行评估。

Result: 所提出的模型在多个数据集上均超越了当前最优方法（state of the art），最大性能提升出现在0-8 eV能量范围以及静态实介电常数（static real permittivity）的预测上，这两个指标对薄膜光学（thin-film optics）尤为重要。

Conclusion: 等变图神经网络能够有效提升光学光谱预测的精度，特别是在对薄膜光电器件具有重要意义的能量和介电常数范围内，为高通量材料筛选提供了更具几何表达能力的替代方案。

Abstract: Scalable prediction of optical spectra is a critical component of high-throughput materials screening for optoelectronic applications such as solar cells. Existing surrogate models are trained on spectra computed from lower levels of theory or rely on rotation-invariant scalar features, limiting their geometric expressiveness. We explore the use of equivariant graph neural networks for optical spectra prediction, adapting GotenNet to this task and evaluating it on multiple datasets including a recently published collection of 10,533 structures with spectra computed at the level of the random phase approximation (RPA). The proposed model outperforms the current state of the art, with the largest gains in the 0-8 eV range and on predicting the static real permittivity, both of particular relevance for thin-film optics.

### [150] [Measurement of isolated photon plus two-jet correlations in Pb+Pb and $pp$ collisions at 5.02 TeV with ATLAS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17760)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ATLAS探测器记录的pp和Pb+Pb碰撞数据（质心能量5.02 TeV），测量了光子加双喷注（photon plus two-jet）事件，通过三个观测量（x_JJγ, A_JJγ, ΔR_JJ）表征多部分子系统在夸克胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）中的能量损失、相对能量损失及张角修正，并与JEWEL、JETSCAPE、LBT三种喷注淬火（jet quenching）模型进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解部分子穿过夸克胶子等离子体时发生的喷注淬火效应，特别是多部分子系统的整体能量损失与色荷载流子（colour-charge carrier）之间的相对能量损失机制。

Method: 利用2017年质子-质子（pp）碰撞数据（积分亮度260 pb⁻¹）和2018年铅-铅（Pb+Pb）碰撞数据（积分亮度1.72 nb⁻¹），选取光子横动量（transverse momentum）90–180 GeV、至少两个反-k_t算法（anti-k_t algorithm, R=0.2）喷注且喷注横动量>30 GeV的事件，测量x_JJγ、A_JJγ和ΔR_JJ三个观测量。采用新型多喷注混合技术（multijet mixing technique）扣除无关联组合本底（combinatoric background），并利用迭代去卷（iterative unfolding）修正光子纯度和探测器分辨率效应。

Result: 在Pb+Pb碰撞的30-80%、10-30%和0-10%中心度区间内，每个光子的双喷注产额（two-jet yield）在所有三个观测量中均表现出显著抑制，即I_AA < 1，表明部分子-介质相互作用（parton-medium interactions）导致的能量损失效应显著。

Conclusion: 实验测量结果与JEWEL、JETSCAPE、LBT三种喷注淬火模型的比较，有助于验证和约束理论模型中关于部分子在核介质中能量损失与色荷效应的描述。

Abstract: This paper presents a measurement of photon plus two-jet events in $pp$ and Pb+Pb collisions, i.e. events in which the transverse momentum of a single photon is balanced by two distinct jets. The measurement was performed using $pp$ data taken in 2017 with an integrated luminosity 260 pb$^{-1}$, and Pb+Pb data taken in 2018 with an integrated luminosity 1.72 nb$^{-1}$, both at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ =5.02 TeV, as recorded by the ATLAS detector. Events with photons in the transverse momentum range 90-180 GeV and at least two anti-$k_t$ $R = 0.2$ jets with a $p_\mathrm{T}$ > 30 GeV are selected, and three observables are measured: ${\mathrm{x}}_{\mathrm{JJ}γ}$, $\mathrm{A}_{\mathrm{JJ}γ}$, and $ΔR_{\mathrm{JJ}}$. These observables characterise the overall energy loss of the multiparton system from medium interactions (${\mathrm{x}}_{\mathrm{JJ}γ}$), the relative energy loss between the two colour-charge carriers ($\mathrm{A}_{\mathrm{JJ}γ}$), and medium-induced modifications to their opening angle ($ΔR_{\mathrm{JJ}}$). The observables are corrected for uncorrelated combinatoric background contributions using a novel multijet mixing technique, for photon purity, and for detector resolution effects via iterative unfolding. Final results are presented per photon, and the ratio ($I_\mathrm{AA}$) is taken between measurements in Pb+Pb and $pp$ collisions, for Pb+Pb centrality intervals of 30-80%, 10-30%, and 0-10%. Significant suppression of per photon two-jet yields in all three observables, $I_\mathrm{AA} < 1$, is observed as a result of parton-medium interactions. The experimental measurements are compared to three different jet quenching models: JEWEL, JETSCAPE, and LBT.

</details>
